mandaḥ sahāmātyaḥ sabāndhavaḥc niṣṭhām āpatsyate mūḍhaḥ kruddhe gāṇḍīvadhanvani vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tataḥ satkṛtya vārṣṇeyaṃ virāṭaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥc gṛhān prasthāpayām āsa sagaṇaṃ sahabāndhavama dvārakāṃ tu gate kṛṣṇe yudhiṣṭhirapurogamāḥc cakruḥ sāṃgrāmikaṃ sarvaṃ virāṭaś ca mahīpatiḥa tataḥ saṃpreṣayām āsa virāṭaḥ saha bāndhavaiḥc sarveṣāṃ bhūmipālānāṃ drupadaś ca mahīpatiḥa vacanāt kurusiṃhānāṃ matsyapāñcālayoś ca tec samājagmur mahīpālāḥ saṃprahṛṣṭā mahābalāḥa tac chrutvā pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ samāgacchan mahad balamc dhṛtarāṣṭrasutaś cāpi samāninye mahīpatīna samākulā mahī rājan kurupāṇḍavakāraṇātc tadā samabhavat kṛtsnā saṃprayāṇe mahīkṣitāmd saṃkulā ca tadā bhūmiś caturaṅgabalānvitāa balāni teṣāṃ vīrāṇām āgacchanti tatas tataḥc cālayantīva gāṃ devīṃ saparvatavanām imāma tataḥ prajñāvayovṛddhaṃ pāñcālyaḥ svapurohitamc kurubhyaḥ preṣayām āsa yudhiṣṭhiramate tadā drupada uvācaa bhūtānāṃ prāṇinaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ prāṇināṃ buddhijīvinaḥc buddhimatsu narāḥ śreṣṭhā narāṇāṃ tu dvijātayaḥa dvijeṣu vaidyāḥ śreyāṃso vaidyeṣu kṛtabuddhayaḥb kṛtabuddhiṣu kartāraḥ kartṛṣu brahmavādinaḥc sa bhavān kṛtabuddhīnāṃ pradhāna iti me matiḥa kulena ca viśiṣṭo si vayasā ca śrutena cac prajñayānavamaś cāsi śukreṇāṅgirasena caa viditaṃ cāpi te sarvaṃ yathāvṛttaḥ sa kauravaḥc pāṇḍavaś ca yathāvṛttaḥ kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥa dhṛtarāṣṭrasya vidite vañcitāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ paraiḥc vidureṇānunīto pi putram evānuvartatea śakunir buddhipūrvaṃ hi kuntīputraṃ samāhvayatc anakṣajñaṃ matākṣaḥ san kṣatravṛtte sthitaṃ śucima te tathā vañcayitvā tu dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiramc na kasyāṃ cid avasthāyāṃ rājyaṃ dāsyanti vai svayama bhavāṃs tu dharmasaṃyuktaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ bruvan vacaḥc manāṃsi tasya yodhānāṃ dhruvam āvartayiṣyatia viduraś cāpi tad vākyaṃ sādhayiṣyati tāvakamc bhīṣmadroṇakṛpāṇāṃ ca bhedaṃ saṃjanayiṣyatia amātyeṣu ca bhinneṣu yodheṣu vimukheṣu cac punar ekāgrakaraṇaṃ teṣāṃ karma bhaviṣyatia etasminn antare pārthāḥ sukham ekāgrabuddhayaḥc senākarma kariṣyanti dravyāṇāṃ caiva saṃcayama bhidyamāneṣu ca sveṣu lambamāne ca vai tvayic na tathā te kariṣyanti senākarma na saṃśayaḥa etat prayojanaṃ cātra prādhānyenopalabhyatec saṃgatyā dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca kuryād dharmyaṃ vacas tavaa sa bhavān dharmayuktaś ca dharmyaṃ teṣu samācaranc kṛpāluṣu parikleśān pāṇḍavānāṃ prakīrtayana vṛddheṣu kuladharmaṃ ca bruvan pūrvair anuṣṭhitamc vibhetsyati manāṃsy eṣām iti me nātra saṃśayaḥa na ca tebhyo bhayaṃ te sti brāhmaṇo hy asi vedavitc dūtakarmaṇi yuktaś ca sthaviraś ca viśeṣataḥa sa bhavān puṣyayogena muhūrtena jayena cac kauraveyān prayātv āśu kaunteyasyārthasiddhaye vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tathānuśiṣṭaḥ prayayau drupadena mahātmanāc purodhā vṛttasaṃpanno nagaraṃ nāgasāhvayamd śiṣyaiḥ parivṛto vidvān nītiśāstrārthakovidaḥd pāṇḍavānāṃ hitārthāya kauravān prati jagmivān vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca purohitaṃ te prasthāpya nagaraṃ nāgasāhvayam dūtān prasthāpayām āsuḥ pārthivebhyas tatas tataḥ prasthāpya dūtān anyatra dvārakāṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ svayaṃ jagāma kauravyaḥ kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥa gate dvāravatīṃ kṛṣṇe baladeve ca mādhavec saha vṛṣṇyandhakaiḥ sarvair bhojaiś ca śataśas tathāa sarvam āgamayām āsa pāṇḍavānāṃ viceṣṭitamc dhṛtarāṣṭrātmajo rājā dūtaiḥ praṇihitaiś caraiḥa sa śrutvā mādhavaṃ yātaṃ sadaśvair anilopamaiḥc balena nātimahatā dvārakām abhyayāt purīma tam eva divasaṃ cāpi kaunteyaḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥc ānartanagarīṃ ramyāṃ jagāmāśu dhanaṃjayaḥa tau yātvā puruṣavyāghrau dvārakāṃ kurunandanauc suptaṃ dadṛśatuḥ kṛṣṇaṃ śayānaṃ copajagmatuḥa tataḥ śayāne govinde praviveśa suyodhanaḥc ucchīrṣataś ca kṛṣṇasya niṣasāda varāsaned siṃhāsanagataṃ paścāt parivṛtya ca dṛṣṭavāna tataḥ kirīṭī tasyānu praviveśa mahāmanāḥc paścārdhe ca sa kṛṣṇasya prahvo tiṣṭhat kṛtāñjaliḥa pratibuddhaḥ sa vārṣṇeyo dadarśāgre kirīṭinamb ucchīrṣataś cāsanasthaṃ dadarśātha suyodhanamb paścād duryodhanaṃ bhūpam ucchīrṣe saṃsthitaṃ tadāb vaicitravīryajaṃ paścād yādavānāṃ dhuraṃdharaḥb paścād duryodhanaṃ śaurir apaśyad amitadyutiḥc sa tayoḥ svāgataṃ kṛtvā yathārhaṃ pratipūjya cae tadāgamanajaṃ hetuṃ papraccha madhusūdanaḥa tato duryodhanaḥ kṛṣṇam uvāca prahasann ivac vigrahe smin bhavān sāhyaṃ mama dātum ihārhatia samaṃ hi bhavataḥ sakhyaṃ mayi caivārjune pi cac tathā saṃbandhakaṃ tulyam asmākaṃ tvayi mādhavaa ahaṃ cābhigataḥ pūrvaṃ tvām adya madhusūdanac pūrvaṃ cābhigataṃ santo bhajante pūrvasāriṇaḥa tvaṃ ca śreṣṭhatamo loke satām adya janārdanac satataṃ saṃmataś caiva sadvṛttam anupālayad śrībhagavān uvācad svāgataṃ tava gāndhāre na mayā vidito bhavānd duryodhanaḥd kiṃ cāgamanakṛtyaṃ te kasmin kāle tvam āgataḥd tvaddarśanārthī govinda ahaṃ pūrvam ihāgataḥd prītyarthī sa bhavān sāhyaṃ mama dātum ihārhatid dhārtarāṣṭrasya tad vākyaṃ śrutvāmaravarottamaḥd puruṣottamas tv idaṃ vākyaṃ duryodhanam abhāṣata kṛṣṇa uvācaa bhavān abhigataḥ pūrvam atra me nāsti saṃśayaḥc dṛṣṭas tu prathamaṃ rājan mayā pārtho dhanaṃjayaḥa tava pūrvābhigamanāt pūrvaṃ cāpy asya darśanātc sāhāyyam ubhayor eva kariṣyāmi suyodhanaa pravāraṇaṃ tu bālānāṃ pūrvaṃ kāryam iti śrutiḥc tasmāt pravāraṇaṃ pūrvam arhaḥ pārtho dhanaṃjayaḥa matsaṃhananatulyānāṃ gopānām arbudaṃ mahatc nārāyaṇā iti khyātāḥ sarve saṃgrāmayodhinaḥa te vā yudhi durādharṣā bhavantv ekasya sainikāḥc ayudhyamānaḥ saṃgrāme nyastaśastro ham ekataḥd etad viditvā kaunteya vicārya ca punaḥ punaḥd tān vā varaya sāhāyye māṃ sācivyena vā punaḥa ābhyām anyataraṃ pārtha yat te hṛdyataraṃ matamc tad vṛṇītāṃ bhavān agre pravāryas tvaṃ hi dharmataḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa evam uktas tu kṛṣṇena kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥc ayudhyamānaṃ saṃgrāme varayām āsa keśavamd nārāyaṇam amitraghnaṃ kāmāj jātam ajaṃ nṛṣud sarvakṣatrasya purato devadānavayor apid duryodhanas tu tat sainyaṃ sarvam āvarayat tadāa sahasrāṇāṃ sahasraṃ tu yodhānāṃ prāpya bhāratac kṛṣṇaṃ cāpahṛtaṃ jñātvā saṃprāpa paramāṃ mudama duryodhanas tu tat sainyaṃ sarvam ādāya pārthivaḥc tato bhyayād bhīmabalo rauhiṇeyaṃ mahābalama sarvaṃ cāgamane hetuṃ sa tasmai saṃnyavedayatc pratyuvāca tataḥ śaurir dhārtarāṣṭram idaṃ vacaḥa viditaṃ te naravyāghra sarvaṃ bhavitum arhatic yan mayoktaṃ virāṭasya purā vaivāhike tadāa nigṛhyokto hṛṣīkeśas tvadarthaṃ kurunandanac mayā saṃbandhakaṃ tulyam iti rājan punaḥ punaḥa na ca tad vākyam uktaṃ vai keśavaḥ pratyapadyatac na cāham utsahe kṛṣṇaṃ vinā sthātum api kṣaṇama nāhaṃ sahāyaḥ pārthānāṃ nāpi duryodhanasya vaic iti me niścitā buddir vāsudevam avekṣya haa jāto si bhārate vaṃśe sarvapārthivapūjitec gaccha yudhyasva dharmeṇa kṣātreṇa bharatarṣabhaa ity evam uktaḥ sa tadā pariṣvajya halāyudhamc kṛṣṇaṃ cāpahṛtaṃ jñātvā yuddhān mene jitaṃ jayama so bhyayāt kṛtavarmāṇaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasuto nṛpaḥc kṛtavarmā dadau tasya senām akṣauhiṇīṃ tadāa sa tena sarvasainyena bhīmena kurunandanaḥc vṛtaḥ pratiyayau hṛṣṭaḥ suhṛdaḥ saṃpraharṣayand tataḥ pītāmbaradharo jagatsraṣṭā janārdanaḥa gate duryodhane kṛṣṇaḥ kirīṭinam athābravītc ayudhyamānaḥ kāṃ buddhim āsthāyāhaṃ tvayā vṛtaḥ arjuna uvācaa bhavān samarthas tān sarvān nihantuṃ nātra saṃśayaḥc nihantum aham apy ekaḥ samarthaḥ puruṣottamaa bhavāṃs tu kīrtimāṃl loke tad yaśas tvāṃ gamiṣyatic yaśasā cāham apy arthī tasmād asi mayā vṛtaḥa sārathyaṃ tu tvayā kāryam iti me mānasaṃ sadāc cirarātrepsitaṃ kāmaṃ tad bhavān kartum arhati vāsudeva uvācaa upapannam idaṃ pārtha yat spardhethā mayā sahac sārathyaṃ te kariṣyāmi kāmaḥ saṃpadyatāṃ tava vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa evaṃ pramuditaḥ pārthaḥ kṛṣṇena sahitas tadāc vṛto dāśārhapravaraiḥ punar āyād yudhiṣṭhiram vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa śalyaḥ śrutvā tu dūtānāṃ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥc abhyayāt pāṇḍavān rājan saha putrair mahārathaiḥa tasya senāniveśo bhūd adhyardham iva yojanamc tathā hi bahulāṃ senāṃ sa bibharti nararṣabhaḥd akṣauhiṇīpatī rājan mahāvīryaparākramaḥa vicitrakavacāḥ śūrā vicitradhvajakārmukāḥc vicitrābharaṇāḥ sarve vicitrarathavāhanāḥd vicitrasragdharāḥ sarve vicitrāmbarabhūṣaṇāḥa svadeśaveṣābharaṇā vīrāḥ śatasahasraśaḥc tasya senāpraṇetāro babhūvuḥ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥa vyathayann iva bhūtāni kampayann iva medinīmc śanair viśrāmayan senāṃ sa yayau yena pāṇḍavaḥa tato duryodhanaḥ śrutvā mahāsenaṃ mahārathamc upāyāntam abhidrutya svayam ānarca bhāratad śalyasya mantribhiḥ sarvair duryodhanavaśānugaiḥd avijñātaṃ ca śalyasya hṛdayasya priyaṃ kṛtama kārayām āsa pūjārthaṃ tasya duryodhanaḥ sabhāḥc ramaṇīyeṣu deśeṣu ratnacitrāḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥd śilpibhir vividhaiś caiva krīḍās tatra prayojitāḥd tatra mālyāni māṃsāni bhakṣyaṃ peyaṃ ca satkṛtamd kūpāś ca vividhākārā manoharṣavivardhanāḥd vāpyaś ca vividhākārā audakāni gṛhāṇi caa sa tāḥ sabhāḥ samāsādya pūjyamāno yathāmaraḥc duryodhanasya sacivair deśe deśe yathārhataḥe ājagāma sabhām anyāṃ devāvasathavarcasamf tatra vāsāṃsi mālyāni bhakṣyaṃ peyaṃ ca puṣkalamf gandhā ghrāṇasya sukhadā divyāś cittamanoharāḥf sarāṃsi sādaro rājā savihaṃgamṛgāni caa sa tatra viṣayair yuktaḥ kalyāṇair atimānuṣaiḥc mene bhyadhikam ātmānam avamene puraṃdarama papraccha sa tataḥ preṣyān prahṛṣṭaḥ kṣatriyarṣabhaḥc yudhiṣṭhirasya puruṣāḥ ke nu cakruḥ sabhā imāḥe ānīyantāṃ sabhākārāḥ pradeyārhā hi me matāḥf prasādam eṣāṃ dāsyāmi kuntīputro numanyatāmf duryodhanāya tat sarvaṃ kathayanti sma vismitāḥf saṃprahṛṣṭo yadā śalyo diditsur api jīvitamf tataḥ prahṛṣṭaṃ rājānaṃ jñātvā te sacivās tadāa gūḍho duryodhanas tatra darśayām āsa mātulamc taṃ dṛṣṭvā madrarājas tu jñātvā yatnaṃ ca tasya tamd dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaṃ rājā vismitaḥ sa narottamaḥd mantriṇaś cāpi śaṃsanti madrarājaṃ suvismitamd duryodhanena te rājañ śuśrūṣitam idaṃ prabhod priyaṃ priyārhasya sataḥ kartum arhasi bhūmipad tam aṅkam upaveśyāśu mūrdhni cāghrāya madrarāṭe pariṣvajyābravīt prīta iṣṭo rtho gṛhyatām iti duryodhana uvācaa satyavāg bhava kalyāṇa varo vai mama dīyatāmc sarvasenāpraṇetā me bhavān bhavitum arhatid yathaiva pāṇḍavās tubhyaṃ tathaiva bhavato hy ahamd śalyaḥd anumānyaṃ ca pālyaṃ ca bhaktaṃ ca bhaja māṃ vibhod evam etan mahārāja yathā vadasi bhāratad varaṃ dadāmi te prīta evam etad bhaviṣyati vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa kṛtam ity abravīc chalyaḥ kim anyat kriyatām itic kṛtam ity eva gāndhāriḥ pratyuvāca punaḥ punaḥd śalya uvācad gaccha duryodhana puraṃ svakam eva nararṣabhad ahaṃ gamiṣye draṣṭuṃ vai yudhiṣṭhiram ariṃdamamd dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiraṃ rājan kṣipram eṣye narādhipad duryodhana uvācad avaśyaṃ cāpi draṣṭavyaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥd kṣipram āgamyatāṃ rājan pāṇḍavaṃ vīkṣya pārthivad śalya uvācad tvayy adhīnāḥ sma rājendra varadānaṃ smarasva naḥd kṣipram eṣyāmi bhadraṃ te gacchasva svapuraṃ nṛpad pariṣvajya tathānyonyaṃ śalyaduryodhanāv ubhaud dṛṣṭvā tu pāṇḍavān rājan na mithyā kartum utsahea sa tathā śalyam āmantrya punar āyāt svakaṃ puramc śalyo jagāma kaunteyān ākhyātuṃ karma tasya tata upaplavyaṃ sa gatvā tu skandhāvāraṃ praviśya cac pāṇḍavān atha tān sarvāñ śalyas tatra dadarśa had cirāt tu dṛṣṭvā rājānaṃ mātulaṃ samitiṃjayamd āsanebhyaḥ samutpetuḥ sarve sahayudhiṣṭhirāḥa sametya tu mahābāhuḥ śalyaḥ pāṇḍusutais tadāc pādyam arghyaṃ ca gāṃ caiva pratyagṛhṇād yathāvidhid kṛtāñjalir adīnātmā dharmātmā śalyam abravītd svāgataṃ te stu vai rājann etad āsanam āsyatāmd tato nyaṣīdac chalyaś ca kāñcane paramāsaned tatra pādyam athārghyaṃ ca nyavedayata pāṇḍavaḥd nivedya cārghyaṃ vidhivan madrarājāya bhāratad kuśalaṃ pāṇḍavo pṛcchac chalyaṃ sarvasukhāvahamd sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ sarvaiḥ pāṇḍavair dharmacāribhiḥa tataḥ kuśalapūrvaṃ sa madrarājo risūdanaḥc prītyā paramayā yuktaḥ samāśliṣya yudhiṣṭhirama tathā bhīmārjunau hṛṣṭau svasrīyau ca yamāv ubhaub draupadī ca subhadrā ca abhimanyuś ca bhāratac āsane copaviṣṭas tu śalyaḥ pārtham uvāca haa kuśalaṃ rājaśārdūla kaccit te kurunandanac araṇyavāsād diṣṭyāsi vimukto jayatāṃ varaa suduṣkaraṃ kṛtaṃ rājan nirjane vasatā vanec bhrātṛbhiḥ saha rājendra kṛṣṇayā cānayā sahaa ajñātavāsaṃ ghoraṃ ca vasatā duṣkaraṃ kṛtamc duḥkham eva kutaḥ saukhyaṃ rājyabhraṣṭasya bhārataa duḥkhasyaitasya mahato dhārtarāṣṭrakṛtasya vaic avāpsyasi sukhaṃ rājan hatvā śatrūn paraṃtapaa viditaṃ te mahārāja lokatattvaṃ narādhipac tasmāl lobhakṛtaṃ kiṃ cit tava tāta na vidyated rājarṣīṇāṃ purāṇānāṃ mārgam anviccha bhāratad dāne tapasi satye ca bhava tāta yudhiṣṭhirad kṣamā damaś ca satyaṃ ca ahiṃsā ca yudhiṣṭhirad adbhutaś ca punar lokas tvayi rājan pratiṣṭhitaḥd mṛdur vadānyo brahmaṇyo dātā dharmaparāyaṇaḥd dharmās te viditā rājan bahavo lokasākṣikāḥd sarvaṃ jagad idaṃ tāta viditaṃ te paraṃtapad diṣṭyā kṛcchram idaṃ rājan pāritaṃ bharatarṣabhad diṣṭyā paśyāmi rājendra dharmātmānaṃ sahānugamd nistīrṇaṃ duṣkaraṃ rājaṃs tvāṃ dharmanicayaṃ prabhod utthānaṃ saṃyamo dākṣyam apramādo dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥa tato syākathayad rājā duryodhanasamāgamamc tac ca śuśrūṣitaṃ sarvaṃ varadānaṃ ca bhārata yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa sukṛtaṃ te kṛtaṃ rājan prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanāc duryodhanasya yad vīra tvayā vācā pratiśrutamd duryodhanasya cāsmākaṃ viśeṣo tra na vidyatee ekaṃ tv icchāmi bhadraṃ te kriyamāṇaṃ mahīpatef rājann akartavyam api kartum arhasi sattamaf mama tv avekṣayā vīra śṛṇu vijñāpayāmi tef spardhate hi sadā karṇaḥ pārthena raṇamūrdhania bhavān iha mahārāja vāsudevasamo yudhic karṇārjunābhyāṃ saṃprāpte dvairathe rājasattamad vāsudevena sārathyaṃ kāryaṃ pārthasya mātulae karṇasya bhavatā kāryaṃ sārathyaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥa tatra pālyo rjuno rājan yadi matpriyam icchasic tejovadhaś ca te kāryaḥ sauter asmajjayāvahaḥe akartavyam api hy etat kartum arhasi mātula śalya uvācaa śṛṇu pāṇḍava bhadraṃ te yad bravīṣi durātmanaḥc tejovadhanimittaṃ māṃ sūtaputrasya saṃyuged tejovadhanimittaṃ māṃ tat kariṣyāmi te priyama ahaṃ tasya bhaviṣyāmi saṃgrāme sārathir dhruvamc vāsudevena hi samaṃ nityaṃ māṃ sa hi manyatea tasyāhaṃ kuruśārdūla pratīpam ahitaṃ vacaḥc dhruvaṃ saṃkathayiṣyāmi yoddhukāmasya saṃyuged ahaṃ tasya bhaviṣyāmi sārathī raṇamūrdhania yathā sa hṛtadarpaś ca hṛtatejāś ca pāṇḍavac bhaviṣyati sukhaṃ hantuṃ satyam etad bravīmi tea evam etat kariṣyāmi yathā tāta tvam āttha māmc yac cānyad api śakṣyāmi tat kariṣyāmi te priyama yac ca duḥkhaṃ tvayā prāptaṃ dyūte vai kṛṣṇayā sahac paruṣāṇi ca vākyāni sūtaputrakṛtāni vaia jaṭāsurāt parikleśaḥ kīcakāc ca mahādyutec draupadyādhigataṃ sarvaṃ damayantyā yathāśubhama sarvaṃ duḥkham idaṃ vīra sukhodarkaṃ bhaviṣyatic nātra manyus tvayā kāryo vidhir hi balavattaraḥa duḥkhāni hi mahātmānaḥ prāpnuvanti yudhiṣṭhirac devair api hi duḥkhāni prāptāni jagatīpated devadānavagandharvāḥ kiṃnaroragarākṣasāḥd duḥkhaṃ prāptā yathā rājaṃs tac chṛṇuṣva narādhipaa indreṇa śrūyate rājan sabhāryeṇa mahātmanāc anubhūtaṃ mahad duḥkhaṃ devarājena bhārata yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa katham indreṇa rājendra sabhāryeṇa mahātmanāc duḥkhaṃ prāptaṃ paraṃ ghoram etad icchāmi veditum śalya uvācaa śṛṇu rājan purā vṛttam itihāsaṃ purātanamc sabhāryeṇa yathā prāptaṃ duḥkham indreṇa bhārataa tvaṣṭā prajāpatir hy āsīd devaśreṣṭho mahātapāḥc sa putraṃ vai triśirasam indradrohāt kilāsṛjata aindraṃ sa prārthayat sthānaṃ viśvarūpo mahādyutiḥc tais tribhir vadanair ghoraiḥ sūryendujvalanopamaiḥa vedān ekena so dhīte surām ekena cāpibatc ekena ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ pibann iva nirīkṣatea sa tapasvī mṛdur dānto dharme tapasi codyataḥc tapo tapyan mahat tīvraṃ suduścaram ariṃdamaa tasya dṛṣṭvā tapovīryaṃ sattvaṃ cāmitatejasaḥc viṣādam agamac chakra indro yaṃ mā bhaved itia kathaṃ sajjeta bhogeṣu na ca tapyen mahat tapaḥc vivardhamānas triśirāḥ sarvaṃ tribhuvanaṃ graseta iti saṃcintya bahudhā buddhimān bharatarṣabhac ājñāpayat so psarasas tvaṣṭṛputrapralobhanea yathā sa sajjet triśirāḥ kāmabhogeṣu vai bhṛśamc kṣipraṃ kuruta gacchadhvaṃ pralobhayata mācirama śṛṅgāraveṣāḥ suśroṇyo bhāvair yuktā manoharaiḥb hāvabhāvasamāyuktāḥ sarvāḥ saundaryaśobhitāḥc pralobhayata bhadraṃ vaḥ śamayadhvaṃ bhayaṃ mamad prajāpatir bhaved eṣa candro vaiśravaṇo yamaḥd varuṇaḥ pāśahasto vā dharma eva bhavet svayama asvasthaṃ hy ātmanātmānaṃ lakṣayāmi varāṅganāḥc bhayam etan mahāghoraṃ kṣipraṃ nāśayatābalāḥ apsarasa ūcuḥa tathā yatnaṃ kariṣyāmaḥ śakra tasya pralobhanec yathā nāvāpsyasi bhayaṃ tasmād balaniṣūdanaa nirdahann iva cakṣurbhyāṃ yo sāv āste taponidhiḥc taṃ pralobhayituṃ deva gacchāmaḥ sahitā vayame yatiṣyāmo vaśe kartuṃ vyapanetuṃ ca te bhayam śalya uvācaa indreṇa tās tv anujñātā jagmus triśiraso ntikamc tatra tā vividhair bhāvair lobhayantyo varāṅganāḥe nṛtyaṃ saṃdarśayantyaś ca tathaivāṅgeṣu sauṣṭhavama viceruḥ saṃpraharṣaṃ ca nābhyagacchan mahātapāḥc indriyāṇi vaśe kṛtvā pūrṇasāgarasaṃnibhaḥa tās tu yatnaṃ paraṃ kṛtvā punaḥ śakram upasthitāḥc kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ sarvā devarājam athābruvana na sa śakyaḥ sudurdharṣo dhairyāc cālayituṃ prabhoc yat te kāryaṃ mahābhāga kriyatāṃ tadanantarama saṃpūjyāpsarasaḥ śakro visṛjya ca mahāmatiḥc cintayām āsa tasyaiva vadhopāyaṃ mahātmanaḥa sa tūṣṇīṃ cintayan vīro devarājaḥ pratāpavānc viniścitamatir dhīmān vadhe triśiraso bhavata vajram asya kṣipāmy adya sa kṣipraṃ na bhaviṣyatic śatruḥ pravṛddho nopekṣyo durbalo pi balīyasāa śāstrabuddhyā viniścitya kṛtvā buddhiṃ vadhe dṛḍhāmc atha vaiśvānaranibhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayāvahame mumoca vajraṃ saṃkruddhaḥ śakras triśirasaṃ pratia sa papāta hatas tena vajreṇa dṛḍham āhataḥc parvatasyeva śikharaṃ praṇunnaṃ medinītalea taṃ tu vajrahataṃ dṛṣṭvā śayānam acalopamamc na śarma lebhe devendro dīpitas tasya tejasād ghorarūpo mahāraudras tīvras tīvraparākramaḥe hato pi dīptatejāḥ sa jīvann iva ca dṛśyatef ghātitasya śirāṃsyājau jīvantīvādbhutāni vaif tato tibhītagātras tu śakra āste vicārayanf athājagāma paraśuṃ skandhenādāya vardhakiḥf tad araṇyaṃ mahārāja yatrāste sau nipātitaḥf śirāṃsi tasya jāyante trīṇy eva śakunās trayaḥf tittiriḥ kalaviṅkaś ca tathaiva ca kapiñjalaḥf viśvarūpaśirāṃsy eva jāyante tasya bhārataa abhitas tatra takṣāṇaṃ ghaṭamānaṃ śacīpatiḥc apaśyad abravīc cainaṃ satvaraṃ pākaśāsanaḥe kṣipraṃ chindhi śirāṃsy asya kuruṣva vacanaṃ mama takṣovācaa mahāskandho bhṛśaṃ hy eṣa paraśur na tariṣyatic kartuṃ cāhaṃ na śakṣyāmi karma sadbhir vigarhitam indra uvācaa mā bhais tvaṃ kṣipram etad vai kuruṣva vacanaṃ mamac matprasādād dhi te śastraṃ vajrakalpaṃ bhaviṣyati takṣovācaa kaṃ bhavantam ahaṃ vidyāṃ ghorakarmāṇam adya vaic etad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ tattvena kathayasva me indra uvācaa aham indro devarājas takṣan viditam astu tec kuruṣvaitad yathoktaṃ me takṣan mā tvaṃ vicārayad mayā hi nihataḥ śete triśirās tvaṃ ca viddhi vaid sa prahvaḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā idaṃ vacanam abravīt takṣovācaa krūreṇa nāpatrapase kathaṃ śakreha karmaṇāc ṛṣiputram imaṃ hatvā brahmahatyābhayaṃ na te indra uvācaa paścād dharmaṃ cariṣyāmi pāvanārthaṃ suduścaramc śatrur eṣa mahāvīryo vajreṇa nihato mayāa adyāpi cāham udvignas takṣann asmād bibhemi vaic kṣipraṃ chindhi śirāṃsi tvaṃ kariṣye nugrahaṃ tavaa śiraḥ paśos te dāsyanti bhāgaṃ yajñeṣu mānavāḥc eṣa te nugrahas takṣan kṣipraṃ kuru mama priyam śalya uvācaa etac chrutvā tu takṣā sa mahendravacanaṃ tadāc śirāṃsy atha triśirasaḥ kuṭhāreṇācchinat tadāa nikṛtteṣu tatas teṣu niṣkrāmaṃs triśirās tv athac kapiñjalās tittirāś ca kalaviṅkāś ca sarvaśaḥa yena vedān adhīte sma pibate somam eva cac tasmād vaktrān viniṣpetuḥ kṣipraṃ tasya kapiñjalāḥa yena sarvā diśo rājan pibann iva nirīkṣatec tasmād vaktrād viniṣpetus tittirās tasya pāṇḍavaa yat surāpaṃ tu tasyāsīd vaktraṃ triśirasas tadāc kalaviṅkā viniṣpetus tenāsya bharatarṣabhaa tatas teṣu nikṛtteṣu vijvaro maghavān abhūtb takṣṇe caiva varaṃ dattvā prahṛṣṭas tridaśeśvaraḥc jagāma tridivaṃ hṛṣṭas takṣāpi svagṛhān yayaud takṣāpi svagṛhaṃ gatvā naiva śaṃsati kasya citd athainaṃ nābhijānanti varṣam ekaṃ tathāgatamd atha saṃvatsare pūrṇe bhūtāḥ paśupateḥ prabhod te cākrośanta maghavān naḥ prabhur brahmahā itid tata indro vrataṃ ghoram acarat pākaśāsanaḥd tapasā ca susaṃyuktaḥ saha devair marudgaṇaiḥd samudre ca pṛthivyāṃ ca vanaspatiṣu strīṣu cad vibhajya brahmahatyāṃ ca tāṃś ca saṃyojayad varaiḥd varadas tu varaṃ dattvā pṛthivyai sāgarāya cad vanaspatibhyaḥ strībhyaś ca brahmahatyāṃ nunoda tāmd tatas tu śuddho bhagavān devair lokaiś ca pūjitaḥd indrasthānam upātiṣṭhat pūjyamāno maharṣibhiḥd mene kṛtārtham ātmānaṃ hatvā śatruṃ surārihāa tvaṣṭā prajāpatiḥ śrutvā śakreṇātha hataṃ sutamc krodhasaṃraktanayana idaṃ vacanam abravīta tapyamānaṃ tapo nityaṃ kṣāntaṃ dāntaṃ jitendriyamc anāparādhinaṃ yasmāt putraṃ hiṃsitavān mamaa tasmāc chakravadhārthāya vṛtram utpādayāmy ahamc lokāḥ paśyantu me vīryaṃ tapasaś ca balaṃ mahate sa ca paśyatu devendro durātmā pāpacetanaḥa upaspṛśya tataḥ kruddhas tapasvī sumahāyaśāḥc agniṃ hutvā samutpādya ghoraṃ vṛtram uvāca hae indraśatro vivardhasva prabhāvāt tapaso mamaa so vardhata divaṃ stabdhvā sūryavaiśvānaropamaḥc kiṃ karomīti covāca kālasūrya ivoditaḥe śakraṃ jahīti cāpy ukto jagāma tridivaṃ tataḥa tato yuddhaṃ samabhavad vṛtravāsavayos tadāc saṃkruddhayor mahāghoraṃ prasaktaṃ kurusattamad grastā lokāś ca vṛtreṇa sarve bharatasattamad tvaṣṭṛtejovivṛddhena vṛtreṇa sumahātmanād sarve gandhendriyarasā hṛtā bhārata tena vaid pṛthivī vāyur ākāśa āpo jyotiś ca pañcamaḥd hṛtam etan mahārāja vṛtreṇa sumahātmanāa tato jagrāha devendraṃ vṛtro vīraḥ śatakratumc apāvṛtya sa jagrāsa vṛtraḥ krodhasamanvitaḥa graste vṛtreṇa śakre tu saṃbhrāntās tridaśās tadāc asṛjaṃs te mahāsattvā jṛmbhikāṃ vṛtranāśinīma vijṛmbhamāṇasya tato vṛtrasyāsyād apāvṛtātc svāny aṅgāny abhisaṃkṣipya niṣkrānto balasūdanaḥe tataḥ prabhṛti lokeṣu jṛmbhikā prāṇisaṃśritāa jahṛṣuś ca surāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā śakraṃ viniḥsṛtamc tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ vṛtravāsavayoḥ punaḥe saṃrabdhayos tadā ghoraṃ suciraṃ bharatarṣabhaa yadā vyavardhata raṇe vṛtro balasamanvitaḥc tvaṣṭus tapobalād vidvāṃs tadā śakro nyavartataa nivṛtte tu tadā devā viṣādam agaman paramc sametya śakreṇa ca te tvaṣṭus tejovimohitāḥe amantrayanta te sarve munibhiḥ saha bhārataa kiṃ kāryam iti te rājan vicintya bhayamohitāḥc jagmuḥ sarve mahātmānaṃ manobhir viṣṇum avyayame upaviṣṭā mandarāgre sarve vṛtravadhepsavaḥ indra uvāca śalyaḥ ākhyānam uttamam idam itihāsaṃ purātanam śṛṇu me bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ draupadyā ca jayāvaham evaṃ vicintya vibudhaiḥ śakras tribhuvaneśvaraḥ vṛtrasya maraṇopāyaṃ punar vacanam abravīt sarvaṃ vyāptaṃ jagat tena vṛtreṇetīha naḥ śrutam vṛtrabhūteṣu lokeṣu bhayam indram upāgamat athendro hi mahātejāḥ sametya saha devataiḥ amantrayata tejasvī vṛtrasya vadhakāraṇāta sarvaṃ vyāptam idaṃ devā vṛtreṇa jagad avyayamc na hy asya sadṛśaṃ kiṃ cit pratighātāya yad bhaveta samartho hy abhavaṃ pūrvam asamartho smi sāṃpratamc kathaṃ kuryāṃ nu bhadraṃ vo duṣpradharṣaḥ sa me mataḥa tejasvī ca mahātmā ca yuddhe cāmitavikramaḥc graset tribhuvanaṃ sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣama tasmād viniścayam imaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ me divaukasaḥc viṣṇoḥ kṣayam upāgamya sametya ca mahātmanāe tena saṃmantrya vetsyāmo vadhopāyaṃ durātmanaḥ śalya uvācaa evam ukte maghavatā devāḥ sarṣigaṇās tadāb praṇipatya mahātmānaṃ sarvabhūtanamaskṛtamc śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ devaṃ jagmur viṣṇuṃ mahābalama ūcuś ca sarve deveśaṃ viṣṇuṃ vṛtrabhayārditāḥc tvayā lokās trayaḥ krāntās tribhir vikramaṇaiḥ prabhoa amṛtaṃ cāhṛtaṃ viṣṇo daityāś ca nihatā raṇec baliṃ baddhvā mahādaityaṃ śakro devādhipaḥ kṛtaḥa tvaṃ prabhuḥ sarvalokānāṃ tvayā sarvam idaṃ tatamc tvaṃ hi deva mahādevaḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥd gandharvoragarakṣāṇāṃ sarveṣām amarottamaa gatir bhava tvaṃ devānāṃ sendrāṇām amarottamac jagad vyāptam idaṃ sarvaṃ vṛtreṇāsurasūdana viṣṇur uvācaa avaśyaṃ karaṇīyaṃ me bhavatāṃ hitam uttamamc tasmād upāyaṃ vakṣyāmi yathāsau na bhaviṣyatia gacchadhvaṃ sarṣigandharvā yatrāsau viśvarūpadhṛkc sāma tasya prayuñjadhvaṃ tata enaṃ vijeṣyathaa bhaviṣyati gatir devāḥ śakrasya mama tejasāc adṛśyaś ca pravekṣyāmi vajram asyāyudhottamama gacchadhvam ṛṣibhiḥ sārdhaṃ gandharvaiś ca surottamāḥc vṛtrasya saha śakreṇa saṃdhiṃ kuruta māciram śalya uvācaa evam uktās tu devena ṛṣayas tridaśās tathāc yayuḥ sametya sahitāḥ śakraṃ kṛtvā puraḥsaramc   cakruś caiva vibhor vacaḥc tataḥ sametya vṛtreṇaa samīpam etya ca tadā sarva eva mahaujasaḥc taṃ tejasā prajvalitaṃ pratapantaṃ diśo daśaa grasantam iva lokāṃs trīn sūryācandramasau yathāc dadṛśus tatra te vṛtraṃ śakreṇa saha devatāḥa ṛṣayo tha tato bhyetya vṛtram ūcuḥ priyaṃ vacaḥc vyāptaṃ jagad idaṃ sarvaṃ tejasā tava durjayaa na ca śaknoṣi nirjetuṃ vāsavaṃ bhūrivikramamc yudhyatoś cāpi vāṃ kālo vyatītaḥ sumahān ihaa pīḍyante ca prajāḥ sarvāḥ sadevāsuramānavāḥc sakhyaṃ bhavatu te vṛtra śakreṇa saha nityadāe avāpsyasi sukhaṃ tvaṃ ca śakralokāṃś ca śāśvatāna ṛṣivākyaṃ niśamyātha sa vṛtraḥ sumahābalaḥc uvāca tāṃs tadā sarvān praṇamya śirasāsuraḥa sarve yūyaṃ mahābhāgā gandharvāś caiva sarvaśaḥc yad brūta tac chrutaṃ sarvaṃ mamāpi śṛṇutānaghāḥa saṃdhiḥ kathaṃ vai bhavitā mama śakrasya cobhayoḥc tejasor hi dvayor devāḥ sakhyaṃ vai bhavitā kathamd etad veditum icchāmi bruvantu ṛṣisattamāḥ ṛṣaya ūcuḥa sakṛt satāṃ saṃgataṃ lipsitavyaṃtataḥ paraṃ bhavitā bhavyam evac nātikramet satpuruṣeṇa saṃgataṃtasmāt satāṃ saṃgataṃ lipsitavyama dṛḍhaṃ satāṃ saṃgataṃ cāpi nityaṃbrūyāc cārthaṃ hy arthakṛcchreṣu dhīraḥc mahārthavat satpuruṣeṇa saṃgataṃtasmāt santaṃ na jighāṃseta dhīraḥa indraḥ satāṃ saṃmataś ca nivāsaś ca mahātmanāmc satyavādī hy adīnaś ca dharmavit suviniścitaḥa tena te saha śakreṇa saṃdhir bhavatu śāśvataḥc evaṃ viśvāsam āgaccha mā te bhūd buddhir anyathā śalya uvācaa maharṣivacanaṃ śrutvā tān uvāca mahādyutiḥc avaśyaṃ bhagavanto me mānanīyās tapasvinaḥa bravīmi yad ahaṃ devās tat sarvaṃ kriyatām ihac tataḥ sarvaṃ kariṣyāmi yad ūcur māṃ dvijarṣabhāḥa na śuṣkeṇa na cārdreṇa nāśmanā na ca dāruṇāc na śastreṇa na vajreṇa na divā na tathā niśia vadhyo bhaveyaṃ viprendrāḥ śakrasya saha daivataiḥc evaṃ me rocate saṃdhiḥ śakreṇa saha nityadāa bāḍham ity eva ṛṣayas tam ūcur bharatarṣabhac evaṃ kṛte tu saṃdhāne vṛtraḥ pramudito bhavatd tataḥ saṃdhiṃ mithaḥ kṛtvā ṛṣayo dīptatejasaḥd śakrasya saha vṛtreṇa punar jagmur yathāgatamd atha dīrghasya kālasya śakraḥ saṃcintya bhārataa yattaḥ sadābhavac cāpi śakro marṣasamanvitaḥc vṛtrasya vadhasaṃyuktān upāyān anucintayane randhrānveṣī samudvignaḥ sadābhūd balavṛtrahāf abhisaṃdhir mahendrasya saṃdhikarmaṇi yaḥ kṛtaḥf ṛṣibhis tv īritaṃ yac ca mahendras tad anusmarana sa kadā cit samudrānte tam apaśyan mahāsuramc saṃdhyākāla upāvṛtte muhūrte ramyadāruṇea tataḥ saṃcintya bhagavān varadānaṃ mahātmanaḥc saṃdhyeyaṃ vartate raudrā na rātrir divasaṃ na cad varaś cānena saṃprāpto hy avadhyo daivatair apid tat kathaṃ tv iha kartavyam upāyaṃ cintaye sadāe vṛtraś cāvaśyavadhyo yaṃ mama sarvaharo ripuḥa yadi vṛtraṃ na hanmy adya vañcayitvā mahāsuramc mahābalaṃ mahākāyaṃ na me śreyo bhaviṣyatia evaṃ saṃcintayann eva śakro viṣṇum anusmaranc atha phenaṃ tadāpaśyat samudre parvatopamama nāyaṃ śuṣko na cārdro yaṃ na ca śastram idaṃ tathāc enaṃ kṣepsyāmi vṛtrasya kṣaṇād eva naśiṣyatia savajram atha phenaṃ taṃ kṣipraṃ vṛtre nisṛṣṭavānb jagrāha ca sa taṃ phenam indro vṛtranibarhaṇamb nigṛhya śakro bāhubhyāṃ prāhiṇod vṛtramastakec praviśya phenaṃ taṃ viṣṇur atha vṛtraṃ vyanāśayata nihate tu tato vṛtre diśo vitimirābhavanc pravavau ca śivo vāyuḥ prajāś ca jahṛṣus tadāa tato devāḥ sagandharvā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥc ṛṣayaś ca mahendraṃ tam astuvan vividhaiḥ stavaiḥa namaskṛtaḥ sarvabhūtaiḥ sarvabhūtāni sāntvayanc hataśatruḥ prahṛṣṭātmā vāsavaḥ saha daivataiḥe viṣṇuṃ tribhuvanaśreṣṭhaṃ pūjayām āsa dharmavita tato hate mahāvīrye vṛtre devabhayaṃkarec anṛtenābhibhūto bhūc chakraḥ paramadurmanāḥe traiśīrṣayābhibhūtaś ca sa pūrvaṃ brahmahatyayāf mahādevasya bhūtaiś ca sa punar brahmahann itif ākruṣṭo nirbhayair bhūyo vrīḍito balavṛtrahāa so ntam āśritya lokānāṃ naṣṭasaṃjño vicetanaḥc na prājñāyata devendras tv abhibhūtaḥ svakalmaṣaiḥe praticchanno vasaty apsu prati vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa sa tu kauravyam āsādya drupadasya purohitaḥc satkṛto dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa bhīṣmeṇa vidureṇa caa sarvaṃ kauśalyam uktvādau pṛṣṭvā caivam anāmayamc sarvasenāpraṇetṝṇāṃ madhye vākyam uvāca haa sarvair bhavadbhir vidito rājadharmaḥ sanātanaḥc vākyopādānahetos tu vakṣyāmi vidite satia dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca pāṇḍuś ca sutāv ekasya viśrutauc tayoḥ samānaṃ draviṇaṃ paitṛkaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥa dhṛtarāṣṭrasya ye putrās te prāptāḥ paitṛkaṃ vasuc pāṇḍuputrāḥ kathaṃ nāma na prāptāḥ paitṛkaṃ vasua evaṃ gate pāṇḍaveyair viditaṃ vaḥ purā yathāc na prāptaṃ paitṛkaṃ dravyaṃ dhārtarāṣṭreṇa saṃvṛtama prāṇāntikair apy upāyaiḥ prayatadbhir anekaśaḥc śeṣavanto na śakitā nayituṃ yamasādanama punaś ca vardhitaṃ rājyaṃ svabalena mahātmabhiḥc chadmanāpahṛtaṃ kṣudrair dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ sasaubalaiḥa tad apy anumataṃ karma tathāyuktam anena vaic vāsitāś ca mahāraṇye varṣāṇīha trayodaśaa sabhāyāṃ kleśitair vīraiḥ sahabhāryais tathā bhṛśamc araṇye vividhāḥ kleśāḥ saṃprāptās taiḥ sudāruṇāḥa tathā virāṭanagare yonyantaragatair ivac prāptaḥ paramasaṃkleśo yathā pāpair mahātmabhiḥa te sarve pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā tat sarvaṃ pūrvakilbiṣamc sāmaiva kurubhiḥ sārdham icchanti kurupuṃgavāḥa teṣāṃ ca vṛttam ājñāya vṛttaṃ duryodhanasya cac anunetum ihārhanti dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ suhṛjjanāḥa na hi te vigrahaṃ vīrāḥ kurvanti kurubhiḥ sahac avināśena lokasya kāṅkṣante pāṇḍavāḥ svakama yaś cāpi dhārtarāṣṭrasya hetuḥ syād vigrahaṃ pratic sa ca hetur na mantavyo balīyāṃsas tathā hi tea akṣauhiṇyo hi saptaiva dharmaputrasya saṃgatāḥc yuyutsamānāḥ kurubhiḥ pratīkṣante sya śāsanama apare puruṣavyāghrāḥ sahasrākṣauhiṇīsamāḥc sātyakir bhīmasenaś ca yamau ca sumahābalaua ekādaśaitāḥ pṛtanā ekataś ca samāgatāḥc ekataś ca mahābāhur bahurūpo dhanaṃjayaḥa yathā kirīṭī senābhyaḥ sarvābhyo vyatiricyatec evam eva mahābāhur vāsudevo mahādyutiḥa bahulatvaṃ ca senānāṃ vikramaṃ ca kirīṭinaḥc buddhimattāṃ ca kṛṣṇasya buddhvā yudhyeta ko naraḥa te bhavanto yathādharmaṃ yathāsamayam eva cac prayacchantu pradātavyaṃ mā vaḥ kālo tyagād ayam vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā prajñāvṛddho mahādyutiḥc saṃpūjyainaṃ yathākālaṃ bhīṣmo vacanam abravīta diṣṭyā kuśalinaḥ sarve pāṇḍavāḥ saha bāndhavaiḥc diṣṭyā sahāyavantaś ca diṣṭyā dharme ca te ratāḥa diṣṭyā ca saṃdhikāmās te bhrātaraḥ kurunandanāḥc diṣṭyā na yuddhamanasaḥ saha dāmodareṇa tea bhavatā satyam uktaṃ ca sarvam etan na saṃśayaḥc atitīkṣṇaṃ tu te vākyaṃ brāhmaṇyād iti me matiḥa asaṃśayaṃ kleśitās te vane ceha ca pāṇḍavāḥc prāptāś ca dharmataḥ sarvaṃ pitur dhanam asaṃśayama kirīṭī balavān pārthaḥ kṛtāstraś ca mahābalaḥc ko hi pāṇḍusutaṃ yuddhe viṣaheta dhanaṃjayama api vajradharaḥ sākṣāt kim utānye dhanurbhṛtaḥc trayāṇām api lokānāṃ samartha iti me matiḥa bhīṣme bruvati tad vākyaṃ dhṛṣṭam ākṣipya manyumānc duryodhanaṃ samālokya karṇo vacanam abravīta na tan na viditaṃ brahmaṃl loke bhūtena kena citc punaruktena kiṃ tena bhāṣitena punaḥ punaḥa duryodhanārthe śakunir dyūte nirjitavān purāc samayena gato raṇyaṃ pāṇḍuputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥa na taṃ samayam ādṛtya rājyam icchati paitṛkamc balam āśritya matsyānāṃ pāñcālānāṃ ca pārthivaḥa duryodhano bhayād vidvan na dadyāt padam antataḥc dharmatas tu mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ pradadyāc chatrave pi caa yadi kāṅkṣanti te rājyaṃ pitṛpaitāmahaṃ punaḥc yathāpratijñaṃ kālaṃ taṃ carantu vanam āśritāḥa tato duryodhanasyāṅke vartantām akutobhayāḥc adhārmikām imāṃ buddhiṃ kuryur maurkhyād dhi kevalama atha te dharmam utsṛjya yuddham icchanti pāṇḍavāḥc āsādyemān kuruśreṣṭhān smariṣyanti vaco mama bhīṣma uvācaa kiṃ nu rādheya vācā te karma tat smartum arhasic eka eva yadā pārthaḥ ṣaḍ rathāñ jitavān yudhid bahuśo jīyamānasya karma dṛṣṭaṃ tadaiva ted virāṭanagare dhīraḥ kiṃ tvaṃ tatraiva nāgataḥa na ced evaṃ kariṣyāmo yad ayaṃ brāhmaṇo bravītc dhruvaṃ yudhi hatās tena bhakṣayiṣyāma pāṃsukānd duryodhanaḥ sahāmātyo vinaṅkṣayati na saṃśayaḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa dhṛtarāṣṭras tato bhīṣmam anumānya prasādya cac avabhartsya ca rādheyam idaṃ vacanam abravīta asmaddhitam idaṃ vākyaṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo bravītb duryodhanasamakṣaṃ ca pārthivānāṃ ca saṃnidhaub eṣa vakṣyati dharmātmā vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥb asmad dhitam idaṃ vākyaṃ bhīṣmeṇoktaṃ mahātmanāc pāṇḍavānāṃ hitaṃ caiva sarvasya jagatas tathāa cintayitvā tu pārthebhyaḥ preṣayiṣyāmi saṃjayamc sa bhavān pratiyātv adya pāṇḍavān eva mācirama sa taṃ satkṛtya kauravyaḥ preṣayām āsa pāṇḍavānc sabhāmadhye samāhūya saṃjayaṃ vākyam abravīt dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa prāptān āhuḥ saṃjaya pāṇḍuputrānupaplavye tān vijānīhi gatvāc ajātaśatruṃ ca sabhājayethādiṣṭyānagha grāmam upasthitas tvamd putro mahyaṃ mṛtyuvaśaṃ jagāmad duryodhanaḥ saṃjaya rāgabuddhiḥa sarvān vadeḥ saṃjaya svastimantaḥkṛcchraṃ vāsam atadarhā niruṣyac teṣāṃ śāntir vidyate smāsu śīghraṃmithyopetānām upakāriṇāṃ satāma nāhaṃ kva cit saṃjaya pāṇḍavānāṃmithyāvṛttiṃ kāṃ cana jātv apaśyamc sarvāṃ śriyaṃ hy ātmavīryeṇa labdhvāparyākārṣuḥ pāṇḍavā mahyam evaa doṣaṃ hy eṣāṃ nādhigacche parikṣannityaṃ kaṃ cid yena garheya pārthānc dharmārthābhyāṃ karma kurvanti nityaṃsukhapriyā nānurudhyanti kāmāna gharmaṃ śītaṃ kṣutpipāse tathaivanidrāṃ tandrīṃ krodhaharṣau pramādamc dhṛtyā caiva prajñayā cābhibhūyadharmārthayogān prayatanti pārthāḥa tyajanti mitreṣu dhanāni kālena saṃvāsāj jīryati maitram eṣāmc yathārhamānārthakarā hi pārthāsteṣāṃ dveṣṭā nāsty ājamīḍhasya pakṣea anyatra pāpād viṣamān mandabuddherduryodhanāt kṣudratarāc ca karṇātc teṣāṃ hīme hīnasukhapriyāṇāṃmahātmanāṃ saṃjanayanti tejaḥd bhāgaṃ gantuṃ ghaṭate mandabuddhird mahātmanāṃ saṃjaya dīptatejasāma utthānavīryaḥ sukham edhamānoduryodhanaḥ sukṛtaṃ manyate tatc teṣāṃ bhāgaṃ yac ca manyeta bālaḥśakyaṃ hartuṃ jīvatāṃ pāṇḍavānāma yasyārjunaḥ padavīṃ keśavaś cavṛkodaraḥ sātyako jātaśatroḥc mādrīputrau sṛñjayāś cāpi sarvepurā yuddhāt sādhu tasya pradānama sa hy evaikaḥ pṛthivīṃ savyasācīgāṇḍīvadhanvā praṇuded rathasthaḥc tathā viṣṇuḥ keśavo py apradhṛṣyolokatrayasyādhipatir mahātmāa tiṣṭheta kas tasya martyaḥ purastādyaḥ sarvadeveṣu vareṇya īḍyaḥc parjanyaghoṣān pravapañ śaraughānpataṃgasaṃghān iva śīghravegāna diśaṃ hy udīcīm api cottarān kurūngāṇḍīvadhanvaikaratho jigāyac dhanaṃ caiṣām āharat savyasācīsenānugān balidāṃś caiva cakrea yaś caiva devān khāṇḍave savyasācīgāṇḍīvadhanvā prajigāya sendrānc upāharat phalguno jātavedaseyaśo mānaṃ vardhayan pāṇḍavānāma gadābhṛtāṃ nādya samo sti bhīmāddhastyāroho nāsti samaś ca tasyac rathe rjunād āhur ahīnam enaṃbāhvor bale cāyutanāgavīryama suśikṣitaḥ kṛtavairas tarasvīdahet kruddhas tarasā dhārtarāṣṭrānc sadātyamarṣī balavān na śakyoyuddhe jetuṃ vāsavenāpi sākṣāta sucetasau balinau śīghrahastausuśikṣitau bhrātarau phalgunenac śyenau yathā pakṣipūgān rujantaumādrīputrau neha kurūn viśetāmd etad balaṃ pūrṇam asmākam evaṃd yat sātvatāṃ nāsti tṛtīyam anyata teṣāṃ madhye vartamānas tarasvīdhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pāṇḍavānām ihaikaḥc sahāmātyaḥ somakānāṃ prabarhaḥsaṃtyaktātmā pāṇḍavānāṃ jayāyad ajātaśatruṃ prasaheta ko nyod yeṣāṃ sa syād agraṇīr vṛṣṇisiṃhaḥa sahoṣitaś caritārtho vayaḥsthaḥśālveyānām adhipo vai virāṭaḥc saha putraiḥ pāṇḍavārthe ca śaśvadyudhiṣṭhiraṃ bhakta iti śrutaṃ mea avaruddhā balinaḥ kekayebhyomaheṣvāsā bhrātaraḥ pañca santic kekayebhyo rājyam ākāṅkṣamāṇāyuddhārthinaś cānuvasanti pārthāna sarve ca vīrāḥ pṛthivīpatīnāṃsamānītāḥ pāṇḍavārthe niviṣṭāḥc śūrān ahaṃ bhaktimataḥ śṛṇomiprītyā yuktān saṃśritān dharmarājama giryāśrayā durganivāsinaś cayodhāḥ pṛthivyāṃ kulajā viśuddhāḥc mlecchāś ca nānāyudhavīryavantaḥsamāgatāḥ pāṇḍavārthe niviṣṭāḥa pāṇḍyaś ca rājāmita indrakalpoyudhi pravīrair bahubhiḥ sametaḥc samāgataḥ pāṇḍavārthe mahātmālokapravīro prativīryatejāḥa astraṃ droṇād arjunād vāsudevātkṛpād bhīṣmād yena kṛtaṃ śṛṇomic yaṃ taṃ kārṣṇipratimaṃ prāhur ekaṃsa sātyakiḥ pāṇḍavārthe niviṣṭaḥa apāśritāś cedikarūṣakāś casarvotsāhair bhūmipālaiḥ sametāḥc teṣāṃ madhye sūryam ivātapantaṃśriyā vṛtaṃ cedipatiṃ jvalantama astambhanīyaṃ yudhi manyamānaṃjyākarṣatāṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ pṛthivyāmc sarvotsāhaṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ nihatyaprasahya kṛṣṇas tarasā mamardaa yaśomānau vardhayan yādavānāṃpurābhinac chiśupālaṃ samīkec yasya sarve vardhayanti sma mānaṃkarūṣarājapramukhā narendrāḥa tam asahyaṃ keśavaṃ tatra matvāsugrīvayuktena rathena kṛṣṇamc saṃprādravaṃś cedipatiṃ vihāyasiṃhaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣudramṛgā ivānyea yas taṃ pratīpas tarasā pratyudīyādāśaṃsamāno dvairathe vāsudevamc so śeta kṛṣṇena hataḥ parāsurvātenevonmathitaḥ karṇikāraḥa parākramaṃ me yad avedayantateṣām arthe saṃjaya keśavasyac anusmaraṃs tasya karmāṇi viṣṇorgāvalgaṇe nādhigacchāmi śāntima na jātu tāñ śatrur anyaḥ sahetayeṣāṃ sa syād agraṇīr vṛṣṇisiṃhaḥc pravepate me hṛdayaṃ bhayenaśrutvā kṛṣṇāv ekarathe sametaua no ced gacchet saṃgaraṃ mandabuddhistābhyāṃ suto me viparītacetāḥc no cet kurūn saṃjaya nirdahetāmindrāviṣṇū daityasenāṃ yathaivae mato hi me śakrasamo dhanaṃjayaḥsanātano vṛṣṇivīraś ca viṣṇuḥa dharmārāmo hrīniṣedhas tarasvīkuntīputraḥ pāṇḍavo jātaśatruḥc duryodhanena nikṛto manasvīno cet kruddhaḥ pradahed dhārtarāṣṭrāna nāhaṃ tathā hy arjunād vāsudevādbhīmād vāpi yamayor vā bibhemic yathā rājñaḥ krodhadīptasya sūtamanyor ahaṃ bhītataraḥ sadaivaa alaṃ tapobrahmacaryeṇa yuktaḥsaṃkalpo yaṃ mānasas tasya sidhyetc tasya krodhaṃ saṃjayāhaṃ samīkesthāne jānan bhṛśam asmy adya bhītaḥa sa gaccha śīghraṃ prahito rathenapāñcālarājasya camūṃ paretyac ajātaśatruṃ kuśalaṃ sma pṛccheḥpunaḥ punaḥ prītiyuktaṃ priyaś caiṣām ātmasamaś ca kṛṣṇovidvāṃś caiṣāṃ karmaṇi nityayuktaḥa samānīya pāṇḍavān sṛñjayāṃś cajanārdanaṃ yuyudhānaṃ virāṭamc anāmayaṃ madvacanena pṛccheḥsarvāṃs tathā draupadeyāṃś ca pañcaa yad yat tatra prāptakālaṃ parebhyastvaṃ manyethā bhāratānāṃ hitaṃ cac tat tad bhāṣethāḥ saṃjaya rājamadhyena mūrchayed yan na bhavec ca yuddham vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa rājñas tu vacanaṃ śrutvā dhṛtarāṣṭrasya saṃjayaḥc upaplavyaṃ yayau draṣṭuṃ pāṇḍavān amitaujasaḥa sa tu rājānam āsādya dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiramc praṇipatya tataḥ pūrvaṃ sūtaputro bhyabhāṣataa gāvalgaṇiḥ saṃjayaḥ sūtasūnurajātaśatrum avadat pratītaḥc diṣṭyā rājaṃs tvām arogaṃ prapaśyesahāyavantaṃ ca mahendrakalpama anāmayaṃ pṛcchati tvāmbikeyovṛddho rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro manīṣīc kaccid bhīmaḥ kuśalī pāṇḍavāgryodhanaṃjayas tau ca mādrītanūjaua kaccit kṛṣṇā draupadī rājaputrīsatyavratā vīrapatnī saputrāc manasvinī yatra ca vāñchasi tvamiṣṭān kāmān bhārata svastikāmaḥ yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa gāvalgaṇe saṃjaya svāgataṃ teprītātmāhaṃ tvābhivadāmi sūtac anāmayaṃ pratijāne tavāhaṃsahānujaiḥ kuśalī cāsmi vidvana cirād idaṃ kuśalaṃ bhāratasyaśrutvā rājñaḥ kuruvṛddhasya sūtac manye sākṣād dṛṣṭam ahaṃ narendraṃdṛṣṭvaiva tvāṃ saṃjaya prītiyogāta pitāmaho naḥ sthaviro manasvīmahāprājñaḥ sarvadharmopapannaḥc sa kauravyaḥ kuśalī tāta bhīṣmoyathāpūrvaṃ vṛttir apy asya kaccita kaccid rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputrovaicitravīryaḥ kuśalī mahātmāc mahārājo bāhlikaḥ prātipeyaḥkaccid vidvān kuśalī sūtaputraa sa somadattaḥ kuśalī tāta kaccidbhūriśravāḥ satyasaṃdhaḥ śalaś cac droṇaḥ saputraś ca kṛpaś ca vipromaheṣvāsāḥ kaccid ete py arogāḥc śāradvataḥ kuśalī tāta vipraḥa mahāprājñāḥ sarvaśāstrāvadātādhanurbhṛtāṃ mukhyatamāḥ pṛthivyāmc kaccin mānaṃ tāta labhanta etedhanurbhṛtaḥ kaccid ete py arogāḥa sarve kurubhyaḥ spṛhayanti saṃjayadhanurdharā ye niśitās tīkṣṇadhārāḥsuvāsasaḥ saṃmato hastavāpaḥa gadāpāṇir bhīmasenas tarasvīpravepayañ śatrusaṃghān anīkec nāgaḥ prabhinna iva naḍvalāsucaṅkramyate kaccid enaṃ smarantia mādrīputraḥ sahadevaḥ
