kṛṣṇonātikrame vacanaṃ keśavasya vāsudeva uvācaa avināśaṃ saṃjaya pāṇḍavānāmicchāmy ahaṃ bhūtim eṣāṃ priyaṃ cac tathā rājño dhṛtarāṣṭrasya sūtasadāśaṃse bahuputrasya vṛddhima kāmo hi me saṃjaya nityam evanānyad brūyāṃ tān prati śāmyatetic rājñaś ca hi priyam etac chṛṇomimanye caitat pāṇḍavānāṃ samarthama suduṣkaraś cātra śamo hi nūnaṃpradarśitaḥ saṃjaya pāṇḍavenac yasmin gṛddho dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputraḥkasmād eṣāṃ kalaho nātra mūrccheta tattvaṃ dharmaṃ vicaran saṃjayehamattaś ca jānāsi yudhiṣṭhirāc cac atho kasmāt saṃjaya pāṇḍavasyautsāhinaḥ pūrayataḥ svakarmae yathākhyātam āvasataḥ kuṭumbaṃpurākalpāt sādhu vilopam ātthaa asmin vidhau vartamāne yathāvaduccāvacā matayo brāhmaṇānāmc karmaṇāhuḥ siddhim eke paratrahitvā karma vidyayā siddhim eked no vindanti kṣatriyāḥ saṃjayāpie nābhuñjāno bhakṣyabhojyasya tṛpyedvidvān apīha viditaṃ brāhmaṇānāma yā vai vidyāḥ sādhayantīha karmatāsāṃ phalaṃ vidyate netarāsāmc tatreha vai dṛṣṭaphalaṃ tu karmapītvodakaṃ śāmyati tṛṣṇayārtaḥa so yaṃ vidhir vihitaḥ karmaṇaivatad vartate saṃjaya tatra karmac tatra yo nyat karmaṇaḥ sādhu manyenmoghaṃ tasya lapitaṃ durbalasyaa karmaṇāmī bhānti devāḥ paratrakarmaṇaiveha plavate mātariśvāc ahorātre vidadhat karmaṇaivaatandrito nityam udeti sūryaḥa māsārdhamāsān atha nakṣatrayogānatandritaś candramā abhyupaitic atandrito dahate jātavedāḥsamidhyamānaḥ karma kurvan prajābhyaḥa atandritā bhāram imaṃ mahāntaṃbibharti devī pṛthivī balenac atandritāḥ śīghram apo vahantisaṃtarpayantyaḥ sarvabhūtāni nadyaḥa atandrito varṣati bhūritejāḥsaṃnādayann antarikṣaṃ divaṃ cac atandrito brahmacaryaṃ cacāraśreṣṭhatvam icchan balabhid devatānāma hitvā sukhaṃ manasaś ca priyāṇitena śakraḥ karmaṇā śraiṣṭhyam āpac satyaṃ dharmaṃ pālayann apramattodamaṃ titikṣāṃ samatāṃ priyaṃ cae etāni sarvāṇy upasevamānodevarājyaṃ maghavān prāpa mukhyama bṛhaspatir brahmacaryaṃ cacārasamāhitaḥ saṃśitātmā yathāvatc hitvā sukhaṃ pratirudhyendriyāṇitena devānām agamad gauravaṃ saḥa nakṣatrāṇi karmaṇāmutra bhāntirudrādityā vasavo thāpi viśvec yamo rājā vaiśravaṇaḥ kuberogandharvayakṣāpsarasaś ca śubhrāḥe brahmacaryaṃ vedavidyāḥ kriyāś caniṣevamāṇā munayo mutra bhāntia jānann imaṃ sarvalokasya dharmaṃbrāhmaṇānāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ viśāṃ cac sa kasmāt tvaṃ jānatāṃ jñānavān sanvyāyacchase saṃjaya kauravārthea āmnāyeṣu nityasaṃyogam asyatathāśvamedhe rājasūye ca viddhic saṃyujyate dhanuṣā varmaṇā cahastatrāṇai rathaśastraiś ca bhūyaḥa te ced ime kauravāṇām upāyamadhigaccheyur avadhenaiva pārthāḥc dharmatrāṇaṃ puṇyam eṣāṃ kṛtaṃ syādārye vṛtte bhīmasenaṃ nigṛhyaa te cet pitrye karmaṇi vartamānāāpadyeran diṣṭavaśena mṛtyumc yathāśaktyā pūrayantaḥ svakarmatad apy eṣāṃ nidhanaṃ syāt praśastama utāho tvaṃ manyase sarvam evarājñāṃ yuddhe vartate dharmatantramc ayuddhe vā vartate dharmatantraṃtathaiva te vācam imāṃ śṛṇomia cāturvarṇyasya prathamaṃ vibhāgamavekṣya tvaṃ saṃjaya svaṃ ca karmac niśamyātho pāṇḍavānāṃ svakarmapraśaṃsa vā ninda vā yā matis tea adhīyīta brāhmaṇo tho yajetadadyād iyāt tīrthamukhyāni caivac adhyāpayed yājayec cāpi yājyānpratigrahān vā viditān pratīcchetd adhīyīta kṣatriyo tho yajetad dadyād dhanaṃ na tu yāceta kiṃ citd na yājayen na tu cādhyāpayītad evaṃ smṛtaḥ kṣatradharmaḥ purāṇaḥa tathā rājanyo rakṣaṇaṃ vai prajānāṃkṛtvā dharmeṇāpramatto tha dattvāc yajñair iṣṭvā sarvavedān adhītyadārān kṛtvā puṇyakṛd āvased gṛhānd sa dharmātmā dharmam adhītya puṇyaṃd yad icchayā vrajati brahmalokama vaiśyo dhītya kṛṣigorakṣapaṇyairvittaṃ cinvan pālayann apramattaḥc priyaṃ kurvan brāhmaṇakṣatriyāṇāṃdharmaśīlaḥ puṇyakṛd āvased gṛhāna paricaryā vandanaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃnādhīyīta pratiṣiddho sya yajñaḥc nityotthito bhūtaye tandritaḥ syādeṣa smṛtaḥ śūdradharmaḥ purāṇaḥa etān rājā pālayann apramattoniyojayan sarvavarṇān svadharmec akāmātmā samavṛttiḥ prajāsunādhārmikān anurudhyeta kāmāna śreyāṃs tasmād yadi vidyeta kaś cidabhijñātaḥ sarvadharmopapannaḥb yatrāpramatto rakṣati bhūmipālob niyojayan sveṣu dharmeṣu varṇānc sa taṃ duṣṭam anuśiṣyāt prajānanna ced gṛdhyed iti tasmin na sādhua yadā gṛdhyet parabhūmiṃ nṛśaṃsovidhiprakopād balam ādadānaḥc tato rājñāṃ bhavitā yuddham etattatra jātaṃ varma śastraṃ dhanuś cae indreṇedaṃ dasyuvadhāya karmautpāditaṃ varma śastraṃ dhanuś caf tatra puṇyaṃ dasyuvadhena labhyatef so yaṃ doṣaḥ kurubhis tīvrarūpaḥf adharmajñair dharmam abudhyamānaiḥf prādurbhūtaḥ saṃjaya tan na sādhuf tatra rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputrof dhanaṃ haret pāṇḍavānām akasmātf nāvekṣante rājadharmaṃ purāṇaṃf tadanvayāḥ kuravaḥ sarva evaa steno hared yatra dhanaṃ hy adṛṣṭaḥprasahya vā yatra hareta dṛṣṭaḥc ubhau garhyau bhavataḥ saṃjayaitaukiṃ vai pṛthak tvaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putree yo yaṃ lobhān manyate dharmam etaṃyam icchate manyuvaśānugāmīe svadharmaṃ vai paravittāpahārāne nāsau dharmaḥ steyam āhur vidhijñāḥa bhāgaḥ punaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ niviṣṭastaṃ no kasmād ādadīran pare vaic asmin pade yudhyatāṃ no vadho piślāghyaḥ pitryaḥ pararājyād viśiṣṭaḥe etān dharmān kauravāṇāṃ purāṇānācakṣīthāḥ saṃjaya rājyamadhyea ye te mandā mṛtyuvaśābhipannāḥsamānītā dhārtarāṣṭreṇa mūḍhāḥc idaṃ punaḥ karma pāpīya evasabhāmadhye paśya vṛttaṃ kurūṇāma priyāṃ bhāryāṃ draupadīṃ pāṇḍavānāṃyaśasvinīṃ śīlavṛttopapannāmc yad upekṣanta kuravo bhīṣmamukhyāḥkāmānugenoparuddhāṃ rudantīmd kāmātmāno mandabuddher viceṣṭāṃa taṃ cet tadā te sakumāravṛddhāavārayiṣyan kuravaḥ sametāḥc mama priyaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro kariṣyatputrāṇāṃ ca kṛtam asyābhaviṣyata duḥśāsanaḥ prātilomyān nināyasabhāmadhye śvaśurāṇāṃ ca kṛṣṇāmc sā tatra nītā karuṇāny avocannānyaṃ kṣattur nātham adṛṣṭa kaṃ cita kārpaṇyād eva sahitās tatra rājñonāśaknuvan prativaktuṃ sabhāyāmc ekaḥ kṣattā dharmyam arthaṃ bruvāṇodharmaṃ buddhvā pratyuvācālpabuddhima anuktvā tvaṃ dharmam evaṃ sabhāyāmathecchase pāṇḍavasyopadeṣṭumc kṛṣṇā tv etat karma cakāra śuddhaṃsuduṣkaraṃ tad dhi sabhāṃ sametyae yena kṛcchrāt pāṇḍavān ujjahāratathātmānaṃ naur iva sāgaraughāta yatrābravīt sūtaputraḥ sabhāyāṃkṛṣṇāṃ sthitāṃ śvaśurāṇāṃ samīpec na te gatir vidyate yājñaseniprapadyedānīṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya veśmae parājitās te patayo na santipatiṃ cānyaṃ bhāmini tvaṃ vṛṇīṣvaa yo bībhatsor hṛdaye prauḍha āsīdasthipracchinmarmaghātī sughoraḥc karṇāc charo vāṅmayas tigmatejāḥpratiṣṭhito hṛdaye phalgunasyaa kṛṣṇājināni paridhit samānānduḥśāsanaḥ kaṭukāny abhyabhāṣatc ete sarve ṣaṇḍhatilā vinaṣṭāḥkṣayaṃ gatā narakaṃ dīrghakālama gāndhārarājaḥ śakunir nikṛtyāyad abravīd dyūtakāle sa pārthānc parājito nakulaḥ kiṃ tavāstikṛṣṇayā tvaṃ dīvya vai yājñasenyāa jānāsi tvaṃ saṃjaya sarvam etaddyūte vācyaṃ vākyam evaṃ yathoktamc svayaṃ tv ahaṃ prārthaye tatra gantuṃsamādhātuṃ kāryam etad vipannamd jānāsi tvaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya mohaṃd durātmanaḥ pāpavaśānugasyaa ahāpayitvā yadi pāṇḍavārthaṃśamaṃ kurūṇām atha cec careyamc puṇyaṃ ca me syāc caritaṃ mahodayaṃmucyeraṃś ca kuravo mṛtyupāśāta api vācaṃ bhāṣamāṇasya kāvyāṃdharmārāmām arthavatīm ahiṃsrāmc avekṣeran dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ samakṣaṃmāṃ ca prāptaṃ kuravaḥ pūjayeyuḥa ato nyathā rathinā phalgunenabhīmena caivāhavadaṃśitenac parāsiktān dhārtarāṣṭrāṃs tu viddhipradahyamānān karmaṇā svena mandāna parājitān pāṇḍaveyāṃs tu vācoraudrarūpā bhāṣate dhārtarāṣṭraḥc gadāhasto bhīmaseno pramattoduryodhanaṃ smārayitvā hi kālea suyodhano manyumayo mahādrumaḥskandhaḥ karṇaḥ śakunis tasya śākhāḥc duḥśāsanaḥ puṣpaphale samṛddhemūlaṃ rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro manīṣīa yudhiṣṭhiro dharmamayo mahādrumaḥskandho rjuno bhīmaseno sya śākhāḥc mādrīputrau puṣpaphale samṛddhemūlaṃ tv ahaṃ brahma ca brāhmaṇāś caa vanaṃ rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputrovyāghrā vane saṃjaya pāṇḍaveyāḥb dhārtarāṣṭro vanaṃ rājā vyāghrāḥ pāṇḍusutā matāḥb latādharmā dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrāb naravyāghrāḥ saṃjaya pāṇḍaveyāḥb siṃhābhiguptaṃ na vanaṃ vinaśyetb siṃho na naśyeta vanābhiguptaḥb vanaṃ rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro vane vyāghrāś ca pāṇḍavāḥc mā vanaṃ chindhi savyāghraṃ mā vyāghrān nīnaśo vanāta nirvano vadhyate vyāghro nirvyāghraṃ chidyate vanamc tasmād vyāghro vanaṃ rakṣed vanaṃ vyāghraṃ ca pālayeta latādharmā dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ śālāḥ saṃjaya pāṇḍavāḥc na latā vardhate jātu anāśritya mahādrumama sthitāḥ śuśrūṣituṃ pārthāḥ sthitā yoddhum ariṃdamāḥc yatkṛtyaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya tat karotu narādhipaḥa sthitāḥ śame mahātmānaḥ pāṇḍavā dharmacāriṇaḥc yodhāḥ samṛddhās tad vidvan nācakṣīthā yathātatham saṃjaya uvācaa āmantraye tvā naradevadevagacchāmy ahaṃ pāṇḍava svasti te stuc kaccin na vācā vṛjinaṃ hi kiṃ ciduccāritaṃ me manaso bhiṣaṅgāta janārdanaṃ bhīmasenārjunau camādrīsutau sātyakiṃ cekitānamc āmantrya gacchāmi śivaṃ sukhaṃ vaḥsaumyena māṃ paśyata cakṣuṣā nṛpāḥ yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa anujñātaḥ saṃjaya svasti gacchana no kārṣīr apriyaṃ jātu kiṃ citc vidmaś ca tvā te ca vayaṃ ca sarveśuddhātmānaṃ madhyagataṃ sabhāsthama āpto dūtaḥ saṃjaya supriyo sikalyāṇavāk śīlavān dṛṣṭimāṃś cac na muhyes tvaṃ saṃjaya jātu matyāna ca krudhyer ucyamāno pi tathyama na marmagāṃ jātu vaktāsi rūkṣāṃnopastutiṃ kaṭukāṃ nota śuktāmc dharmārāmām arthavatīm ahiṃsrāmetāṃ vācaṃ tava jānāmi sūtaa tvam eva naḥ priyatamo si dūtaihāgacched viduro vā dvitīyaḥc abhīkṣṇadṛṣṭo si purā hi nas tvaṃdhanaṃjayasyātmasamaḥ sakhāsia ito gatvā saṃjaya kṣipram evaupātiṣṭhethā brāhmaṇān ye tadarhāḥc viśuddhavīryāṃś caraṇopapannānkule jātān sarvadharmopapannāna svādhyāyino brāhmaṇā bhikṣavaś catapasvino ye ca nityā vaneṣuc abhivādyā vai madvacanena vṛddhāstathetareṣāṃ kuśalaṃ vadethāḥa purohitaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya rājñaācāryāś ca ṛtvijo ye ca tasyac taiś ca tvaṃ tāta sahitair yathārhaṃsaṃgacchethāḥ kuśalenaiva sūtad aśrotriyā ye ca vasanti vṛddhād manasvinaḥ śīlabalopapannāḥd āśaṃsanto smākam anusmarantod yathāśakti dharmamātrāṃ carantaḥd ślāghasva māṃ kuśalinaṃ sma tebhyod hy anāmayaṃ tāta pṛccher jaghanyamd tato vyagras tanmanāḥ prāñjaliś cad kuryā namo madvacanena tebhyaḥd ye jīvanti vyavahāreṇa rāṣṭred ye pālayanto nivasanti rāṣṭred kṛṣīvalā bibhrati ye ca lokaṃd teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ kuśalaṃ sma pṛccheḥa ācārya iṣṭo napago vidheyovedān īpsan brahmacaryaṃ cacārac yo straṃ catuṣpāt punar eva cakredroṇaḥ prasanno bhivādyo yathārhama adhītavidyaś caraṇopapannoyo straṃ catuṣpāt punar eva cakrec gandharvaputrapratimaṃ tarasvinaṃtam aśvatthāmānaṃ kuśalaṃ sma pṛccheḥa śāradvatasyāvasathaṃ sma gatvāmahārathasyāstravidāṃ varasyac tvaṃ mām abhīkṣṇaṃ parikīrtayan vaikṛpasya pādau saṃjaya pāṇinā spṛśeḥa yasmiñ śauryam ānṛśaṃsyaṃ tapaś caprajñā śīlaṃ śrutisattve dhṛtiś cab nivedayāsmāsu yathānuvṛttamc pādau gṛhītvā kurusattamasyabhīṣmasya māṃ tatra nivedayethāḥa prajñācakṣur yaḥ praṇetā kurūṇāṃbahuśruto vṛddhasevī manīṣīc tasmai rājñe sthavirāyābhivādyaācakṣīthāḥ saṃjaya mām arogama jyeṣṭhaḥ putro dhṛtarāṣṭrasya mandomūrkhaḥ śaṭhaḥ saṃjaya pāpaśīlaḥc praśāstā vai pṛthivī yena sarvāsuyodhanaṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥa bhrātā kanīyān api tasya mandastathāśīlaḥ saṃjaya so pi śaśvatc maheṣvāsaḥ śūratamaḥ kurūṇāṃduḥśāsanaṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥd tathaiva ye tasya vaśānugāś cad ye cāpy anye pārthivāś ca pradhānāḥd tebhyo yathārhaṃ kuśalaṃ sma sarvaṃd tathā vācyaṃ madvacanād dhi sūtaa vṛndārakaṃ kavim artheṣv amūḍhaṃmahāprajñaṃ sarvadharmopapannamc na tasya yuddhaṃ rocate vai kadā cidvaiśyāputraṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥa nikartane devane yo dvitīyaśchannopadhaḥ sādhudevī matākṣaḥc yo durjayo devitavyena saṃkhyesa citrasenaḥ kuśalaṃ tāta vācyaḥa yasya kāmo vartate nityam evanānyaḥ śamād bhāratānām iti smac sa bāhlikānām ṛṣabho manasvīpurā yathā mābhivadet prasannaḥa guṇair anekaiḥ pravaraiś ca yuktovijñānavān naiva ca niṣṭhuro yaḥc snehād amarṣaṃ sahate sadaivasa somadattaḥ pūjanīyo mato mea arhattamaḥ kuruṣu saumadattiḥsa no bhrātā saṃjaya matsakhā cac maheṣvāso rathinām uttamo yaḥsahāmātyaḥ kuśalaṃ tasya pṛccheḥd bhūriśravās tāta nipātayodhīd maheṣvāso rathinām uttamo gryaḥd gatvā sma taṃ madvacanena brūyāḥd śalyaṃ tathā madvacanāt pratītaḥd maheṣvāso rathinām uttamo gryaḥd samaḥ śalo rakṣitā pṛṣṭham asyad hrīniṣedho devitā vai matākṣaḥd satyavrataḥ purumitro jayaś cad ye prasthānaṃ tatra me nābhyanandaṃsd teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥa ye caivānye kurumukhyā yuvānaḥputrāḥ pautrā bhrātaraś caiva ye naḥc yaṃ yam eṣāṃ yena yenābhigaccheranāmayaṃ madvacanena vācyaḥa ye rājānaḥ pāṇḍavāyodhanāyasamānītā dhārtarāṣṭreṇa ke citc vasātayaḥ śālvakāḥ kekayāś catathāmbaṣṭhā ye trigartāś ca mukhyāḥa prācyodīcyā dākṣiṇātyāś ca śūrāstathā pratīcyāḥ pārvatīyāś ca sarvec anṛśaṃsāḥ śīlavṛttopapannāsteṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥa hastyārohā rathinaḥ sādinaś capadātayaś cāryasaṃghā mahāntaḥc ākhyāya māṃ kuśalinaṃ sma teṣāmanāmayaṃ paripṛccheḥ samagrāna tathā rājño hy arthayuktān amātyāndauvārikān ye ca senāṃ nayantic āyavyayaṃ ye gaṇayanti yuktāarthāṃś ca ye mahataś cintayantia gāndhārarājaḥ śakuniḥ pārvatīyonikartane yo dvitīyo kṣadevīc mānaṃ kurvan dhārtarāṣṭrasya sūtamithyābuddheḥ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥa yaḥ pāṇḍavān ekarathena vīraḥsamutsahaty apradhṛṣyān vijetumc yo muhyatāṃ mohayitādvitīyovaikartanaṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥa sa eva bhaktaḥ sa guruḥ sa bhṛtyaḥsa vai pitā sa ca mātā suhṛc cac agādhabuddhir viduro dīrghadarśīsa no mantrī kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥd vṛddhāṃ gāndhārīṃ samupetya saṃjayad kuntyā dvitīyām abhivādya pṛccheḥa vṛddhāḥ striyo yāś ca guṇopapannāyā jñāyante saṃjaya mātaras tāḥc tābhiḥ sarvābhiḥ sahitābhiḥ sametyastrībhir vṛddhābhir abhivādaṃ vadethāḥa kaccit putrā jīvaputrāḥ susamyagvartante vo vṛttim anṛśaṃsarūpāmc iti smoktvā saṃjaya brūhi paścādajātaśatruḥ kuśalī saputraḥa yā no bhāryāḥ saṃjaya vettha tatratāsāṃ sarvāsāṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥc susaṃguptāḥ surabhayo navadyāḥkaccid gṛhān āvasathāpramattāḥd ākhyāya māṃ kuśalinaṃ sma tebhyod hy anāmayaṃ saṃjaya tāta pṛccheḥa kaccid vṛttiṃ śvaśureṣu bhadrāḥkalyāṇīṃ vartadhvam anṛśaṃsarūpāmc yathā ca vaḥ syuḥ patayo nukūlāstathā vṛttim ātmanaḥ sthāpayadhvama yā naḥ snuṣāḥ saṃjaya vettha tatraprāptāḥ kulebhyaś ca guṇopapannāḥc prajāvatyo brūhi sametya tāś cayudhiṣṭhiro vo bhyavadat prasannaḥa kanyāḥ svajethāḥ sadaneṣu saṃjayaanāmayaṃ madvacanena pṛṣṭvāc kalyāṇā vaḥ santu patayo nukūlāyūyaṃ patīnāṃ bhavatānukūlāḥa alaṃkṛtā vastravatyaḥ sugandhāabībhatsāḥ sukhitā bhogavatyaḥc laghu yāsāṃ darśanaṃ vāk ca laghvīveśastriyaḥ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥa dāsīputrā ye ca dāsāḥ kurūṇāṃtadāśrayā bahavaḥ kubjakhañjāḥc ākhyāya māṃ kuśalinaṃ sma tebhyoanāmayaṃ paripṛccher jaghanyama kaccid vṛttir vartate vai purāṇīkaccid bhogān dhārtarāṣṭro dadātic aṅgahīnān kṛpaṇān vāmanāṃś caānṛśaṃsyād dhṛtarāṣṭro bibhartia andhāś ca sarve sthavirās tathaivahastājīvā bahavo ye tra santic ākhyāya māṃ kuśalinaṃ sma teṣāmanāmayaṃ paripṛccher jaghanyama mā bhaiṣṭa duḥkhena kujīvitenanūnaṃ kṛtaṃ paralokeṣu pāpamc nigṛhya śatrūn suhṛdo nugṛhyavāsobhir annena ca vo bhariṣyed na cāpy etac chakyam ekena vaktuṃd nānādeśyā bahavo jātisaṃghāḥd viproṣito bālavad draṣṭum icchand namasye haṃ saṃjaya bhaimasenānd te me yathā vācam imāṃ yathoktāṃd tvayocyamānāṃ śṛṇuyus tathā kurua santy eva me brāhmaṇebhyaḥ kṛtānibhāvīny atho no bata vartayantic paśyāmy ahaṃ yuktarūpāṃs tathaivatām eva siddhiṃ śrāvayethā nṛpaṃ tama ye cānāthā durbalāḥ sarvakālamātmany eva prayatante tha mūḍhāḥc tāṃś cāpi tvaṃ kṛpaṇān sarvathaivaasmadvākyāt kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥa ye cāpy anye saṃśritā dhārtarāṣṭrānnānādigbhyo bhyāgatāḥ sūtaputrac dṛṣṭvā tāṃś caivārhataś cāpi sarvānsaṃpṛcchethāḥ kuśalaṃ cāvyayaṃ caa evaṃ sarvānāgatābhyāgatāṃś carājño dūtān sarvadigbhyo bhyupetānc pṛṣṭvā sarvān kuśalaṃ tāṃś ca sūtapaścād ahaṃ kuśalī teṣu vācyaḥa na hīdṛśāḥ santy apare pṛthivyāṃye yodhakā dhārtarāṣṭreṇa labdhāḥc dharmas tu nityo mama dharma evamahābalaḥ śatrunibarhaṇāyaa idaṃ punar vacanaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃsuyodhanaṃ saṃjaya śrāvayethāḥc yas te śarīre hṛdayaṃ dunotikāmaḥ kurūn asapatno nuśiṣyāma na vidyate yuktir etasya kā cinnaivaṃvidhāḥ syāma yathā priyaṃ tec dadasva vā śakrapuraṃ mamaivayudhyasva vā bhāratamukhya vīra yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa uta santam asantaṃ ca bālaṃ vṛddhaṃ ca saṃjayac utābalaṃ balīyāṃsaṃ dhātā prakurute vaśea uta bālāya pāṇḍityaṃ paṇḍitāyota bālatāmc dadāti sarvam īśānaḥ purastāc chukram uccarana alaṃ vijñāpanāya syād ācakṣīthā yathātathamc atho mantraṃ mantrayitvā anyonyenātihṛṣṭavata gāvalgaṇe kurūn gatvā dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ mahābalamc abhivādyopasaṃgṛhya tataḥ pṛccher anāmayama brūyāś cainaṃ tvam āsīnaṃ kurubhiḥ parivāritamc tavaiva rājan vīryeṇa sukhaṃ jīvanti pāṇḍavāḥa tava prasādād bālās te prāptā rājyam ariṃdamac rājye tān sthāpayitvāgre nopekṣīr vinaśiṣyataḥa sarvam apy etad ekasya nālaṃ saṃjaya kasya citc tāta saṃhatya jīvāmo mā dviṣadbhyo vaśaṃ gamaḥa tathā bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ bhāratānāṃ pitāmahamc śirasābhivadethās tvaṃ mama nāma prakīrtayana abhivādya ca vaktavyas tato smākaṃ pitāmahaḥc bhavatā śaṃtanor vaṃśo nimagnaḥ punar uddhṛtaḥa sa tvaṃ kuru tathā tāta svamatena pitāmahac yathā jīvanti te pautrāḥ prītimantaḥ parasparama tathaiva viduraṃ brūyāḥ kurūṇāṃ mantradhāriṇamc ayuddhaṃ saumya bhāṣasva hitakāmo yudhiṣṭhiraḥa atho suyodhanaṃ brūyā rājaputram amarṣaṇamc madhye kurūṇām āsīnam anunīya punaḥ punaḥa apaśyan mām upekṣantaṃ kṛṣṇām ekāṃ sabhāgatāmc tadduḥkham atitikṣāma mā vadhīṣma kurūn itia evaṃ pūrvāparān kleśān atitikṣanta pāṇḍavāḥc yathā balīyasaḥ santas tat sarvaṃ kuravo viduḥa yan naḥ prāvrājayaḥ saumya ajinaiḥ prativāsitānc tadduḥkham atitikṣāma mā vadhīṣma kurūn itia yat tat sabhāyām ākramya kṛṣṇāṃ keśeṣv adharṣayatc duḥśāsanas te numate tac cāsmābhir upekṣitama yathocitaṃ svakaṃ bhāgaṃ labhemahi paraṃtapac nivartaya paradravye buddhiṃ gṛddhāṃ nararṣabhaa śāntir evaṃ bhaved rājan prītiś caiva parasparamc rājyaikadeśam api naḥ prayaccha śamam icchatāma kuśasthalaṃ vṛkasthalam āsandī vāraṇāvatamc avasānaṃ bhaved atra kiṃ cid eva tu pañcamama bhrātṝṇāṃ dehi pañcānāṃ grāmān pañca suyodhanac śāntir no stu mahāprājña jñātibhiḥ saha saṃjayaa bhrātā bhrātaram anvetu pitā putreṇa yujyatāmc smayamānāḥ samāyāntu pāñcālāḥ kurubhiḥ sahaa akṣatān kurupāñcālān paśyema iti kāmayec sarve sumanasas tāta śāmyāma bharatarṣabhaa alam eva śamāyāsmi tathā yuddhāya saṃjayac dharmārthayor alaṃ cāhaṃ mṛdave dāruṇāya ca vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa anujñātaḥ pāṇḍavena prayayau saṃjayas tadāc śāsanaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya sarvaṃ kṛtvā mahātmanaḥd tatas tu saṃjayaḥ kṣipram ekāhnaiva paraṃtapad yāti sma hāstinapuraṃ niśākāle samāviśata saṃprāpya hāstinapuraṃ śīghraṃ ca praviveśa hac antaḥpuram upasthāya dvāḥsthaṃ vacanam abravīta ācakṣva māṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrāya dvāḥsthaupāgataṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ sakāśātb ācakṣva dhṛtarāṣṭrāya dvāḥstha māṃ samupāgatamb sakāśāt pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ saṃjayaṃ mā ciraṃ kṛthāḥc jāgarti ced abhivades tvaṃ hi kṣattaḥpraviśeyaṃ vidito bhūmipasyad nivedyam atrātyayikaṃ hi me stid dvāḥstho tha śrutvā nṛpatiṃ jagādad jāgarti ced abhivādyasya pādaud nivedyāhaṃ pāṇḍavoktiṃ sayuktim dvāḥstha uvācaa saṃjayo yaṃ bhūmipate namas tedidṛkṣayā dvāram upāgatas tec prāpto dūtaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ sakāśātpraśādhi rājan kim ayaṃ karotu dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa ācakṣva māṃ sukhinaṃ kālyam asmaipraveśyatāṃ svāgataṃ saṃjayāyac na cāham etasya bhavāmy akālyaḥsa me kasmād dvāri tiṣṭheta kṣattaḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tataḥ praviśyānumate nṛpasyamahad veśma prājñaśūrāryaguptamc siṃhāsanasthaṃ pārthivam āsasādavaicitravīryaṃ prāñjaliḥ sūtaputraḥ saṃjaya uvācaa saṃjayo haṃ bhūmipate namas teprāpto smi gatvā naradeva pāṇḍavānc abhivādya tvāṃ pāṇḍuputro manasvīyudhiṣṭhiraḥ kuśalaṃ cānvapṛcchata sa te putrān pṛcchati prīyamāṇaḥkaccit putraiḥ prīyase naptṛbhiś cac tathā suhṛdbhiḥ sacivaiś ca rājanye cāpi tvām upajīvanti taiś ca dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa abhyetya tvāṃ tāta vadāmi saṃjayaajātaśatruṃ ca sukhena pārthamc kaccit sa rājā kuśalī saputraḥsahāmātyaḥ sānujaḥ kauravāṇām saṃjaya uvācaa sahāmātyaḥ kuśalī pāṇḍuputrobhūyaś cāto yac ca te gre mano bhūtc nirṇiktadharmārthakaro manasvībahuśruto dṛṣṭimāñ śīlavāṃś caa paraṃ dharmāt pāṇḍavasyānṛśaṃsyaṃdharmaḥ paro vittacayān mato syac sukhapriye dharmahīne na pārthonurudhyate bhārata tasya viddhid akurvataḥ sidhyati cāpi sarvaṃd tasmād āhuḥ puruṣaṃ karmaṇo nyata paraprayuktaḥ puruṣo viceṣṭatesūtraprotā dārumayīva yoṣāc imaṃ dṛṣṭvā niyamaṃ pāṇḍavasyamanye paraṃ karma daivaṃ manuṣyāta imaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā tava karmadoṣaṃpādodarkaṃ ghoram avarṇarūpamc yāvan naraḥ kāmayate tikālyaṃtāvan naro yaṃ labhate praśaṃsāma ajātaśatrus tu vihāya pāpaṃjīrṇāṃ tvacaṃ sarpa ivāsamarthāmc virocate hāryavṛttena dhīroyudhiṣṭhiras tvayi pāpaṃ visṛjyaa aṅgātmanaḥ karma nibodha rājandharmārthayuktād āryavṛttād apetamc upakrośaṃ ceha gato si rājannoheś ca pāpaṃ prasajed amutraa sa tvam arthaṃ saṃśayitaṃ vinā tairāśaṃsase putravaśānugo dyac adharmaśabdaś ca mahān pṛthivyāṃnedaṃ karma tvatsamaṃ bhāratāgryaa hīnaprajño dauṣkuleyo nṛśaṃsodīrghavairī kṣatravidyāsv adhīraḥc evaṃdharmā nāpadaḥ saṃtitīrṣeddhīnavīryo yaś ca bhaved aśiṣṭaḥa kule jāto dharmavān yo yaśasvībahuśrutaḥ sukhajīvī yatātmāc dharmārthayor grathitayor bibhartinānyatra diṣṭasya vaśād upaitia kathaṃ hi mantrāgryadharo manīṣīdharmārthayor āpadi saṃpraṇetāc evaṃyuktaḥ sarvamantrair ahīnoanānṛśaṃsyaṃ karma kuryād amūḍhaḥa tavāpīme mantravidaḥ sametyasamāsate karmasu nityayuktāḥc teṣām ayaṃ balavān niścayaś cakurukṣayārthe nirayo vyapādia akālikaṃ kuravo nābhaviṣyanpāpena cet pāpam ajātaśatruḥc icchej jātu tvayi pāpaṃ visṛjyanindā ceyaṃ tava loke bhaviṣyata kim anyatra viṣayād īśvarāṇāṃyatra pārthaḥ paralokaṃ dadarśac atyakrāmat sa tathā saṃmataḥ syānna saṃśayo nāsti manuṣyakāraḥa etān guṇān karmakṛtān avekṣyabhāvābhāvau vartamānāv anityauc balir hi rājā pāram avindamānonānyat kālāt kāraṇaṃ tatra menea cakṣuḥ śrotre nāsikā tvak ca jihvājñānasyaitāny āyatanāni jantoḥc tāni prītāny eva tṛṣṇākṣayāntetāny avyatho duḥkhahīnaḥ praṇudyāta na tv eva manye puruṣasya karmasaṃvartate suprayuktaṃ yathāvatc mātuḥ pituḥ karmaṇābhiprasūtaḥsaṃvardhate vidhivad bhojanenaa priyāpriye sukhaduḥkhe ca rājannindāpraśaṃse ca bhajeta enamc paras tv enaṃ garhayate parādhepraśaṃsate sādhuvṛttaṃ tam evaa sa tvā garhe bhāratānāṃ virodhādanto nūnaṃ bhavitāyaṃ prajānāmc no ced idaṃ tava karmāparādhātkurūn dahet kṛṣṇavartmeva kakṣama tvam evaiko jātaputreṣu rājanvaśaṃ gantā sarvaloke narendrac kāmātmanāṃ ślāghase dyūtakālenānyac chamāt paśya vipākam asyaa anāptānāṃ pragrahāt tvaṃ narendratathāptānāṃ nigrahāc caiva rājanc bhūmiṃ sphītāṃ durbalatvād anantāṃna śaktas tvaṃ rakṣituṃ kauraveyaa anujñāto rathavegāvadhūtaḥśrānto nipadye śayanaṃ nṛsiṃhac prātaḥ śrotāraḥ kuravaḥ sabhāyāmajātaśatror vacanaṃ sametāḥd dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācad anujñāto syāvasathaṃ paraihid prapadyasva śayanaṃ sūtaputrad prātaḥ śrotāraḥ kuravaḥ sabhāyāmd ajātaśatror vacanaṃ tvayoktam vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa dvāḥsthaṃ prāha mahāprājño dhṛtarāṣṭro mahīpatiḥc viduraṃ draṣṭum icchāmi tam ihānaya mācirama prahito dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa dūtaḥ kṣattāram abravītc īśvaras tvāṃ mahārājo mahāprājña didṛkṣatia evam uktas tu viduraḥ prāpya rājaniveśanamc abravīd dhṛtarāṣṭrāya dvāḥstha māṃ prativedaya dvāḥstha uvācaa viduro yam anuprāpto rājendra tava śāsanātc draṣṭum icchati te pādau kiṃ karotu praśādhi mām dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa praveśaya mahāprājñaṃ viduraṃ dīrghadarśinamc ahaṃ hi vidurasyāsya nākālyo jātu darśane dvāḥstha uvācaa praviśāntaḥpuraṃ kṣattar mahārājasya dhīmataḥc na hi te darśane kālyo jātu rājā bravīti mām vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tataḥ praviśya viduro dhṛtarāṣṭraniveśanamc abravīt prāñjalir vākyaṃ cintayānaṃ narādhipamd evam uktaḥ praviśyātha kṣattā rājānam abravīta viduro haṃ mahāprājña saṃprāptas tava śāsanātc yadi kiṃ cana kartavyam ayam asmi praśādhi mām dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa saṃjayo vidura prāpto garhayitvā ca māṃ gataḥc ajātaśatroḥ śvo vākyaṃ sabhāmadhye sa vakṣyatia tasyādya kuruvīrasya na vijñātaṃ vaco mayāc tan me dahati gātrāṇi tad akārṣīt prajāgarama jāgrato dahyamānasya śreyo yad iha paśyasic tad brūhi tvaṃ hi nas tāta dharmārthakuśalo hy asia yataḥ prāptaḥ saṃjayaḥ pāṇḍavebhyona me yathāvan manasaḥ praśāntiḥc sarvendriyāṇy aprakṛtiṃ gatānikiṃ vakṣyatīty eva hi me dya cintād tan me brūhi vidura sarvaṃ yathāvatd sāntvaṃ tasmai sarvam ajātaśatroḥd yathā ca nas tāta hitaṃ bhavetad prājñāś ca sarve sukhino bhaveyuḥ vidura uvācaa abhiyuktaṃ balavatā durbalaṃ hīnasādhanamc hṛtasvaṃ kāminaṃ coram āviśanti prajāgarāḥa kaccid etair mahādoṣair na spṛṣṭo si narādhipac kaccin na paravitteṣu gṛdhyan viparitapyase dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa śrotum icchāmi te dharmyaṃ paraṃ naiḥśreyasaṃ vacaḥc asmin rājarṣivaṃśe hi tvam ekaḥ prājñasaṃmataḥ vidura uvāca rājā lakṣaṇasaṃpannas trailokyasyāpi yo bhavet preṣyas te preṣitaś caiva dhṛtarāṣṭra yudhiṣṭhiraḥ viparītataraś ca tvaṃ bhāgadheyena saṃmataḥ arciṣā prajñayā caiva dharmātmā dharmakovidaḥ ānṛśaṃsyād anukrośād dharmāt satyaparākramāt gurutvaṃ tvayi saṃprekṣya bahūn kleśāṃs titikṣate duryodhane saubaleye karṇe duḥśāsane tathā eteṣv aiśvaryam ādhāya kathaṃ tvaṃ bhūtim icchasi ātmajñānaṃ samārambhas titikṣā dharmanityatā vāksaṃyamaś ca dānaṃ ca naiteṣv etāni kṛtsnaśaḥ ekasmād vṛkṣād yajñapātrāṇi rājan sruk ca droṇī voḍhanī pīḍanī ca etad rājan bruvato me nibodha ekasmāt puruṣāj jāyate sac ca sac caa niṣevate praśastāni ninditāni na sevatec anāstikaḥ śraddadhāna etat paṇḍitalakṣaṇama krodho harṣaś ca darpaś ca hrīstambho mānyamānitāc yam arthān nāpakarṣanti sa vai paṇḍita ucyated yo nyathā santam ātmānam anyathā pratipadyated kitavena kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ caureṇātmāpahāriṇāa yasya kṛtyaṃ na jānanti mantraṃ vā mantritaṃ parec kṛtam evāsya jānanti sa vai paṇḍita ucyatea yasya kṛtyaṃ na vighnanti śītam uṣṇaṃ bhayaṃ ratiḥc samṛddhir asamṛddhir vā sa vai paṇḍita ucyatea yasya saṃsāriṇī prajñā dharmārthāv anuvartatec kāmād arthaṃ vṛṇīte yaḥ sa vai paṇḍita ucyated kāmād arthaṃ vṛṇīte yo mokṣād arthaṃ sa vindatid rājanītiṃ samīkṣyātha sa vai paṇḍita ucyatea yathāśakti cikīrṣanti yathāśakti ca kurvatec na kiṃ cid avamanyante paṇḍitā bharatarṣabhaa kṣipraṃ vijānāti ciraṃ śṛṇotivijñāya cārthaṃ bhajate na kāmātc nāsaṃpṛṣṭo vyupayuṅkte parārthetat prajñānaṃ prathamaṃ paṇḍitasyaa nāprāpyam abhivāñchanti naṣṭaṃ necchanti śocitumc āpatsu ca na muhyanti narāḥ paṇḍitabuddhayaḥa niścitya yaḥ prakramate nāntar vasati karmaṇaḥc avandhyakālo vaśyātmā sa vai paṇḍita ucyatea āryakarmaṇi rajyante bhūtikarmāṇi kurvatec hitaṃ ca nābhyasūyanti paṇḍitā bharatarṣabhaa na hṛṣyaty ātmasaṃmāne nāvamānena tapyatec gāṅgo hrada ivākṣobhyo yaḥ sa paṇḍita ucyatea tattvajñaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ yogajñaḥ sarvakarmaṇāmc upāyajño manuṣyāṇāṃ naraḥ paṇḍita ucyatea pravṛttavāk citrakatha ūhavān pratibhānavānc āśu granthasya vaktā ca sa vai paṇḍita ucyatea śrutaṃ prajñānugaṃ yasya prajñā caiva śrutānugāc asaṃbhinnāryamaryādaḥ paṇḍitākhyāṃ labheta saḥa aśrutaś ca samunnaddho daridraś ca mahāmanāḥc arthāṃś cākarmaṇā prepsur mūḍha ity ucyate budhaiḥa svam arthaṃ yaḥ parityajya parārtham anutiṣṭhatic mithyā carati mitrārthe yaś ca mūḍhaḥ sa ucyated yaḥ prāpya mānuṣaṃ janma mokṣadvāram apāvṛtamd gṛheṣu sajjate mūḍhas tam ārūḍhacyutaṃ viduḥa akāmān kāmayati yaḥ kāmayānān paridviṣanc balavantaṃ ca yo dveṣṭi tam āhur mūḍhacetasama amitraṃ kurute mitraṃ mitraṃ dveṣṭi hinasti cac karma cārabhate duṣṭaṃ tam āhur mūḍhacetasama saṃsārayati kṛtyāni sarvatra vicikitsatec ciraṃ karoti kṣiprārthe sa mūḍho bharatarṣabhad śrāddhaṃ pitṛbhyo na dadāti daivatāni na cārcatid suhṛn mitraṃ na labhate tam āhur mūḍhalakṣaṇama anāhūtaḥ praviśati apṛṣṭo bahu bhāṣatec viśvasaty apramatteṣu mūḍhacetā narādhamaḥa paraṃ kṣipati doṣeṇa vartamānaḥ svayaṃ tathāc yaś ca krudhyaty anīśaḥ san sa ca mūḍhatamo naraḥa ātmano balam ajñāya dharmārthaparivarjitamc alabhyam icchan naiṣkarmyān mūḍhabuddhir ihocyatea aśiṣyaṃ śāsti yo rājan yaś ca śūnyam upāsatec kadaryaṃ bhajate yaś ca tam āhur mūḍhacetasama arthaṃ mahāntam āsādya vidyām aiśvaryam eva vāc vicaraty asamunnaddho yaḥ sa paṇḍita ucyatea ekaḥ saṃpannam aśnāti vas te vāsaś ca śobhanamc yo saṃvibhajya bhṛtyebhyaḥ ko nṛśaṃsataras tataḥa ekaḥ pāpāni kurute phalaṃ bhuṅkte mahājanaḥc bhoktāro vipramucyante kartā doṣeṇa lipyatea ekaṃ hanyān na vā hanyād iṣur mukto dhanuṣmatāc buddhir buddhimatotsṛṣṭā hanyād rāṣṭraṃ sarājakama ekayā dve viniścitya trīṃś caturbhir vaśe kuruc pañca jitvā viditvā ṣaṭ sapta hitvā sukhī bhavaa ekaṃ viṣaraso hanti śastreṇaikaś ca vadhyatec sarāṣṭraṃ saprajaṃ hanti rājānaṃ mantravisravaḥa ekaḥ svādu na bhuñjīta ekaś cārthān na cintayetc eko na gacched adhvānaṃ naikaḥ supteṣu jāgṛyāta ekam evādvitīyaṃ tad yad rājan nāvabudhyasec satyaṃ svargasya sopānaṃ pārāvārasya naur ivaa ekaḥ kṣamāvatāṃ doṣo dvitīyo nopalabhyatec yad enaṃ kṣamayā yuktam aśaktaṃ manyate janaḥd so sya doṣo na mantavyaḥ kṣamā hi paramaṃ balamd kṣamā guṇo hy aśaktānāṃ śaktānāṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ kṣamād kṣamā vaśīkṛtir loke kṣamayā kiṃ na sādhyated śāntikhaḍgaḥ kare yasya kiṃ kariṣyati durjanaḥd atṛṇe patito vahniḥ svayam evopaśāmyatid akṣamāvān paraṃ doṣair ātmānaṃ caiva yojayeta eko dharmaḥ paraṃ śreyaḥ kṣamaikā śāntir uttamāc vidyaikā paramā dṛṣṭir ahiṃsaikā sukhāvahāa dvāv imau grasate bhūmiḥ sarpo bilaśayān ivac rājānaṃ cāviroddhāraṃ brāhmaṇaṃ cāpravāsinamd pṛthivyāṃ sāgarāntāyāṃ dvāv imau puruṣādhamaua dve karmaṇī naraḥ kurvann asmiṃl loke virocatec abruvan paruṣaṃ kiṃ cid asato nārthayaṃs tathāa dvāv imau puruṣavyāghra parapratyayakāriṇauc striyaḥ kāmitakāminyo lokaḥ pūjitapūjakaḥa dvāv imau kaṇṭakau tīkṣṇau śarīrapariśoṣaṇauc yaś cādhanaḥ kāmayate yaś ca kupyaty anīśvaraḥd dvāv imau puruṣau loke sūryamaṇḍalabhedinaud parivrāḍyogayuktaś ca raṇe cābhimukho hataḥd dvāv imau na virājete viparītena karmaṇād gṛhasthaś ca nirārambhaḥ kāryavāṃś caiva bhikṣukaḥa dvāv imau puruṣau rājan svargasyopari tiṣṭhataḥc prabhuś ca kṣamayā yukto daridraś ca pradānavāna nyāyāgatasya dravyasya boddhavyau dvāv atikramauc apātre pratipattiś ca pātre cāpratipādanamd dvāv ambhasi niveṣṭavyau gale baddhvā dṛḍhāṃ śilāmd dhanavantam adātāraṃ daridraṃ cātapasvinama trayo nyāyā manuṣyāṇāṃ śrūyante bharatarṣabhac kanīyān madhyamaḥ śreṣṭha iti vedavido viduḥa trividhāḥ puruṣā rājann uttamādhamamadhyamāḥc niyojayed yathāvat tāṃs trividheṣv eva karmasua traya evādhanā rājan bhāryā dāsas tathā sutaḥc yat te samadhigacchanti yasya te tasya tad dhanamd haraṇaṃ ca parasvānāṃ paradārābhimarśanamd suhṛdaś ca parityāgas trayo doṣāḥ kṣayāvahāḥd trividhaṃ narakasyedaṃ dvāraṃ nāśanam ātmanaḥd kāmaḥ krodhas tathā lobhas tasmād etat trayaṃ tyajetd bhaktaṃ ca bhajamānaṃ ca tavāsmīti ca vādinamd trīn etāñ śaraṇaṃ prāptān viṣame pi na saṃtyajetd varapradānaṃ rājyaṃ ca putrajanma ca bhāratad śatroś ca mokṣaṇaṃ kṛcchrāt trīṇi caikaṃ ca tatsamama catvāri rājñā tu mahābalenavarjyāny āhuḥ paṇḍitas tāni vidyātc alpaprajñaiḥ saha mantraṃ na kuryānna dīrghasūtrair alasaiś cāraṇaiś caa catvāri te tāta gṛhe vasantuśriyābhijuṣṭasya gṛhasthadharmec vṛddho jñātir avasannaḥ kulīnaḥsakhā daridro bhaginī cānapatyāa catvāry āha mahārāja sadyaskāni bṛhaspatiḥc pṛcchate tridaśendrāya tānīmāni nibodha mea devatānāṃ ca saṃkalpam anubhāvaṃ ca dhīmatāmc vinayaṃ kṛtavidyānāṃ vināśaṃ pāpakarmaṇāmd catvāri karmāṇy abhayaṃkarāṇid bhayaṃ prayacchanty ayathākṛtānid mānāgnihotram uta mānamaunaṃd mānenādhītam uta mānayajñaḥa pañcāgnayo manuṣyeṇa paricaryāḥ prayatnataḥc pitā mātāgnir ātmā ca guruś ca bharatarṣabhaa pañcaiva pūjayaṃl loke yaśaḥ prāpnoti kevalamc devān pitṝn manuṣyāṃś ca bhikṣūn atithipañcamāna pañca tvānugamiṣyanti yatra yatra gamiṣyasic mitrāṇy amitrā madhyasthā upajīvyopajīvinaḥa pañcendriyasya martyasya chidraṃ ced ekam indriyamc tato sya sravati prajñā dṛteḥ pādād ivodakama ṣaḍ doṣāḥ puruṣeṇeha hātavyā bhūtim icchatāc nidrā tandrī bhayaṃ krodha ālasyaṃ dīrghasūtratāa ṣaḍ imān puruṣo jahyād bhinnāṃ nāvam ivārṇavec apravaktāram ācāryam anadhīyānam ṛtvijama arakṣitāraṃ rājānaṃ bhāryāṃ cāpriyavādinīmc grāmakāmaṃ ca gopālaṃ vanakāmaṃ ca nāpitama ṣaḍ eva tu guṇāḥ puṃsā na hātavyāḥ kadā canac satyaṃ dānam anālasyam anasūyā kṣamā dhṛtiḥd ṣaḍ imāni vinaśyanti muhūrtam anavekṣaṇātd gāvaḥ sevā kṛṣir bhāryā vidyā vṛṣalasaṃgatiḥd ṣaḍ ete hy avamanyante nityaṃ pūrvopakāriṇamd ācāryaṃ śikṣitāḥ śiṣyāḥ kṛtadārāś ca mātaramd nārīṃ vigatakāmās tu kṛtārthāś ca prayojanamd nāvaṃ nistīrṇakāntārā āturāś ca cikitsakamd ārogyam ānṛṇyam avipravāsaḥd sadbhir manuṣyaiḥ saha saṃprayogaḥd svapratyayā vṛttir abhītavāsaḥd ṣaḍ jīvalokasya sukhāni rājand īrṣur ghṛṇī na saṃtuṣṭaḥ krodhano nityaśaṅkitaḥd parabhāgyopajīvī ca ṣaḍ ete nityaduḥkhitāḥd arthāgamo nityam arogitā cad priyā ca bhāryā priyavādinī cad vaśyaś ca putro rthakarī ca vidyād ṣaḍ jīvalokasya sukhāni rājana ṣaṇṇām ātmani nityānām aiśvaryaṃ yo dhigacchatic na sa pāpaiḥ kuto narthair yujyate vijitendriyaḥa ṣaḍ ime ṣaṭsu jīvanti saptamo nopalabhyatec corāḥ pramatte jīvanti vyādhiteṣu cikitsakāḥa pramadāḥ kāmayāneṣu yajamāneṣu yājakāḥc rājā vivadamāneṣu nityaṃ mūrkheṣu paṇḍitāḥa sapta doṣāḥ sadā rājñā hātavyā vyasanodayāḥc prāyaśo yair vinaśyanti kṛtamūlāś ca pārthivāḥa striyo kṣā mṛgayā pānaṃ vākpāruṣyaṃ ca pañcamamc mahac ca daṇḍapāruṣyam arthadūṣaṇam eva caa aṣṭau pūrvanimittāni narasya vinaśiṣyataḥc brāhmaṇān prathamaṃ dveṣṭi brāhmaṇaiś ca virudhyatea brāhmaṇasvāni cādatte brāhmaṇāṃś ca jighāṃsatic ramate nindayā caiṣāṃ praśaṃsāṃ nābhinandatia naitān smarati kṛtyeṣu yācitaś cābhyasūyatib yasyaitāni nimittāni tasyāsan naḥ parābhavaḥc etān doṣān naraḥ prājño buddhyā buddhvā vivarjayeta aṣṭāv imāni harṣasya navanītāni bhāratac vartamānāni dṛśyante tāny eva susukhāny apia samāgamaś ca sakhibhir mahāṃś caiva dhanāgamaḥc putreṇa ca pariṣvaṅgaḥ saṃnipātaś ca maithunea samaye ca priyālāpaḥ svayūtheṣu ca saṃnatiḥc abhipretasya lābhaś ca pūjā ca janasaṃsadia navadvāram idaṃ veśma tristhūṇaṃ pañcasākṣikamc kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitaṃ vidvān yo veda sa paraḥ kaviḥa daśa dharmaṃ na jānanti dhṛtarāṣṭra nibodha tānc mattaḥ pramatta unmattaḥ śrāntaḥ kruddho bubhukṣitaḥa tvaramāṇaś ca bhīruś ca lubdhaḥ kāmī ca te daśac tasmād eteṣu bhāveṣu na prasajjeta paṇḍitaḥa atraivodāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc putrārtham asurendreṇa gītaṃ caiva sudhanvanāa yaḥ kāmamanyū prajahāti rājāpātre pratiṣṭhāpayate dhanaṃ cac viśeṣavic chrutavān kṣiprakārītaṃ sarvalokaḥ kurute pramāṇama jānāti viśvāsayituṃ manuṣyānvijñātadoṣeṣu dadhāti daṇḍamc jānāti mātrāṃ ca tathā kṣamāṃ cataṃ tādṛśaṃ śrīr juṣate samagrāa sudurbalaṃ nāvajānāti kaṃ cidyukto ripuṃ sevate buddhipūrvamc na vigrahaṃ rocayate balasthaiḥkāle ca yo vikramate sa dhīraḥa prāpyāpadaṃ na vyathate kadā cidudyogam anvicchati cāpramattaḥc duḥkhaṃ ca kāle sahate jitātmādhuraṃdharas tasya jitāḥ sapatnāḥa anarthakaṃ vipravāsaṃ gṛhebhyaḥpāpaiḥ saṃdhiṃ paradārābhimarśamc dambhaṃ stainyaṃ paiśunaṃ madyapānaṃna sevate yaḥ sa sukhī sadaivaa na saṃrambheṇārabhate rthavargamākāritaḥ śaṃsati tathyam evac na mātrārthe rocayate vivādaṃnāpūjitaḥ kupyati cāpy amūḍhaḥa na yo bhyasūyaty anukampate cana durbalaḥ prātibhāvyaṃ karotic nātyāha kiṃ cit kṣamate vivādaṃsarvatra tādṛg labhate praśaṃsāma yo noddhataṃ kurute jātu veṣaṃna pauruṣeṇāpi vikatthate nyānc na mūrcchitaḥ kaṭukāny āha kiṃ citpriyaṃ sadā taṃ kurute jano pia na vairam uddīpayati praśāntaṃna darpam ārohati nāstam etic na durgato smīti karoti manyuṃtam āryaśīlaṃ param āhur agryama na sve sukhe vai kurute praharṣaṃnānyasya duḥkhe bhavati pratītaḥc dattvā na paścāt kurute nutāpaṃna katthate satpuruṣāryaśīlaḥa deśācārān samayāñ jātidharmānbubhūṣate yas tu parāvarajñaḥc sa tatra tatrādhigataḥ sadaivamahājanasyādhipatyaṃ karotia dambhaṃ mohaṃ matsaraṃ pāpakṛtyaṃrājadviṣṭaṃ paiśunaṃ pūgavairamc mattonmattair durjanaiś cāpi vādaṃyaḥ prajñāvān varjayet sa pradhānaḥa damaṃ śaucaṃ daivataṃ maṅgalāniprāyaścittaṃ vividhāṃl lokavādānc etāni yaḥ kurute naityakānitasyotthānaṃ devatā rādhayantia samair vivāhaṃ kurute na hīnaiḥsamaiḥ sakhyaṃ vyavahāraṃ kathāś cac guṇair viśiṣṭāṃś ca purodadhātivipaścitas tasya nayāḥ sunītāḥa mitaṃ bhuṅkte saṃvibhajyāśritebhyomitaṃ svapity amitaṃ karma kṛtvāc dadāty amitreṣv api yācitaḥ saṃstam ātmavantaṃ prajahaty anarthāḥa cikīrṣitaṃ viprakṛtaṃ ca yasyanānye janāḥ karma jānanti kiṃ citc mantre gupte samyag anuṣṭhite casvalpo nāsya vyathate kaś cid arthaḥa yaḥ sarvabhūtapraśame niviṣṭaḥsatyo mṛdur dānakṛc chuddhabhāvaḥc atīva saṃjñāyate jñātimadhyemahāmaṇir jātya iva prasannaḥa ya ātmanāpatrapate bhṛśaṃ naraḥsa sarvalokasya gurur bhavaty utac anantatejāḥ sumanāḥ samāhitaḥsvatejasā sūrya ivāvabhāsatea vane jātāḥ śāpadagdhasya rājñaḥpāṇḍoḥ putrāḥ pañca pañcendrakalpāḥc tvayaiva bālā vardhitāḥ śikṣitāś catavādeśaṃ pālayanty āmbikeyaa pradāyaiṣām ucitaṃ tāta rājyaṃsukhī putraiḥ sahito modamānaḥc na devānāṃ nāpi ca mānuṣāṇāṃbhaviṣyasi tvaṃ tarkaṇīyo narendra dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa jāgrato dahyamānasya yat kāryam anupaśyasic tad brūhi tvaṃ hi nas tāta dharmārthakuśalaḥ śuciḥa tvaṃ māṃ yathāvad vidura praśādhiprajñāpūrvaṃ sarvam ajātaśatroḥc yan manyase pathyam adīnasattvaśreyaskaraṃ brūhi tad vai kurūṇāma pāpāśaṅkī pāpam evānupaśyanpṛcchāmi tvāṃ vyākulenātmanāhamc kave tan me brūhi sarvaṃ yathāvanmanīṣitaṃ sarvam ajātaśatroḥ vidura uvāca sulabhāḥ puruṣā rājan satataṃ priyavādinaḥ apriyasya ca pathyasya vaktā śrotā ca durlabhaḥa śubhaṃ vā yadi vā pāpaṃ dveṣyaṃ vā yadi vā priyamc apṛṣṭas tasya tad brūyād yasya necchet parābhavama tasmād vakṣyāmi te rājan bhavam icchan kurūn pratic vacaḥ śreyaskaraṃ dharmyaṃ bruvatas tan nibodha mea mithyopetāni karmāṇi sidhyeyur yāni bhāratac anupāyaprayuktāni mā sma teṣu manaḥ kṛthāḥa tathaiva yogavihitaṃ na sidhyet karma yan nṛpac upāyayuktaṃ medhāvī na tatra glapayen manaḥa anubandhān avekṣeta sānubandheṣu karmasuc saṃpradhārya ca kurvīta na vegena samācareta anubandhaṃ ca saṃprekṣya vipākāṃś caiva karmaṇāmc utthānam ātmanaś caiva dhīraḥ kurvīta vā na vāa yaḥ pramāṇaṃ na jānāti sthāne vṛddhau tathā kṣayec kośe janapade daṇḍe na sa rājye vatiṣṭhatea yas tv etāni pramāṇāni yathoktāny anupaśyatic yukto dharmārthayor jñāne sa rājyam adhigacchatia na rājyaṃ prāptam ity eva vartitavyam asāṃpratamc śriyaṃ hy avinayo hanti jarā rūpam ivottamama bhakṣyottamapraticchannaṃ matsyo baḍiśam āyasamc rūpābhipātī grasate nānubandham avekṣatea yac chakyaṃ grasituṃ grasyaṃ grastaṃ pariṇamec ca yatc hitaṃ ca pariṇāme yat tad adyaṃ bhūtim icchatāa vanaspater apakvāni phalāni pracinoti yaḥc sa nāpnoti rasaṃ tebhyo bījaṃ cāsya vinaśyatia yas tu pakvam upādatte kāle pariṇataṃ phalamc phalād rasaṃ sa labhate bījāc caiva phalaṃ punaḥa yathā madhu samādatte rakṣan puṣpāṇi ṣaṭpadaḥc tadvad arthān manuṣyebhya ādadyād avihiṃsayāa puṣpaṃ puṣpaṃ vicinvīta mūlacchedaṃ na kārayetc mālākāra ivārāme na yathāṅgārakārakaḥa kiṃ nu me syād idaṃ kṛtvā kiṃ nu me syād akurvataḥc iti karmāṇi saṃcintya kuryād vā puruṣo na vāa anārabhyā bhavanty arthāḥ ke cin nityaṃ tathāgatāḥc kṛtaḥ puruṣakāro pi bhaved yeṣu nirarthakaḥd anarthe caiva niratam arthe caiva parāṅmukhama kāṃś cid arthān naraḥ prājño laghumūlān mahāphalānc kṣipram ārabhate kartuṃ na vighnayati tādṛśāna ṛju paśyati yaḥ sarvaṃ cakṣuṣānupibann ivac āsīnam api tūṣṇīkam anurajyanti taṃ prajāḥd supuṣpitaḥ syād aphalaḥ phalitaḥ syād durāruhaḥd apakvaḥ pakvasaṃkāśo na tu śīryeta karhi cita cakṣuṣā manasā vācā karmaṇā ca caturvidhamc prasādayati lokaṃ yaḥ taṃ loko nuprasīdatia yasmāt trasyanti bhūtāni mṛgavyādhān mṛgā ivac sāgarāntām api mahīṃ labdhvā sa parihīyatea pitṛpaitāmahaṃ rājyaṃ prāptavān svena tejasāc vāyur abhram ivāsādya bhraṃśayaty anaye sthitaḥa dharmam ācarato rājñaḥ sadbhiś caritam āditaḥc vasudhā vasusaṃpūrṇā vardhate bhūtivardhanīa atha saṃtyajato dharmam adharmaṃ cānutiṣṭhataḥc pratisaṃveṣṭate bhūmir agnau carmāhitaṃ yathāa ya eva yatnaḥ kriyate pararāṣṭrāvamardanec sa eva yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ svarāṣṭraparipālanea dharmeṇa rājyaṃ vindeta dharmeṇa paripālayetc dharmamūlāṃ śriyaṃ prāpya na jahāti na hīyatea apy unmattāt pralapato bālāc ca parisarpataḥc sarvataḥ sāram ādadyād aśmabhya iva kāñcanama suvyāhṛtāni sudhiyāṃ sukṛtāni tatas tataḥc saṃcinvan dhīra āsīta śilāhārī śilaṃ yathāa gandhena gāvaḥ paśyanti vedaiḥ paśyanti brāhmaṇāḥc cāraiḥ paśyanti rājānaś cakṣurbhyām itare janāḥa bhūyāṃsaṃ labhate kleśaṃ yā gaur bhavati durduhāc atha yā suduhā rājan naiva tāṃ vinayanty apia yad ataptaṃ praṇamati na tat saṃtāpayanty apic yac ca svayaṃ nataṃ dāru na tat saṃnāmayanty apia etayopamayā dhīraḥ saṃnameta balīyasec indrāya sa praṇamate namate yo balīyasea parjanyanāthāḥ paśavo rājāno mitrabāndhavāḥc patayo bāndhavāḥ strīṇāṃ brāhmaṇā vedabāndhavāḥa satyena rakṣyate dharmo vidyā yogena rakṣyatec mṛjayā rakṣyate rūpaṃ kulaṃ vṛttena rakṣyatea mānena rakṣyate dhānyam aśvān rakṣaty anukramaḥc abhīkṣṇadarśanād gāvaḥ striyo rakṣyāḥ kucelataḥa na kulaṃ vṛttahīnasya pramāṇam iti me matiḥc antyeṣv api hi jātānāṃ vṛttam eva viśiṣyatea ya īrṣyuḥ paravitteṣu rūpe vīrye kulānvayec sukhe saubhāgyasatkāre tasya vyādhir anantakaḥa akāryakaraṇād bhītaḥ kāryāṇāṃ ca vivarjanātc akāle mantrabhedāc ca yena mādyen na tat pibeta vidyāmado dhanamadas tṛtīyo bhijano madaḥc ete madāvaliptānām eta eva satāṃ damāḥa asanto bhyarthitāḥ sadbhiḥ kiṃ cit kāryaṃ kadā canab tāvan na tasya sukṛtaṃ kiṃ cit kāryaṃ kadā canac manyante santam ātmānam asantam api viśrutama gatir ātmavatāṃ santaḥ santa eva satāṃ gatiḥc asatāṃ ca gatiḥ santo na tv asantaḥ satāṃ gatiḥa jitā sabhā vastravatā samāśā gomatā jitāc adhvā jito yānavatā sarvaṃ śīlavatā jitama śīlaṃ pradhānaṃ puruṣe tad yasyeha praṇaśyatic na tasya jīvitenārtho na dhanena na bandhubhiḥa āḍhyānāṃ māṃsaparamaṃ madhyānāṃ gorasottaramc lavaṇottaraṃ daridrāṇāṃ bhojanaṃ bharatarṣabhaa saṃpannataram evānnaṃ daridrā bhuñjate sadāc kṣut svādutāṃ janayati sā cāḍhyeṣu sudurlabhāa prāyeṇa śrīmatāṃ loke bhoktuṃ śaktir na vidyatec daridrāṇāṃ tu rājendra api kāṣṭhaṃ hi jīryated yathā yathā mahat tantraṃ vistaraś ca yathā yathād tathā tathā mahad duḥkhaṃ sukhaṃ tu na tathā tathāa avṛttir bhayam antyānāṃ madhyānāṃ maraṇād bhayamc uttamānāṃ tu martyānām avamānāt paraṃ bhayama aiśvaryamadapāpiṣṭhā madāḥ pānamadādayaḥc aiśvaryamadamatto hi nāpatitvā vibudhyatea indriyair indriyārtheṣu vartamānair anigrahaiḥc tair ayaṃ tāpyate loko nakṣatrāṇi grahair ivaa yo jitaḥ pañcavargeṇa sahajenātmakarśināc āpadas tasya vardhante śuklapakṣa ivoḍurāṭa avijitya ya ātmānam amātyān vijigīṣatec amitrān vājitāmātyaḥ so vaśaḥ parihīyatea ātmānam eva prathamaṃ deśarūpeṇa yo jayetc tato mātyān amitrāṃś ca na moghaṃ vijigīṣatea vaśyendriyaṃ jitāmātyaṃ dhṛtadaṇḍaṃ vikāriṣuc parīkṣyakāriṇaṃ dhīram atyantaṃ śrīr niṣevatea rathaḥ śarīraṃ puruṣasya rājannātmā niyantendriyāṇy asya cāśvāḥc tair apramattaḥ kuśalaḥ sadaśvairdāntaiḥ sukhaṃ yāti rathīva dhīraḥa etāny anigṛhītāni vyāpādayitum apy alamc avidheyā ivādāntā hayāḥ pathi kusārathima anartham arthataḥ paśyann arthaṃ caivāpy anarthataḥc indriyaiḥ prasṛto bālaḥ suduḥkhaṃ manyate sukhama dharmārthau yaḥ parityajya syād indriyavaśānugaḥc śrīprāṇadhanadārebhya kṣipraṃ sa parihīyatea arthānām īśvaro yaḥ syād indriyāṇām anīśvaraḥc indriyāṇām anaiśvaryād aiśvaryād bhraśyate hi saḥa ātmanātmānam anvicchen manobuddhīndriyair yataiḥc ātmaiva hy ātmano bandhur ātmaiva ripur ātmanaḥd bandhur ātmātmanas tasya yenaivātmātmanā jitaḥd sa eva niyato bandhuḥ sa eva niyato ripuḥa kṣudrākṣeṇeva jālena jhaṣāv apihitāv ubhauc kāmaś ca rājan krodhaś ca tau prajñānaṃ vilumpataḥa samavekṣyeha dharmārthau saṃbhārān yo dhigacchatic sa vai saṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraḥ satataṃ sukham edhatea yaḥ pañcābhyantarāñ śatrūn avijitya matikṣayānc jigīṣati ripūn anyān ripavo bhibhavanti tama dṛśyante hi durātmāno vadhyamānāḥ svakarmabhiḥc indriyāṇām anīśatvād rājāno rājyavibhramaiḥa asaṃtyāgāt pāpakṛtām apāpāṃstulyo daṇḍaḥ spṛśate miśrabhāvātc śuṣkeṇārdraṃ dahyate miśrabhāvāttasmāt pāpaiḥ saha saṃdhiṃ na kuryāta nijān utpatataḥ śatrūn pañca pañcaprayojanānc yo mohān na nigṛhṇāti tam āpad grasate narama anasūyārjavaṃ śaucaṃ saṃtoṣaḥ priyavāditāc damaḥ satyam anāyāso na bhavanti durātmanāma ātmajñānam anāyāsas titikṣā dharmanityatāc vāk caiva guptā dānaṃ ca naitāny antyeṣu bhārataa ākrośaparivādābhyāṃ vihiṃsanty abudhā budhānc vaktā pāpam upādatte kṣamamāṇo vimucyatea hiṃsā balam asādhūnāṃ rājñāṃ daṇḍavidhir balamc śuśrūṣā tu balaṃ strīṇāṃ kṣamā guṇavatāṃ balama vāksaṃyamo hi nṛpate suduṣkaratamo mataḥc arthavac ca vicitraṃ ca na śakyaṃ bahu bhāṣituma abhyāvahati kalyāṇaṃ vividhā vāk subhāṣitāc saiva durbhāṣitā rājann anarthāyopapadyatea saṃrohati śarair viddhaṃ vanaṃ paraśunā hatamc vācā duruktaṃ bībhatsaṃ na saṃrohati vākkṣatama karṇinālīkanārācā nirharanti śarīrataḥc vākśalyas tu na nirhartuṃ śakyo hṛdiśayo hi saḥa vāksāyakā vadanān niṣpatantiyair āhataḥ śocati rātryahānic parasya nāmarmasu te patantitān paṇḍito nāvasṛjet pareṣua yasmai devāḥ prayacchanti puruṣāya parābhavamc buddhiṃ tasyāpakarṣanti so pācīnāni paśyatia buddhau kaluṣabhūtāyāṃ vināśe pratyupasthitec anayo nayasaṃkāśo hṛdayān nāpasarpatid na devā yaṣṭim ādāya rakṣanti paśupālavatd yaṃ hi rakṣitum icchanti buddhyā saṃyojayanti tama seyaṃ buddhiḥ parītā te putrāṇāṃ tava bhāratac pāṇḍavānāṃ virodhena na cainām avabudhyasea rājā lakṣaṇasaṃpannas trailokyasyāpi yo bhavetc śiṣyas te śāsitā so stu dhṛtarāṣṭra yudhiṣṭhiraḥa atīva sarvān putrāṃs te bhāgadheyapuraskṛtaḥc tejasā prajñayā caiva yukto dharmārthatattvavita ānṛśaṃsyād anukrośād yo sau dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥc gauravāt tava rājendra bahūn kleśāṃs titikṣati dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa brūhi bhūyo mahābuddhe dharmārthasahitaṃ vacaḥc śṛṇvato nāsti me tṛptir vicitrāṇīha bhāṣase vidura uvācaa sarvatīrtheṣu vā snānaṃ sarvabhūteṣu cārjavamc ubhe ete same syātām ārjavaṃ vā viśiṣyatea ārjavaṃ pratipadyasva putreṣu satataṃ vibhoc iha kīrtiṃ parāṃ prāpya pretya svargam avāpsyasia yāvat kīrtir manuṣyasya puṇyā lokeṣu gīyatec tāvat sa puruṣavyāghra svargaloke mahīyatea atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanamc virocanasya saṃvādaṃ keśinyarthe sudhanvanād svayaṃvare sthitā kanyā keśinī nāma nāmataḥd rūpeṇāpratimā rājan viśiṣṭapatikāmyayād virocano tha daiteyas tadā tatrājagāma had prāptum icchaṃs tatas tatra daityendraṃ prāha keśinī keśiny uvācaa kiṃ brāhmaṇāḥ svic chreyāṃso ditijāḥ svid virocanac atha kena sma paryaṅkaṃ sudhanvā nādhirohati virocana uvācaa prājāpatyā hi vai śreṣṭhā vayaṃ keśini sattamāḥc asmākaṃ khalv ime sudhanvānaṃ ca māṃ caiva prātar draṣṭāsi saṃgataud atītāyāṃ ca śarvaryām udite sūryamaṇḍaled athājagāma taṃ deśaṃ sudhanvā rājasattamad virocano yatra vibho keśinyā sahitaḥ sthitaḥd sudhanvā ca samāgacchat prāhlādiṃ keśinīṃ tathād samāgataṃ dvijaṃ dṛṣṭvā keśinī bharatarṣabhad pratyutthāyāsanaṃ tasmai pādyam arghyaṃ dadau punaḥd etasminn antare tatra sudhanvā pratyadṛśyatad iti hovāca vacanaṃ virocanam anuttamam sudhanvovācaa anvālabhe hiraṇmayaṃ prāhrāde haṃ tavāsanamc ekatvam upasaṃpanno na tv āseyaṃ tvayā saha virocana uvācaa anvāharantu phalakaṃ kūrcaṃ vāpy atha vā bṛsīmb na matto hy adhiko si tvaṃ guṇato janmato pi vāc sudhanvan na tvam arho si mayā saha samāsanam sudhanvovāca pitāputrau sahāsītāṃ dvau viprau dvau ca pārthivau dvau caiva vaiśyau śūdrau ca na tv anyāv itaretaraṃa pitāpi te samāsīnam upāsītaiva mām adhaḥc bālaḥ sukhaidhito gehe na tvaṃ kiṃ cana budhyase virocana uvācaa hiraṇyaṃ ca gavāśvaṃ ca yad vittam asureṣu naḥc sudhanvan vipaṇe tena praśnaṃ pṛcchāva ye viduḥ sudhanvovācaa hiraṇyaṃ ca gavāśvaṃ ca tavaivāstu virocanac prāṇayos tu paṇaṃ kṛtvā praśnaṃ pṛcchāva ye viduḥ virocana uvācaa āvāṃ kutra gamiṣyāvaḥ prāṇayor vipaṇe kṛtec na hi deveṣv ahaṃ sthātā na manuṣyeṣu karhi cit sudhanvovācaa pitaraṃ te gamiṣyāvaḥ prāṇayor vipaṇe kṛtec putrasyāpi sa hetor hi prahrādo nānṛtaṃ vadetd vidura uvācad evaṃ kṛtapaṇau kruddhau tatrābhijagmatus tadād papracchāgamane hetuṃ ubhayor ditijas tataḥ prahrāda uvācaa imau tau saṃpradṛśyete yābhyāṃ na caritaṃ sahac āśīviṣāv iva kruddhāv ekamārgam ihāgataua kiṃ vai sahaiva carato na purā carataḥ sahab tat anṛtaṃ vadīḥd prahlādaḥd na kalmāṣo na kapilo na kṛṣṇo na ca lohitaḥd sudhanvād aṇīyān kṣuradhārāyāḥ ko dharmaṃ vaktum arhatid yad yat tattvaṃ vakṣyasi tvaṃ yadi vā nāpi vakṣyasid prahlāda praśnam anaghaṃ mūrdhnā te viphaliṣyati prahrāda uvācaa udakaṃ madhuparkaṃ cāpy ānayantu sudhanvanec brahmann abhyarcanīyo si śvetā gauḥ pīvarīkṛtā sudhanvovācaa udakaṃ madhuparkaṃ ca patha evārpitaṃ mamac prahrāda tvaṃ tu nau praśnaṃ tathyaṃ prabrūhi pṛcchatoḥd kiṃ brāhmaṇāḥ svic chreyāṃsa utāho svid virocanaḥd satyaṃ prabrūhi daityendra satyaṃ hi paramaṃ tapaḥ prahrāda uvācaa putro vānyo bhavān brahman sākṣye caiva bhavet sthitaḥc tayor vivadatoḥ praśnaṃ katham asmadvidho vadetd viduraḥd ādityena sahāyāntaṃ prahlādo haṃsam abravītd prahlādaḥd dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ mahāprājñaṃ sarvajñaṃ priyadarśanamd putravān yo bhaved brahman sākṣye cāpi bhavet sthitaḥd tayor vivadator haṃsa kathaṃ dharmaḥ pravartated sudhanvovācad gāṃ pradadyās tv aurasāya yad vānyat syāt priyaṃ dhanamd dvayor vivadatos tathyaṃ vācyaṃ ca matimaṃs tvayāa atha yo naiva prabrūyāt satyaṃ vā yadi vānṛtamc etat sudhanvan pṛcchāmi durvivaktā sma kiṃ vasetd haṃsaḥd pṛṣṭo dharmaṃ na vibrūyād gokarṇaśithilaṃ carand dharmād bhraśyati rājaṃs tu nāsya loko sti na prajāḥd dharma etān saṃrujati yathā nady anukūlajānd ye dharmam anupaśyantas tūṣṇīṃ dhyāyanta āsated śreṣṭho rdhaṃ tu haret tatra bhavet pādaś ca kartarid pādas teṣu sabhāsatsu yatra nindyo na nindyated anenā bhavati śreṣṭho mucyante ca sabhāsadaḥd kartāram eno gacchec ca nindyo yatra hi nindyated prahlādaḥd mohād vā caiva kāmād vā mithyāvādaṃ yadi bruvand dhṛtarāṣṭra tvāṃ pṛcchāmi durvivaktā tu kāṃ vaset sudhanvovācaa yāṃ rātrim adhivinnā strī yāṃ caivākṣaparājitaḥc yāṃ ca bhārābhitaptāṅgo durvivaktā sma tāṃ vaseta nagare pratiruddhaḥ san bahirdvāre bubhukṣitaḥc amitrān bhūyasaḥ paśyan durvivaktā sma tāṃ vasetd yāṃ ca rātrim abhidrugdho yāṃ ca mitre priye mṛted sarvasvena ca yo hīno durvivaktā tu tāṃ vaseta pañca paśvanṛte hanti daśa hanti gavānṛtec śatam aśvānṛte hanti sahasraṃ puruṣānṛtea hanti jātān ajātāṃś ca hiraṇyārthe nṛtaṃ vadanc sarvaṃ bhūmyanṛte hanti mā sma bhūmyanṛtaṃ vadīḥ prahrāda uvācaa mattaḥ śreyān aṅgirā vai sudhanvā bhūmyarthe nānṛtaṃ vaktum arhasic mā gamaḥ sasutāmātyo tyayaṃ putrān anubhramana na devā yaṣṭim ādāya rakṣanti paśupālavatc yaṃ tu rakṣitum icchanti buddhyā saṃvibhajanti tama yathā yathā hi puruṣaḥ kalyāṇe kurute manaḥc tathā tathāsya sarvārthāḥ sidhyante nātra saṃśayaḥa na chandāṃsi vṛjināt tārayantimāyāvinaṃ māyayā vartamānamc nīḍaṃ śakuntā iva jātapakṣāśchandāṃsy enaṃ prajahaty antakālea kuṇḍāśī somavikrayīc parvakāraś ca sūcī ca mitradhruk pāradārikaḥa bhrūṇahā gurutalpī ca yaś ca syāt pānapo dvijaḥc atitīkṣṇaś ca kākaś ca nāstiko vedanindakaḥa sruvapragrahaṇo vrātyaḥ kīnāśaś api sevyated uttaras tu caturvargo nāmahātmasu tiṣṭhatia na sā sabhā yatra na santi vṛddhāna te vṛddhā ye na vadanti dharmamc nāsau dharmo yatra na satyam astina tat satyaṃ yac chalenānuviddhama śreṣṭhaḥ pādaṃ haret tatra bhavet pādaś ca kartarid pādas teṣu sabhāsatsu yatra nindyo na nindyated anenāḥ śreṣṭho bhavati pramucyante sabhāsadaḥd eno gacchati kartāraṃ nindārho yatra nindyatea pāpaṃ kurvan pāpakīrtiḥ pāpam evāśnute phalamc puṇyaṃ kurvan puṇyakīrtiḥ puṇyam evāśnute phalamd tasmāt pāpaṃ na kurvīta puruṣaḥ śaṃsitavrataḥa pāpaṃ prajñāṃ nāśayati kriyamāṇaṃ punaḥ punaḥc naṣṭaprajñaḥ pāpam eva nityam ārabhate naraḥa puṇyaṃ prajñāṃ vardhayati kriyamāṇaṃ punaḥ punaḥc vṛddhaprajñaḥ puṇyam eva nityam ārabhate naraḥd puṇyaṃ kurvan puṇyakīrtiḥ puṇyaṃ sthānaṃ sma gacchatid tasmāt puṇyaṃ kumārīḥ pratipādya sarvāaraṇyasaṃstho munivad bubhūṣeta hitaṃ yat sarvabhūtānām ātmanaś ca sukhāvahamc tat kuryād īśvaro hy etan mūlaṃ dharmārthasiddhayea buddhiḥ prabhāvas tejaś ca sattvam utthānam eva cac vyavasāyaś ca yasya syāt tasyāvṛttibhayaṃ kutaḥa paśya doṣān pāṇḍavair vigrahe tvaṃyatra vyatherann api devāḥ saśakrāḥc putrair vairaṃ nityam udvignavāsoyaśaḥpraṇāśo dviṣatāṃ ca harṣaḥa bhīṣmasya kopas tava cendrakalpadroṇasya rājñaś ca yudhiṣṭhirasyac utsādayel lokam imaṃ pravṛddhaḥśveto grahas tiryag ivāpatan khea tava putraśataṃ caiva karṇaḥ pañca ca pāṇḍavāḥc pṛthivīm anuśāseyur akhilāṃ sāgarāmbarāma dhārtarāṣṭrā vanaṃ rājan vyāghrāḥ pāṇḍusutā matāḥc mā vanaṃ chindhi savyāghraṃ mā vyāghrān nīnaśo vanāta na syād vanam ṛte vyāghrān vyāghrā na syur ṛte vanamc vanaṃ hi rakṣyate vyāghrair vyāghrān rakṣati kānanama na tathecchanty akalyāṇāḥ pareṣāṃ vedituṃ guṇānc yathaiṣāṃ jñātum icchanti nairguṇyaṃ pāpacetasaḥa arthasiddhiṃ parām icchan dharmam evāditaś caretc na hi dharmād apaity arthaḥ svargalokād ivāmṛtama yasyātmā virataḥ pāpāt kalyāṇe ca niveśitaḥc tena sarvam idaṃ buddhaṃ prakṛtir vikṛtiś ca yāa yo dharmam arthaṃ kāmaṃ ca yathākālaṃ niṣevatec dharmārthakāmasaṃyogaṃ so mutreha ca vindatia saṃniyacchati yo vegam utthitaṃ krodhaharṣayoḥc sa śriyo bhājanaṃ rājan yaś cāpatsu na muhyatia balaṃ pañcavidhaṃ nityaṃ puruṣāṇāṃ nibodha mec yat tu bāhubalaṃ nāma kaniṣṭhaṃ balam ucyatea amātyalābho bhadraṃ te dvitīyaṃ balam ucyatec dhanalābhas tṛtīyaṃ tu balam āhur jigīṣavaḥa yat tv asya sahajaṃ rājan pitṛpaitāmahaṃ balamc abhijātabalaṃ nāma tac caturthaṃ balaṃ smṛtama yena tv etāni sarvāṇi saṃgṛhītāni bhāratac yad balānāṃ balaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tat prajñābalam ucyatea mahate yo pakārāya narasya prabhaven naraḥc tena vairaṃ samāsajya dūrastho smīti nāśvaseta strīṣu rājasu sarpeṣu svādhyāye śatruseviṣuc bhoge cāyuṣi viśvāsaṃ kaḥ prājñaḥ kartum arhatia prajñāśareṇābhihatasya jantościkitsakāḥ santi na cauṣadhānic na homamantrā na ca maṅgalāninātharvaṇā nāpy agadāḥ susiddhāḥa sarpaś cāgniś ca siṃhaś ca kulaputraś ca bhāratac nāvajñeyā manuṣyeṇa sarve te hy atitejasaḥa agnis tejo mahal loke gūḍhas tiṣṭhati dāruṣuc na copayuṅkte tad dāru yāvan no dīpyate paraiḥa sa eva khalu dārubhyo yadā nirmathya dīpyatec tadā tac ca vanaṃ cānyan nirdahaty āśu tejasāa evam eva kule jātāḥ pāvakopamatejasaḥc kṣamāvanto nirākārāḥ kāṣṭhe gnir iva śeratea latādharmā tvaṃ vanena vidura uvācaa ūrdhvaṃ prāṇā hy utkrāmanti yūnaḥ sthavira āyatic pratyutthānābhivādābhyāṃ punas tān pratipadyatea pīṭhaṃ dattvā sādhave bhyāgatāyaānīyāpaḥ parinirṇijya pādauc sukhaṃ pṛṣṭvā prativedyātmasaṃsthaṃtato dadyād annam avekṣya dhīraḥa yasyodakaṃ madhuparkaṃ ca gāṃ canamantravit pratigṛhṇāti gehec lobhād bhayād arthakārpaṇyato vātasyānarthaṃ jīvitam āhur āryāḥa cikitsakaḥ śalyakartāvakīrṇīstenaḥ krūro madyapo bhrūṇahā cac senājīvī śrutivikrāyakaś cabhṛśaṃ priyo py atithir nodakārhaḥa avikreyaṃ lavaṇaṃ pakvam annaṃdadhi kṣīraṃ madhu tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ cac tilā māṃsaṃ mūlaphalāni śākaṃraktaṃ vāsaḥ sarvagandhā guḍaś caa aroṣaṇo yaḥ samaloṣṭakāñcanaḥprahīṇaśoko gatasaṃdhivigrahaḥc nindāpraśaṃsoparataḥ priyāpriyecarann udāsīnavad eṣa bhikṣukaḥa nīvāramūleṅgudaśākavṛttiḥsusaṃyatātmāgnikāryeṣv acodyaḥc vane vasann atithiṣv apramattodhuraṃdharaḥ puṇyakṛd eṣa tāpasaḥa apakṛtvā buddhimato dūrastho smīti nāśvasetc dīrghau buddhimato bāhū yābhyāṃ vaśago bhaveta pūjanīyā mahābhāgāḥ puṇyāś ca gṛhadīptayaḥc striyaḥ śriyo gṛhasyoktās tasmād rakṣyā viśeṣataḥa pitur antaḥpuraṃ dadyān mātur dadyān mahānasamc goṣu cātmasamaṃ dadyāt svayam eva kṛṣiṃ vrajete bhṛtyair vaṇijyācāraṃ ca putraiḥ seveta brāhmaṇāna adbhyo gnir brahmataḥ kṣatram aśmano loham utthitamc teṣāṃ sarvatragaṃ tejaḥ svāsu yoniṣu śāmyatia nityaṃ santaḥ kule jātāḥ pāvakopamatejasaḥc kṣamāvanto nirākārāḥ kāṣṭhe gnir iva śeratea yasya mantraṃ na jānanti bāhyāś cābhyantarāś ca yec sa rājā sarvataścakṣuś ciram aiśvaryam aśnutea kariṣyan na prabhāṣeta kṛtāny eva ca darśayetc dharmakāmārthakāryāṇi tathā mantro na bhidyatea giripṛṣṭham upāruhya prāsādaṃ vā rahogataḥc araṇye niḥśalāke vā tatra mantro vidhīyatea nāsuhṛt paramaṃ mantraṃ bhāratārhati veditumc apaṇḍito vāpi suhṛt paṇḍito vāpy anātmavānd nāparīkṣya mahīpālaḥ kuryāt sacivam ātmanaḥe amātye hy arthalipsā ca mantrarakṣaṇam eva caa kṛtāni sarvakāryāṇi yasya vā pārṣadā viduḥb dharme cārthe ca kāme ca sa rājā rājasattamaḥc gūḍhamantrasya nṛpates tasya siddhir asaṃśayama apraśastāni karmāṇi yo mohād anutiṣṭhatic sa teṣāṃ viparibhraṃśe bhraśyate jīvitād apia karmaṇāṃ tu praśastānām anuṣṭhānaṃ sukhāvahamc teṣām evānanuṣṭhānaṃ paścāttāpakaraṃ mahatd anadhītya yathā vedān na vipraḥ śrāddham arhatid evam aśrutaṣāḍguṇyo na mantraṃ śrotum arhatia sthānavṛddhikṣayajñasya ṣāḍguṇyaviditātmanaḥc anavajñātaśīlasya svādhīnā pṛthivī nṛpaa amoghakrodhaharṣasya svayaṃ kṛtyānvavekṣiṇaḥc ātmapratyayakośasya vasudheyaṃ vasuṃdharāa nāmamātreṇa tuṣyeta chatreṇa ca mahīpatiḥc bhṛtyebhyo visṛjed arthān naikaḥ sarvaharo bhaveta brāhmaṇo brāhmaṇaṃ veda bhartā veda striyaṃ tathāc amātyaṃ nṛpatir veda rājā rājānam eva caa na śatrur aṅkam āpanno moktavyo vadhyatāṃ gataḥb nyag bhūtvā paryupāsīta vadhyaṃ hanyād bale satib ahanyamāno bhayakṛn na hatāj jāyate bhayamc ahatād dhi bhayaṃ tasmāj jāyate nacirād ivaa daivateṣu ca yatnena rājasu brāhmaṇeṣu cac niyantavyaḥ sadā krodho vṛddhabālātureṣu caa nirarthaṃ kalahaṃ prājño varjayen mūḍhasevitamc kīrtiṃ ca labhate loke na cānarthena yujyatea prasādo niṣphalo yasya krodhaś cāpi nirarthakaḥc na taṃ bhartāram icchanti ṣaṇḍhaṃ patim iva striyaḥa na buddhir dhanalābhāya na jāḍyam asamṛddhayec lokaparyāyavṛttāntaṃ prājño jānāti netaraḥa vidyāśīlavayovṛddhān buddhivṛddhāṃś ca bhāratac dhanābhijanavṛddhāṃś ca nityaṃ mūḍho vamanyatea anāryavṛttam aprājñam asūyakam adhārmikamc anarthāḥ kṣipram āyānti vāgduṣṭaṃ krodhanaṃ tathāa avisaṃvādanaṃ dānaṃ samayasyāvyatikramaḥc āvartayanti bhūtāni samyak praṇihitā ca vāka avisaṃvādako dakṣaḥ kṛtajño matimān ṛjuḥc api saṃkṣīṇakośo pi labhate parivāraṇama dhṛtiḥ śamo damaḥ śaucaṃ kāruṇyaṃ vāg aniṣṭhurāc mitrāṇāṃ cānabhidrohaḥ saptaitāḥ samidhaḥ śriyaḥa asaṃvibhāgī duṣṭātmā kṛtaghno nirapatrapaḥc tādṛṅ narādhamo loke varjanīyo narādhipaa na sa rātrau sukhaṃ śete sasarpa iva veśmanic yaḥ kopayati nirdoṣaṃ sadoṣo bhyantaraṃ janama yeṣu duṣṭeṣu doṣaḥ syād yogakṣemasya bhāratac sadā prasādanaṃ teṣāṃ devatānām ivācareta ye rthāḥ strīṣu samāsaktāḥ prathamotpatiteṣu cac ye cānāryasamāsaktāḥ sarve te saṃśayaṃ gatāḥa yatra strī yatra kitavo yatra bālo nuśāsti cac majjanti te vaśā deśā nadyām aśmaplavā ivaa prayojaneṣu ye saktā na viśeṣeṣu bhāratac tān ahaṃ paṇḍitān manye viśeṣā hi prasaṅginaḥa yaṃ praśaṃsanti kitavā yaṃ praśaṃsanti cāraṇāḥc yaṃ praśaṃsanti bandhakyo na sa jīvati mānavaḥa hitvā tān parameṣvāsān pāṇḍavān amitaujasaḥc āhitaṃ bhārataiśvaryaṃ tvayā duryodhane mahata taṃ drakṣyasi paribhraṣṭaṃ tasmāt tvaṃ nacirād ivac aiśvaryamadasaṃmūḍhaṃ baliṃ lokatrayād iva dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa anīśvaro yaṃ puruṣo bhavābhavesūtraprotā dārumayīva yoṣāc dhātrā tu diṣṭasya vaśe kilāyaṃtasmād vada tvaṃ śravaṇe dhṛto ham vidura uvācaa aprāptakālaṃ vacanaṃ bṛhaspatir api bruvanc labhate buddhyavajñānam avamānaṃ ca bhārataa priyo bhavati dānena priyavādena cāparaḥc mantraṃ mūlabalenānyo yaḥ priyaḥ priya eva saḥa dveṣyo na sādhur bhavati na medhāvī na paṇḍitaḥc priye śubhāni karmāṇi dveṣye pāpāni bhāratad uktaṃ mayā jātamātre pi rājand duryodhanaṃ tyaja putraṃ tvam ekamd tasya tyāgāt putraśatasya vṛddhird asyātyāgāt putraśatasya nāśaḥd na vṛddhir bahumantavyā yā vṛddhiḥ kṣayam āvahetd kṣayo pi bahumantavyo yaḥ kṣayo vṛddhim āvaheta na sa kṣayo mahārāja yaḥ kṣayo vṛddhim āvahetc kṣayaḥ sa tv iha mantavyo yaṃ labdhvā bahu nāśayeta samṛddhā guṇataḥ ke cid bhavanti dhanato parec dhanavṛddhān guṇair hīnān dhṛtarāṣṭra vivarjayet dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa sarvaṃ tvam āyatīyuktaṃ bhāṣase prājñasaṃmatamc na cotsahe sutaṃ tyaktuṃ yato dharmas tato jayaḥ vidura uvācaa svabhāvaguṇasaṃpanno na jātu vinayānvitaḥc susūkṣmam api bhūtānām upamardaṃ prayokṣyatea parāpavādaniratāḥ paraduḥkhodayeṣu cac parasparavirodhe ca yatante satatotthitāḥa sadoṣaṃ darśanaṃ yeṣāṃ saṃvāse sumahad bhayamc arthādāne mahān doṣaḥ pradāne ca mahad bhayamd ye vai bhedanaśīlās tu sakāmā nistrapāḥ śaṭhāḥa ye pāpā iti vikhyātāḥ saṃvāse parigarhitāḥc yuktāś cānyair mahādoṣair ye narās tān vivarjayeta nivartamāne sauhārde prītir nīce praṇaśyatic yā caiva phalanirvṛttiḥ sauhṛde caiva yat sukhama yatate cāpavādāya yatnam ārabhate kṣayec alpe py apakṛte mohān na śāntim upagacchatia tādṛśaiḥ saṃgataṃ nīcair nṛśaṃsair akṛtātmabhiḥc niśāmya nipuṇaṃ buddhyā vidvān dūrād vivarjayeta yo jñātim anugṛhṇāti daridraṃ dīnam āturamc sa putrapaśubhir vṛddhiṃ yaśaś cāvyayam aśnutea jñātayo vardhanīyās tair ya icchanty ātmanaḥ śubhamc kulavṛddhiṃ ca rājendra tasmāt sādhu samācaraa śreyasā yokṣyase rājan kurvāṇo jñātisatkriyāmc viguṇā hy api saṃrakṣyā jñātayo bharatarṣabhaa kiṃ punar guṇavantas te tvatprasādābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥc prasādaṃ kuru dīnānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ viśāṃ patea dīyantāṃ grāmakāḥ ke cit teṣāṃ vṛttyartham īśvarac evaṃ loke yaśaḥprāpto bhaviṣyasi narādhipaa vṛddhena hi tvayā kāryaṃ putrāṇāṃ tāta rakṣaṇamc mayā cāpi hitaṃ vācyaṃ viddhi māṃ tvaddhitaiṣiṇama jñātibhir vigrahas tāta na kartavyo bhavārthināc sukhāni saha bhojyāni jñātibhir bharatarṣabhaa saṃbhojanaṃ saṃkathanaṃ saṃprītiś ca parasparamc jñātibhiḥ saha kāryāṇi na virodhaḥ kathaṃ canaa jñātayas tārayantīha jñātayo majjayanti cac suvṛttās tārayantīha durvṛttā majjayanti caa suvṛtto bhava rājendra pāṇḍavān prati mānadac adharṣaṇīyaḥ śatrūṇāṃ tair vṛtas tvaṃ bhaviṣyasia śrīmantaṃ jñātim āsādya yo jñātir avasīdatib sīdatā yat kṛtaṃ tena tat pāpaṃ samam aśnutec digdhahastaṃ mṛga iva sa enas tasya vindatia paścād api naraśreṣṭha tava tāpo bhaviṣyatic tān vā hatān sutān vāpi śrutvā tad anucintayaa yena khaṭvāṃ samārūḍhaḥ paritapyeta karmaṇāc ādāv eva na tat kuryād adhruve jīvite satia na kaś cin nāpanayate pumān anyatra bhārgavātc śeṣasaṃpratipattis tu buddhimatsv eva tiṣṭhatia duryodhanena yady etat pāpaṃ teṣu purā kṛtamc tvayā tat kulavṛddhena pratyāneyaṃ nareśvaraa tāṃs tvaṃ pade pratiṣṭhāpya loke vigatakalmaṣaḥc bhaviṣyasi naraśreṣṭha pūjanīyo manīṣiṇāma suvyāhṛtāni dhīrāṇāṃ phalataḥ pravicintya yaḥc adhyavasyati kāryeṣu ciraṃ yaśasi tiṣṭhatid asamyag upayuktaṃ hi jñānaṃ sukuśalair apid upalabhyāpy aviditaṃ viditaṃ cāpy anuṣṭhitamd pāpodayaphalaṃ vidvān yo nārabhati vardhated yas tu pūrvakṛtaṃ pāpam avimṛśyānuvartated so nyāparādhe durmedhā viṣame vinipātyated mantrabhedasya ṣaṭ prājño dvārāṇīmāni lakṣayetd arthasaṃtatikāmaś ca rakṣed etāni nityaśaḥd madaṃ svapnam avijñānam ākāraṃ cātmasaṃbhavamd duṣṭāmātyeṣu viśrambhaṃ dūtāc cākuśalād apid dvārāṇy etāni yo jñātvā saṃvṛṇoti sadā nṛpaḥd trivargacaraṇe yuktaḥ sa śatrūn adhitiṣṭhatid na vai śrutam avijñāya vṛddhān anupasevya cad dharmārthau vedituṃ śakyau bṛhaspatisamair apid naṣṭaṃ samudre patitaṃ naṣṭaṃ vākyam aśṛṇvatid anātmani śrutaṃ naṣṭaṃ naṣṭaṃ śrutam anagnikamd matyā parīkṣya medhāvī buddhyā saṃpādya cāsakṛtd śrutvā dṛṣṭvātha vijñāya prājño mantraṃ samācareta avṛttiṃ vinayo hanti hanty anarthaṃ parākramaḥc hanti nityaṃ kṣamā krodham ācāro hanty alakṣaṇama paricchadena kṣetreṇa veśmanā paricaryayāc parīkṣeta kulaṃ rājan bhojanācchādanena cad upasthitasya kāmasya prativādo na vidyated api nirmuktadehasya kāmaraktasya kiṃ punaḥd prājñopasevinaṃ vaidyaṃ dhārmikaṃ priyadarśanamd mitravantaṃ suvākyaṃ ca suhṛdaṃ paripālayetd duṣkulīnaḥ kulīno vā maryādāṃ yo na laṅghayetd dharmāpekṣī mṛdur hrīmān sa kulīnaśatād varaḥd arthasaṃtatikāmaś ca rakṣed etāni nityaśaḥa yayoś cittena vā cittaṃ naibhṛtaṃ naibhṛtena vāc sameti prajñayā prajñā tayor maitrī na jīryatea durbuddhim akṛtaprajñaṃ channaṃ kūpaṃ tṛṇair ivac vivarjayīta medhāvī tasmin maitrī praṇaśyatia avalipteṣu mūrkheṣu raudrasāhasikeṣu cac tathaivāpetadharmeṣu na maitrīm ācared budhaḥa kṛtajñaṃ dhārmikaṃ satyam akṣudraṃ dṛḍhabhaktikamc jitendriyaṃ sthitaṃ sthityāṃ mitram atyāgi ceṣyatea indriyāṇām anutsargo mṛtyunā na viśiṣyatec atyarthaṃ punar utsargaḥ sādayed daivatāny apia mārdavaṃ sarvabhūtānām anasūyā kṣamā dhṛtiḥc āyuṣyāṇi budhāḥ prāhur mitrāṇāṃ cāvimānanāa apanītaṃ sunītena yo rthaṃ pratyāninīṣatec matim āsthāya sudṛḍhāṃ tad akāpuruṣavratama āyatyāṃ pratikārajñas tadātve dṛḍhaniścayaḥc atīte kāryaśeṣajño naro rthair na prahīyatea karmaṇā manasā vācā yad abhīkṣṇaṃ niṣevatec tad evāpaharaty enaṃ tasmāt kalyāṇam ācareta maṅgalālambhanaṃ yogaḥ śrutam utthānam ārjavamc bhūtim etāni kurvanti pāpaṃ coreṇātmāpahāriṇāa aśrāntaḥ syād anādānāt saṃmato nirupadravaḥc śiṣṭo na śiṣṭavat sa syād brāhmaṇo brahmavit kaviḥa anāḍhyā mānuṣe vitte āḍhyā vedeṣu ye dvijāḥc te durdharṣā duṣprakampyā vidyāt abhisaṃjvaretd lokaḥ svabhāvavṛttir hi nimeṣonmeṣavat sadāa vidvāṃso mānayantīha iti manyeta mānitaḥc adharmaviduṣo mūḍhā lokaśāstraviśāradāḥe na mānyaṃ mānayiṣyanti iti manyed amānitaḥa na vai mānaṃ ca maunaṃ ca sahitau carataḥ sadāc ayaṃ hi loko mānasya asau mānasya tad viduḥa śrīḥ sukhasyeha saṃvāsaḥ sā cāpi paripanthinīc brāhmī sudurlabhā śrīr hi prajñāhīnena kṣatriyaa dvārāṇi tasyā hi vadanti santobahuprakārāṇi durāvarāṇic satyārjave hrīr damaśaucavidyāḥṣaṇmānamohapratibādhanāni dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca kasyaiṣa maunaḥ kataran nu maunaṃ prabrūhi vidvann iha maunabhāvam maunena vidvān uta yāti maunaṃ sanatsujāta uvāca kathaṃ mune maunam ihācaranti yato na vedā manasā sahainam anupraviśanti tato tha maunam yatrotthito vedaśabdas tathāyaṃ sa tanmayatvena vibhāti rājan dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa ṛco yajūṃṣy adhīte yaḥ sāmavedaṃ ca yo dvijaḥc pāpāni kurvan pāpena lipyate na sa lipyate sanatsujāta uvācaa nainaṃ sāmāny ṛco vāpi na yajūṃṣi vicakṣaṇac trāyante karmaṇaḥ pāpān na te mithyā bravīmy ahama na chandāṃsi vṛjināt tārayantimāyāvinaṃ māyayā vartamānamc nīḍaṃ śakuntā iva jātapakṣāśchandāṃsy enaṃ prajahaty antakāle dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa na ced vedā vedavidaṃ śaktās trātuṃ vicakṣaṇac atha kasmāt pralāpo yaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ sanātanaḥ sanatsujāta uvāca tasyaiva nāmādiviśeṣarūpair idaṃ jagad bhāti mahānubhāva nirdiśya samyak pravadanti vedās tad viśvavairūpyam udāharanti tadartham uktaṃ tapa etad ijyā tābhyām asau puṇyam upaiti vidvān puṇyena pāpaṃ vinihatya paścāt saṃjāyate jñānavidīpitātmā jñānena cātmānam upaiti vidvān athānyathā vargaphalānukāṅkṣī asmin kṛtaṃ tat parigṛhya sarvam amutra bhuṅkte punar eti mārgam tapas tapyati yo raṇye munir mūlaphalāśanaḥ brāhmaṇānāṃ tapaḥ svṛddham anyeṣāṃ tāvad eva tat etat samṛddham atyṛddhaṃ tapo bhavati kevalama asmiṃl loke tapas taptaṃ phalam anyatra dṛśyatec brāhmaṇānām ime lokā ṛddhe tapasi saṃyatāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa kathaṃ samṛddham apy ṛddhaṃ tapo bhavati kevalamc sanatsujāta tad brūhi yathā vidyāma tad vayamd sanatsujāta uvācad niṣkalmaṣaṃ tapas tv etat kevalaṃ paricakṣated etat samṛddham apy ṛddhaṃ tapo bhavati nānyathād tapomūlam idaṃ sarvaṃ yan māṃ pṛcchasi kṣatriyad dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācad tapasā vedavidvāṃsaḥ paraṃ tv amṛtam āpnuyuḥd kalmaṣaṃ tapaso brūhi śrutaṃ niṣkalmaṣaṃ tapaḥd sanatsujāta yenedaṃ vidyāṃ guhyaṃ sanātanamd śrīr evam ekā yo dhīte tac ca tāvac ca tatsamam sanatsujāta uvācaa krodhādayo dvādaśa yasya doṣāstathā nṛśaṃsādi ṣaḍ atra rājanc dharmādayo dvādaśa cātatānāḥśāstre guṇā ye viditā dvijānāma krodhaḥ kāmo lobhamohau vivitsākṛpāsūyā mānaśokau spṛhā cac īrṣyā jugupsā ca manuṣyadoṣāvarjyāḥ sadā dvādaśaite nareṇaa ekaikam ete rājendra manuṣyān paryupāsatec lipsamāno ntaraṃ teṣāṃ mṛgāṇām iva lubdhakaḥa vikatthanaḥ spṛhayālur manasvībibhrat kopaṃ capalo rakṣaṇaś cac ete prāptāḥ ṣaṇ narān pāpadharmānprakurvate nota santaḥ sudurgea saṃbhogasaṃvid dviṣam edhamānodattānutāpī kṛpaṇo balīyānc vargapraśaṃsī vanitāsu dveṣṭāete pare sapta nṛśaṃsadharmāḥa dharmaś ca satyaṃ ca damas tapaś caamātsaryaṃ hrīs titikṣānasūyāc yajñaś ca dānaṃ ca dhṛtiḥ śrutaṃ camahāvratā dvādaśa brāhmaṇasyaa yas tv etebhyaḥ pravased dvādaśebhyaḥsarvām apīmāṃ pṛthivīṃ praśiṣyātc tribhir dvābhyām ekato vā viśiṣṭonāsya svam astīti sa veditavyaḥa damas tyāgo pramādaś ca eteṣv amṛtam āhitamc tāni satyamukhāny āhur brāhmaṇā ye manīṣiṇaḥd doṣatyāgo pramādaḥ syāt sa cāpy aṣṭaguṇo mataḥa damo ṣṭādaśadoṣaḥ syāt pratikūlaṃ kṛtākṛtec anṛtaṃ cābhyasūyā ca kāmārthau ca tathā spṛhāa krodhaḥ śokas tathā tṛṣṇā lobhaḥ paiśunyam eva cac matsaraś ca vivitsā ca paritāpas tathā ratiḥa apasmāraḥ sātivādas tathā saṃbhāvanātmanib lokadveṣo bhimānaś ca vivādaḥ prāṇipīḍanamb parivādo tivādaś ca paritāpo kṣamā dhṛtiḥb asiddhiḥ pāpakṛtyaṃ ca hiṃsā ceti prakīrtitāḥc etair vimukto doṣair yaḥ sa damaḥ sadbhir ucyated mado ṣṭādaśadoṣaḥ syāt tyāgo bhavati ṣaḍguṇaḥd viparyayāḥ smṛtā ete madadoṣā udāhṛtāḥd śreyāṃs tu ṣaḍvidhas tyāgas tṛtīyas tatra duṣkaraḥd tena duḥkhaṃ taranty eva tasmiṃs tyakte jitaṃ bhavetd doṣā damasya ye proktās tān doṣān parivarjayeta śreyāṃs tu ṣaḍvidhas tyāgaḥ priyaṃ prāpya na hṛṣyatic apriye tu samutpanne vyathāṃ jātu na cārcchatia iṣṭān dārāṃś ca putrāṃś ca na cānyaṃ yad vaco bhavetc arhate yācamānāya pradeyaṃ tad vaco bhavetd iṣṭāpūrtaṃ dvitīyaṃ syān nityaṃ vairāgyayogataḥd kāmatyāgaś ca rājendra sa tṛtīya iti smṛtaḥd apramādī bhaved etaiḥ sa cāpy aṣṭaguṇo mahānd satyaṃ dhyānaṃ samādhānaṃ codyaṃ vairāgyam eva cad asteyo brahmacaryaṃ ca tathāsaṃgraha eva cad evaṃ doṣā madasyoktās tān doṣān parivarjayetd doṣatyāgo pramādaḥ syāt sa cāpy aṣṭaguṇo mataḥd tāṃs tu satyamukhān āhuḥ satye hy amṛtam āhitamd satyātmā bhava rājendra satye lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥd nivṛttenaiva doṣeṇa tapovratam ihācaretd etad dhātṛkṛtaṃ vṛttaṃ satyam eva satāṃ vratame apy avācyaṃ vadaty eva sa tṛtīyo guṇaḥ smṛtaḥa tyaktair dravyair yo bhavati nopayuṅkte ca kāmataḥb na ca dravyais tad bhavati nopayuktaiś ca kāmataḥc na ca karmasu tad dhīnaḥ śiṣyabuddhir naro yathāe sarvair eva guṇair yukto dravyavān api yo bhavetf ṣaṭprakāram imaṃ tyāgaṃ buddhvānyan nāvaśiṣyatea apramādo ṣṭadoṣaḥ syāt tān doṣān parivarjayetc indriyebhyaś ca pañcabhyo manasaś caiva bhāratae atītānāgatebhyaś ca mukto hy etaiḥ sukhī bhaveta doṣair etair vimuktaṃ tu guṇair etaiḥ samanvitamc etat samṛddham apy ṛddhaṃ tapo bhavati kevalame yan māṃ pṛcchasi rājendra kiṃ bhūyaḥ śrotum icchasif etat pāpaharaṃ śuddhaṃ janmamṛtyujarāpaham dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa ākhyānapañcamair vedair bhūyiṣṭhaṃ kathyate janaḥc tathaivānye caturvedās trivedāś ca tathāparea dvivedāś caikavedāś ca anṛcaś ca tathāparec teṣāṃ tu katamaḥ sa syād yam ahaṃ veda brāhmaṇam sanatsujāta uvācaa ekasya vedasyājñānād vedās te bahavo bhavanc satyasyaikasya rājendra satye kaś cid avasthitaḥe evaṃ vedam anutsādya prajñāṃ mahati kurvatea dānam adhyayanaṃ yajño lobhād etat pravartatec satyāt pracyavamānānāṃ saṃkalpo vitatho bhaveta tato yajñaḥ pratāyeta satyasyaivāvadhāraṇātc manasānyasya bhavati vācānyasyota karmaṇāe saṃkalpasiddhaḥ puruṣaḥ saṃkalpān adhitiṣṭhatia anaibhṛtyena vai tasya dīkṣitavratam ācaretc nāmaitad dhātunirvṛttaṃ satyam eva satāṃ parame jñānaṃ vai nāma pratyakṣaṃ parokṣaṃ jāyate tapaḥa vidyād bahu paṭhantaṃ tu bahupāṭhīti brāhmaṇamc tasmāt kṣatriya mā maṃsthā jalpitenaiva brāhmaṇame ya eva satyān nāpaiti sa jñeyo brāhmaṇas tvayāf chandāṃsi nāma dvipadāṃ variṣṭhaf svacchandayogena bhavanti tatraf chandovidas tena ca tān adhītyaf gatā hi vedasya na vedyam āryāḥf na vedānāṃ veditā kaś cid astif vedyena vedaṃ na vidur na vedyamf yo veda vedaṃ sa ca veda vedyaṃf yo veda vedyaṃ na sa veda satyamf yo veda vedān sa ca veda vedyaṃf na taṃ vidur vedavido na vedāḥf tathāpi vedena vidanti vedaṃf ye brāhmaṇā vedavido bhavantif dhāmāṃśabhāgasya tathā hi vedāf yathā hi śākhā ca mahīruhasyaf saṃvedane caiva yathāmanantif tasmin hi satye paramātmano rthea chandāṃsi nāma kṣatriya tāny atharvājagau purastād ṛṣisarga eṣaḥc chandovidas te ya u tān adhītyana vedyavedasya vidur na vedyama na vedānāṃ veditā kaś cid astikaś cid vedān budhyate vāpi rājanc yo veda vedān na sa veda vedyaṃsatye sthito yas tu sa veda vedyama abhijānāmi brāhmaṇam ākhyātāraṃ vicakṣaṇamb evaṃ yo hi vijānāti sa jānāti paraṃ hi tatb paraṃ hi tat paraṃ brahma jānāty eva ca brāhmaṇaḥb yo vai vijānāti paraṃ mayoktaṃb sa vai vijānāti paraṃ krameṇab nāsya paryeṣaṇaṃ gacchet pratyarthiṣu kathaṃ canab avicinvann imaṃ vede tataḥ paśyati taṃ prabhumc yaś chinnavicikitsaḥ sann ācaṣṭe sarvasaṃśayāna tasya paryeṣaṇaṃ gacchet prācīnaṃ nota dakṣiṇamc nārvācīnaṃ kutas tiryaṅ nādiśaṃ tu kathaṃ canaa tūṣṇīṃbhūta upāsīta na ceṣṭen manasā apic abhyāvarteta brahmāsya antarātmani vai śritama maunād dhi sa munir bhavati nāraṇyavasanān muniḥc akṣaraṃ tat tu yo veda sa muniḥ śreṣṭha ucyatea sarvārthānāṃ vyākaraṇād vaiyākaraṇa ucyateb tan mūlato vyākaraṇaṃ vyākarotīti tat tathāc pratyakṣadarśī lokānāṃ sarvadarśī bhaven naraḥa satye vai brāhmaṇas tiṣṭhan brahma paśyati kṣatriyab jñānādiṣu sthito py evaṃ kṣatriya brahma paśyatic vedānāṃ cānupūrvyeṇa etad vidvan bravīmi te dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa sanatsujāta yad imāṃ parārthāṃbrāhmīṃ vācaṃ pravadasi viśvarūpāmc parāṃ hi kāmeṣu sudurlabhāṃ kathāṃtad brūhi me vākyam etat kumāra sanatsujāta uvācaa naitad brahma tvaramāṇena labhyaṃyan māṃ pṛcchasy abhihṛṣyasy atīvab buddhau pralīne manasi pracintyāb vidyā hi sā brahmacaryeṇa labhyāc avyaktavidyām abhidhāsye purāṇīṃbuddhyā ca teṣāṃ brahmacaryeṇa siddhām dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa avyaktavidyām iti yat sanātanīṃbravīṣi tvaṃ brahmacaryeṇa siddhāmb ādyāṃ vidyāṃ vadasi hi satyarūpāṃb yā prāpyate brahmacaryeṇa sadbhiḥb yāṃ prāpyaitāṃ martyalokaṃ tyajantib yā vai vidyā guruvṛddheṣu nityāb dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācab brahmacaryeṇa yā vidyā śakyā veditum añjasāb tat kathaṃ brahmacaryaṃ syād etad vidvan bravīhi mec anārabhyā vasatīhārya kālekathaṃ brāhmaṇyam amṛtatvaṃ labheta sanatsujāta uvācaa ye smiṃl loke vijayantīha kāmānbrāhmīṃ sthitim anutitikṣamāṇāḥc ta ātmānaṃ nirharantīha dehānmuñjād iṣīkām iva sattvasaṃsthāḥd yadi sarve pramucyante kāmā ye hṛdi saṃsthitāḥd atha mṛtyor mṛta iti tatra brahma samaśnutea śarīram etau kurutaḥ pitā mātā ca bhāratac ācāryaśāstā yā jātiḥ sā satyā sājarāmarād ācāryatas tu yaj janma tat satyaṃ vai tathāmṛtamd tasmāt tām eva yatnena buddhimān pratipadyatea ācāryayonim iha ye praviśyabhūtvā garbhaṃ brahmacaryaṃ carantic ihaiva te śāstrakārā bhavantiprahāya dehaṃ paramaṃ yānti yogama ya āvṛṇoty avitathena karṇāvṛtaṃ kurvann amṛtaṃ saṃprayacchanc taṃ manyeta pitaraṃ mātaraṃ catasmai na druhyet kṛtam asya jānana guruṃ śiṣyo nityam abhimanyamānaḥsvādhyāyam icchec chucir apramattaḥc mānaṃ na kuryān na dadhīta roṣameṣa prathamo brahmacaryasya pādaḥd śiṣyavṛttikrameṇaiva vidyām āpnoti yaḥ śuciḥd brahmacaryavratasyāsya prathamaḥ pāda ucyatea ācāryasya priyaṃ kuryāt prāṇair api dhanair apic karmaṇā manasā vācā dvitīyaḥ pāda ucyatea samā gurau yathā vṛttir gurupatnyāṃ tathā bhavetc yathoktakārī priyakṛt tṛtīyaḥ pāda ucyated ācāryeṇa kṛtaṃ jñātvā bhāvito smīti manyated taṃ guruṃ prati hṛṣṭaḥ saṃstṛtīyaḥ pāda ucyated ācāryeṇātmakṛtaṃ vijānañd jñātvā cārthaṃ bhāvito smīty anenad yan manyate taṃ prati hṛṣṭabuddhiḥd sa vai tṛtīyo brahmacaryasya pādaḥa nācāryāyehopakṛtvā pravādaṃprājñaḥ kurvīta naitad ahaṃ karomic itīva manyeta na bhāṣayetasa vai caturtho brahmacaryasya pādaḥd evaṃ vasantaṃ yad upaplaved dhid nācāryāya kṛtam iti cābhimānātd prājño manye naitad ahaṃ karomid sa vai caturtho brahmacaryasya pādaḥd kālena pādaṃ labhate tathārthaṃd tataś ca pādaṃ guruyogataś cad utsāhayogena ca pādam ṛcchecd chāstreṇa pādaṃ ca tato bhiyātid jñānādayo dvādaśa yasya rūpamd anyāni cāṅgāni tathā balaṃ cad ācāryayoge phalatīti cāhurd brahmārthayogena ca brahmacaryama evaṃ vasantaṃ yad upaplaved dhanamācāryāya tad anuprayacchetc satāṃ vṛttiṃ bahuguṇām evam etiguroḥ putre bhavati ca vṛttir eṣāa evaṃ vasan sarvato vardhatīhabahūn putrāṃl labhate ca pratiṣṭhāmc varṣanti cāsmai pradiśo diśaś cavasanty asmin brahmacarye janāś caa etena brahmacaryeṇa devā devatvam āpnuvanc ṛṣayaś ca mahābhāgā brahmalokaṃ manīṣiṇaḥa gandharvāṇām anenaiva rūpam apsarasām abhūtc etena brahmacaryeṇa sūryo ahnāya jāyated ākāṅkṣārthasya saṃyogād rasabhedārthinām ivad evaṃ hy etat samājñāya tādṛg bhāvaṃ gatā imea ya āśayet pāṭayec cāpi rājansarvaṃ śarīraṃ tapasā tapyamānaḥc etenāsau bālyam atyeti vidvānmṛtyuṃ tathā rodhayaty antakālea antavantaḥ kṣatriya te jayantilokāñ janāḥ karmaṇā nirmitenac brahmaiva vidvāṃs tena abhyeti sarvaṃnānyaḥ panthā ayanāya vidyate dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa ābhāti śuklam iva lohitam ivaatho kṛṣṇam athāñjanaṃ kādravaṃ vāc tad brāhmaṇaḥ paśyati yo tra vidvānkathaṃrūpaṃ tad amṛtam akṣaraṃ padam sanatsujāta uvācaa nābhāti śuklam iva lohitam ivaatho kṛṣṇam āyasam arkavarṇamc na pṛthivyāṃ tiṣṭhati nāntarikṣenaitat samudre salilaṃ bibhartia na tārakāsu na ca vidyud āśritaṃna cābhreṣu dṛśyate rūpam asyac na cāpi vāyau na ca devatāsuna tac candre dṛśyate nota sūryea naivarkṣu tan na yajuḥṣu nāpy atharvasuna caiva dṛśyaty amaleṣu sāmasuc rathaṃtare bārhate cāpi rājanmahāvrate naiva dṛśyed dhruvaṃ tata apāraṇīyaṃ tamasaḥ parastāttad antako py eti vināśakālec aṇīyarūpaṃ kṣuradhārayā tanmahac ca rūpaṃ tv api parvatebhyaḥa sā pratiṣṭhā tad amṛtaṃ lokās tad brahma tad yaśaḥc bhūtāni jajñire tasmāt pralayaṃ yānti tatra caa anāmayaṃ tan mahad udyataṃ yaśovāco vikārān kavayo vadantic tasmiñ jagat sarvam idaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃye tad vidur amṛtās te bhavantid sanatsujāta uvācad śokaḥ krodhaś ca lobhaś ca kāmo mānaḥ parāsutād īrṣyā moho vivitsā ca kṛpāsūyā jugupsutād dvādaśaite mahādoṣā manuṣyaprāṇanāśanāḥd ekaikam ete rājendra manuṣyān paryupāsated yair āviṣṭo naraḥ pāpaṃ mūḍhasaṃjño vyavasyatid spṛhayālur ugraḥ paruṣo vāvadānyaḥd krodhaṃ bibhran manasā vai vikatthīd nṛśaṃsadharmāḥ ṣaḍ ime janā vaid prāpyāpy arthaṃ nota sabhājayanted saṃbhogasaṃvid viṣamo timānīd dattvā vikatthī kṛpaṇo durbalaś cad bahupraśaṃsī vanitādviṭ sadaivad saptaivoktāḥ pāpaśīlā nṛśaṃsāḥd dharmaś ca satyaṃ ca tapo damaś cad amātsaryaṃ hrīs titikṣānasūyād dānaṃ śrutaṃ caiva dhṛtiḥ kṣamā cad mahāvratā dvādaśa brāhmaṇasyad yo naitebhyaḥ pracyaved dvādaśabhyaḥd sarvām apīmāṃ pṛthivīṃ sa śiṣyātd tribhir dvābhyām ekato vārthito yod nāsya svam astīti ca veditavyamd damas tyāgo thāpramāda ity eteṣv amṛtaṃ sthitamd etāni brahmamukhyānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ manīṣiṇāmd sad vāsad vā parīvādo brāhmaṇasya na śasyated narakapratiṣṭhās te vai syur ya evaṃ kurvate narāḥd mado ṣṭādaśadoṣaḥ sa syāt purā yo prakīrtitaḥd lokadveṣyaṃ prātikūlyam abhyasūyā mṛṣāvacaḥd kāmakrodhau pāratantryaṃ parivādo tha paiśunamd arthahānir vivitsā ca mātsaryaṃ prāṇipīḍanamd īrṣyā moho tivādaś ca saṃjñānāśo bhyasūyitād tasmāt prājño na mādyeta sadā hy etad vigarhitamd sauhṛde vai ṣaḍ guṇā veditavyāḥd priye hṛṣyanty apriye ca vyathanted syād ātmanaḥ suciraṃ yācate yod dadāty ayācyam api deyaṃ khalu syātd iṣṭān putrān vibhavān svāṃś ca dārānd abhyarthitaś cārhati śuddhabhāvaḥd tyaktadravyaḥ saṃvasen neha kāmādd bhuṅkte karma svāśiṣaṃ bādhate cad dravyavān guṇavān evaṃ tyāgī bhavati sāttvikaḥd pañca bhūtāni pañcabhyo nivartayati tādṛśaḥd etat samṛddham apy ūrdhvaṃ tapo bhavati kevalamd sattvāt pracyavamānānāṃ saṃkalpena samāhitamd yato yajñāḥ pravardhante satyasyaivāvarodhanātd manasānyasya bhavati vācānyasyātha karmaṇād saṃkalpasiddhaṃ puruṣam asaṃkalpo dhitiṣṭhatid brāhmaṇasya viśeṣeṇa kiṃ cānyad api me śruṇud adhyāpayen mahad etad yaśasyaṃd vāco vikāraṃ kavayo vadantid asmin yoge sarvam idaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃd ye tad vidur amṛtās te bhavantid na karmaṇā sukṛtenaiva rājand satyaṃ vadej juhuyād vā yajed vād naitena bālo mṛtyum abhyeti rājand ratiṃ cāsau na labhaty antakāled tūṣṇīm eka upāsīta ceṣṭeta manasāpi nad tathā saṃstutinindābhyāṃ prītiroṣau vivarjayetd atraiva tiṣṭhan kṣatriya brahmāviśati paśyatid vedeṣu cānupūrvyeṇa etad vidvan bravīmi ted tad etad ahnā saṃsthitaṃ bhāti sarvaṃd tad ātmavit paśyati jñānayogātd tasmiñ jagat sarvam idaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃd ya etad vidur amṛtās te bhavanti sanatsujāta uvācaa yat tac chukraṃ mahaj ratha āyāti yo yāsīt pāṇḍavān pratic dūto nas tūrṇam āyātaḥ saindhavaiḥ sādhuvāhibhiḥa upayāya tu sa kṣipraṃ rathāt praskandya kuṇḍalīc praviveśa sabhāṃ pūrṇāṃ mahīpālair mahātmabhiḥ saṃjaya uvācaa prāpto smi pāṇḍavān gatvā tad vijānīta kauravāḥc yathāvayaḥ kurūn sarvān pratinandanti pāṇḍavāḥa abhivādayanti vṛddhāṃś ca vayasyāṃś ca vayasyavatc yūnaś cābhyavadan pārthāḥ pratipūjya yathāvayaḥa śṛṇvataḥ keśavasyaa anvatrasto bāhuvīryaṃ vidānaupahvare vāsudevasya dhīraḥc avocan māṃ yotsyamānaḥ kirīṭīmadhye brūyā dhārtarāṣṭraṃ kurūṇāmd saṃśṛṇvatas tasya durbhāṣiṇo vaid durātmanaḥ sūtaputrasya sūtad yo yoddhum āśaṃsati māṃ sadaivad mandaprajñaḥ kālapakvo timūḍhaḥa ye vai rājānaḥ pāṇḍavāyodhanāyasamānītāḥ śṛṇvatāṃ cāpi teṣāmc yathā samagraṃ vacanaṃ mayoktaṃsahāmātyaṃ śrāvayethā nṛpaṃ tama
