uttamamb evam uktvā sumanasas te bhijagmur janārdanamb pāṇḍavaiḥ saha rājāno marutvantam ivāmarāḥb tathā ca duḥsahāḥ sarve sadasyaiś ca nararṣabhāḥb janārdanaṃ samāsādya kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥb tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājann upagamya nararṣabhamc abhyabhāṣata dāśārham ṛṣabhaṃ sarvasātvatāma ayaṃ sa kālaḥ saṃprāpto mitrāṇāṃ me janārdanac na ca tvad anyaṃ paśyāmi yo na āpatsu tārayeta tvāṃ hi mādhava saṃśritya nirbhayā mohadarpitamc dhārtarāṣṭraṃ sahāmātyaṃ svam aṃśam anuyuñjmahea yathā hi sarvāsv āpatsu pāsi vṛṣṇīn ariṃdamac tathā te pāṇḍavā rakṣyāḥ pāhy asmān mahato bhayāt bhagavān uvācaa ayam asmi mahābāho brūhi yat te vivakṣitamc kariṣyāmi hi tat sarvaṃ yat tvaṃ vakṣyasi bhārata yudhiṣṭhira uvāca mṛdupūrvaṃ sāmamiśraṃ sāntvam ugraṃ ca mādhava na tu tan nyāyam āsthāya garhitāś ca tato vayama śrutaṃ te dhṛtarāṣṭrasya saputrasya cikīrṣitamc etad dhi sakalaṃ kṛṣṇa saṃjayo māṃ yad abravīta tan mataṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya so syātmā vivṛtāntaraḥc yathoktaṃ dūta ācaṣṭe vadhyaḥ syād anyathā bruvana apradānena rājyasya śāntim asmāsu mārgatic lubdhaḥ pāpena manasā carann asamam ātmanaḥa yat tad dvādaśa varṣāṇi vane nirvyuṣitā vayamc chadmanā śaradaṃ caikāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāta sthātā naḥ samaye tasmin dhṛtarāṣṭra iti prabhoc nāhāsma samayaṃ kṛṣṇa tad dhi no brāhmaṇā viduḥa vṛddho rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ svadharmaṃ nānupaśyatic paśyan vā putragṛddhitvān mandasyānveti śāsanama suyodhanamate tiṣṭhan rājāsmāsu janārdanac mithyā carati lubdhaḥ saṃś caran priyam ivātmanaḥa ito duḥkhataraṃ kiṃ nu yatrāhaṃ mātaraṃ tataḥc saṃvidhātuṃ na śaknomi mitrāṇāṃ vā janārdanaa kāśibhiś cedipāñcālair matsyaiś ca madhusūdanac bhavatā caiva nāthena pañca grāmā vṛtā mayāa kuśasthalaṃ vṛkasthalam āsandī vāraṇāvatamc avasānaṃ ca govinda kiṃ cid evātra pañcamama pañca nas tāta dīyantāṃ grāmā vā nagarāṇi vāc vasema sahitā yeṣu mā ca no bharatā naśana na ca tān api duṣṭātmā dhārtarāṣṭro numanyatec svāmyam ātmani matvāsāv ato duḥkhataraṃ nu kima kule jātasya vṛddhasya paravitteṣu gṛdhyataḥc lobhaḥ prajñānam āhanti prajñā hanti hatā hriyama hrīr hatā bādhate dharmaṃ dharmo hanti hataḥ śriyamc śrīr hatā puruṣaṃ hanti puruṣasyāsvatā vadhaḥa asvato hi nivartante jñātayaḥ suhṛdartvijaḥc apuṣpād aphalād vṛkṣād yathā tāta patatriṇaḥa etac ca maraṇaṃ tāta yad asmāt patitād ivac jñātayo vinivartante pretasattvād ivāsavaḥa nātaḥ pāpīyasīṃ kāṃ cid avasthāṃ śambaro bravītc yatra naivādya na prātar bhojanaṃ pratidṛśyatea dhanam āhuḥ paraṃ dharmaṃ dhane sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitamc jīvanti dhanino loke mṛtā ye tv adhanā narāḥa ye dhanād apakarṣanti naraṃ svabalam āśritāḥc te dharmam arthaṃ kāmaṃ ca pramathnanti naraṃ ca tama etām avasthāṃ prāpyaike maraṇaṃ vavrire janāḥc grāmāyaike vanāyaike nāśāyaike pravavrajuḥa unmādam eke puṣyanti yānty anye dviṣatāṃ vaśamc dāsyam eke nigacchanti pareṣām arthahetunāa āpad evāsya maraṇāt puruṣasya garīyasīc śriyo vināśas tad dhy asya nimittaṃ dharmakāmayoḥa yad asya dharmyaṃ maraṇaṃ śāśvataṃ lokavartma tatc samantāt sarvabhūtānāṃ na tad atyeti kaś canaa na tathā bādhyate kṛṣṇa prakṛtyā nirdhano janaḥc yathā bhadrāṃ śriyaṃ prāpya tayā hīnaḥ sukhaidhitaḥa sa tadātmāparādhena saṃprāpto vyasanaṃ mahatc sendrān garhayate devān nātmānaṃ ca kathaṃ canaa na cāsmin sarvaśāstrāṇi prataranti nigarhaṇāmc so bhikrudhyati bhṛtyānāṃ suhṛdaś cābhyasūyatia taṃ tadā manyur evaiti sa bhūyaḥ saṃpramuhyatic sa mohavaśam āpannaḥ krūraṃ karma niṣevatea pāpakarmātyayāyaiva saṃkaraṃ tena puṣyatic saṃkaro narakāyaiva sā kāṣṭhā pāpakarmaṇāma na cet prabudhyate kṛṣṇa narakāyaiva gacchatic tasya prabodhaḥ prajñaiva prajñācakṣur na riṣyatia prajñālābhe hi puruṣaḥ śāstrāṇy evānvavekṣatec śāstranityaḥ punar dharmaṃ tasya hrīr aṅgam uttamama hrīmān hi pāpaṃ pradveṣṭi tasya śrīr abhivardhatec śrīmān sa yāvad bhavati tāvad bhavati pūruṣaḥa dharmanityaḥ praśāntātmā kāryayogavahaḥ sadāc nādharme kurute buddhiṃ na ca pāpeṣu vartatea ahrīko vā vimūḍho vā naiva strī na punaḥ pumānc nāsyādhikāro dharme sti yathā śūdras tathaiva saḥa hrīmān avati devāṃś ca pitṝn ātmānam eva cac tenāmṛtatvaṃ vrajati sā kāṣṭhā puṇyakarmaṇāma tad idaṃ mayi te dṛṣṭaṃ pratyakṣaṃ madhusūdanac yathā rājyāt paribhraṣṭo vasāmi vasatīr imāḥa te vayaṃ na śriyaṃ hātum alaṃ nyāyena kena citc atra no yatamānānāṃ vadhaś ced api sādhu tata tatra naḥ prathamaḥ kalpo yad vayaṃ te ca mādhavac praśāntāḥ samabhūtāś ca śriyaṃ tān aśnuvīmahia tatraiṣā paramā kāṣṭhā raudrakarmakṣayodayāc yad vayaṃ kauravān hatvā tāni rāṣṭrāṇy aśīmahia ye punaḥ syur asaṃbaddhā anāryāḥ kṛṣṇa śatravaḥc teṣām apy avadhaḥ kāryaḥ kiṃ punar ye syur īdṛśāḥa jñātayaś ca hi bhūyiṣṭhāḥ sahāyā guravaś ca naḥc teṣāṃ vadho tipāpīyān kiṃ nu yuddhe sti śobhanama pāpaḥ kṣatriyadharmo yaṃ vayaṃ ca kṣatrabāndhavāḥc sa naḥ svadharmo dharmo vā vṛttir anyā vigarhitāa śūdraḥ karoti śuśrūṣāṃ vaiśyā vipaṇijīvinaḥc vayaṃ vadhena jīvāmaḥ kapālaṃ brāhmaṇair vṛtama kṣatriyaḥ kṣatriyaṃ hanti matsyo matsyena jīvatic śvā śvānaṃ hanti dāśārha paśya dharmo yathāgataḥa yuddhe kṛṣṇa kalir nityaṃ prāṇāḥ sīdanti saṃyugec balaṃ tu nītimātrāya haṭhe jayaparājayaua nātmacchandena bhūtānāṃ jīvitaṃ maraṇaṃ tathāc nāpy akāle sukhaṃ prāpyaṃ duḥkhaṃ vāpi yadūttamaa eko hy api bahūn hanti ghnanty ekaṃ bahavo py utac śūraṃ kāpuruṣo hanti ayaśasvī yaśasvinama jayaś caivobhayor dṛṣṭa ubhayoś ca parājayaḥc tathaivāpacayo dṛṣṭo vyapayāne kṣayavyayaua sarvathā vṛjinaṃ yuddhaṃ ko ghnan na pratihanyatec hatasya ca hṛṣīkeśa samau jayaparājayaua parājayaś ca maraṇān manye naiva viśiṣyatec yasya syād vijayaḥ kṛṣṇa tasyāpy apacayo dhruvama antato dayitaṃ ghnanti ke cid apy apare janāḥc tasyāṅga balahīnasya putrān bhrātṝn apaśyataḥe nirvedo jīvite kṛṣṇa sarvataś copajāyatea ye hy eva vīrā hrīmanta āryāḥ karuṇavedinaḥc ta eva yuddhe hanyante yavīyān mucyate janaḥa hatvāpy anuśayo nityaṃ parān api janārdanac anubandhaś ca pāpo tra śeṣaś cāpy avaśiṣyatea śeṣo hi balam āsādya na śeṣam avaśeṣayetc sarvocchede ca yatate vairasyāntavidhitsayāa jayo vairaṃ prasṛjati duḥkham āste parājitaḥc sukhaṃ praśāntaḥ svapiti hitvā jayaparājayaua jātavairaś ca puruṣo duḥkhaṃ svapiti nityadāc anirvṛtena manasā sasarpa iva veśmania utsādayati yaḥ sarvaṃ yaśasā sa viyujyatec akīrtiṃ sarvabhūteṣu śāśvatīṃ sa niyacchatia na hi vairāṇi śāmyanti dīrghakālakṛtāny apic ākhyātāraś ca vidyante pumāṃś cotpadyate kulea na cāpi vairaṃ vaireṇa keśava vyupaśāmyatic haviṣāgnir yathā kṛṣṇa bhūya evābhivardhatea ato nyathā nāsti śāntir nityam antaram antataḥc antaraṃ lipsamānānām ayaṃ doṣo nirantaraḥa pauruṣeyo hi balavān ādhir hṛdayabādhanaḥc tasya tyāgena vā śāntir nivṛttyā manaso pi vāa atha vā mūlaghātena dviṣatāṃ madhusūdanac phalanirvṛttir iddhā syāt tan nṛśaṃsataraṃ bhaveta yā tu tyāgena śāntiḥ syāt tad ṛte vadha eva saḥc saṃśayāc ca samucchedād dviṣatām ātmanas tathāa na ca tyaktuṃ tad icchāmo na cecchāmaḥ kulakṣayamc atra yā praṇipātena śāntiḥ saiva garīyasīa sarvathā yatamānānām ayuddham abhikāṅkṣatāmc sāntve pratihate yuddhaṃ prasiddham aparākramama pratighātena sāntvasya dāruṇaṃ saṃpravartatec tac chunām iva gopāde paṇḍitair upalakṣitama lāṅgūlacālanaṃ kṣveḍaḥ pratirāvo vivartanamc dantadarśanam ārāvas tato yuddhaṃ pravartatea tatra yo balavān kṛṣṇa jitvā so tti tad āmiṣamc evam eva manuṣyeṣu viśeṣo nāsti kaś canaa sarvathā tv etad ucitaṃ durbaleṣu balīyasāmc anādaro virodhaś ca praṇipātī hi durbalaḥa pitā rājā ca vṛddhaś ca sarvathā mānam arhatic tasmān mānyaś ca pūjyaś ca dhṛtarāṣṭro janārdanaa putrasnehas tu balavān dhṛtarāṣṭrasya mādhavac sa putravaśam āpannaḥ praṇipātaṃ prahāsyatia tatra kiṃ manyase kṛṣṇa prāptakālam anantaramc katham arthāc ca dharmāc ca na hīyemahi mādhavaa īdṛśe hy arthakṛcchre smin kam anyaṃ madhusūdanac upasaṃpraṣṭum arhāmi tvām ṛte puruṣottamaa priyaś ca priyakāmaś ca gatijñaḥ sarvakarmaṇāmc ko hi kṛṣṇāsti nas tvādṛk sarvaniścayavit suhṛt vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca dharmarājaṃ janārdanaḥc ubhayor eva vām arthe yāsyāmi kurusaṃsadama śamaṃ tatra labheyaṃ ced yuṣmadartham ahāpayanc puṇyaṃ me sumahad rājaṃś caritaṃ syān mahāphalama mocayeyaṃ mṛtyupāśāt saṃrabdhān kurusṛñjayānc pāṇḍavān dhārtarāṣṭrāṃś ca sarvāṃ ca pṛthivīm imāmd evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca dharmarājo janārdanamd bhrātṝṇāṃ samavetānāṃ sa kāle puruṣottamam yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa na mamaitan mataṃ kṛṣṇa yat tvaṃ yāyāḥ kurūn pratic suyodhanaḥ sūktam api na kariṣyati te vacaḥd suyodhanaś ca duṣṭātmā karṇaś ca sahasaubalaḥa sametaṃ pārthivaṃ kṣatraṃ suyodhanavaśānugamc teṣāṃ madhyāvataraṇaṃ tava kṛṣṇa na rocayea na hi naḥ prīṇayed dravyaṃ na devatvaṃ kutaḥ sukhamc na ca sarvāmaraiśvaryaṃ tava rodhena mādhava bhagavān uvācaa jānāmy etāṃ mahārāja dhārtarāṣṭrasya pāpatāmc avācyās tu bhaviṣyāmaḥ sarvaloke mahīkṣitāma na cāpi mama paryāptāḥ sahitāḥ sarvapārthivāḥc kruddhasya pramukhe sthātuṃ siṃhasyevetare mṛgāḥa atha cet te pravarteran mayi kiṃ cid asāṃpratamc nirdaheyaṃ kurūn sarvān iti me dhīyate matiḥa na jātu gamanaṃ tatra bhavet pārtha nirarthakamc arthaprāptiḥ kadā cit syād antato vāpy avācyatā yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa yat tubhyaṃ rocate kṛṣṇa svasti prāpnuhi kauravānc kṛtārthaṃ svastimantaṃ tvāṃ drakṣyāmi punarāgatama viṣvaksena kurūn gatvā bhāratāñ śamayeḥ prabhoc yathā sarve sumanasaḥ saha syāmaḥ sucetasaḥa bhrātā cāsi sakhā cāsi bībhatsor mama ca priyaḥc sauhṛdenāviśaṅkyo si svasti prāpnuhi bhūtayea asmān vettha parān vettha vetthārthaṃ vettha bhāṣitamc yad yad asmaddhitaṃ kṛṣṇa tat tad vācyaḥ suyodhanaḥa yad yad dharmeṇa saṃyuktam upapadyed dhitaṃ vacaḥc tat tat keśava bhāṣethāḥ sāntvaṃ vā yadi vetarat bhagavān uvācaa saṃjayasya śrutaṃ vākyaṃ bhavataś ca śrutaṃ mayāc sarvaṃ jānāmy abhiprāyaṃ teṣāṃ ca bhavataś ca yaḥa tava dharmāśritā buddhis teṣāṃ vairāśritā matiḥc yad ayuddhena labhyeta tat te bahumataṃ bhaveta na ca tan naiṣṭhikaṃ karma kṣatriyasya viśāṃ patec āhur āśramiṇaḥ sarve yad bhaikṣaṃ kṣatriyaś careta jayo vadho vā saṃgrāme dhātrā diṣṭaḥ sanātanaḥc svadharmaḥ kṣatriyasyaiṣa kārpaṇyaṃ na praśasyatea na hi kārpaṇyam āsthāya śakyā vṛttir yudhiṣṭhirac vikramasva mahābāho jahi śatrūn ariṃdamaa atigṛddhāḥ kṛtasnehā dīrghakālaṃ sahoṣitāḥc kṛtamitrāḥ kṛtabalā dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ paraṃtapaa na paryāyo sti yat sāmyaṃ tvayi kuryur viśāṃ patec balavattāṃ hi manyante bhīṣmadroṇakṛpādibhiḥa yāvac ca mārdavenaitān rājann upacariṣyasic tāvad ete hariṣyanti tava rājyam ariṃdamaa nānukrośān na kārpaṇyān na ca dharmārthakāraṇātc alaṃ kartuṃ dhārtarāṣṭrās tava kāmam ariṃdamaa etad eva nimittaṃ te pāṇḍavās tu yathā tvayic nānvatapyanta kaupīnaṃ tāvat kṛtvāpi duṣkarama pitāmahasya droṇasya vidurasya ca dhīmataḥb brāhmaṇānāṃ ca sādhūnāṃ rājñaś ca nagarasya cac paśyatāṃ kurumukhyānāṃ sarveṣām eva tattvataḥa dānaśīlaṃ mṛduṃ dāntaṃ dharmakāmam anuvratamc yat tvām upadhinā rājan dyūtenāvañcayat tadāe na cāpatrapate pāpo nṛśaṃsas tena karmaṇāa tathāśīlasamācāre rājan mā praṇayaṃ kṛthāḥc vadhyās te sarvalokasya kiṃ punas tava bhārataa vāgbhis tv apratirūpābhir atudat sakanīyasamc ślāghamānaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ san bhāṣate bhrātṛbhiḥ sahaa etāvat pāṇḍavānāṃ hi nāsti kiṃ cid iha svakamc nāmadheyaṃ ca gotraṃ ca tad apy eṣāṃ na śiṣyatea kālena mahatā caiṣāṃ bhaviṣyati parābhavaḥc prakṛtiṃ te bhajiṣyanti naṣṭaprakṛtayo janāḥd duḥśāsanena pāpena tadā dyūte pravartited anāthavat tadā devī draupadī sudurātmanād ākṛṣya keśe rudatī sabhāyāṃ rājasaṃsadid bhīṣmadroṇapramukhato gaur iti vyāhṛtā muhuḥd bhavatā vāritāḥ sarve bhrātaro bhīmavikramāḥd dharmapāśanibaddhāś ca na kiṃ cit pratipedirea etāś cānyāś ca paruṣā vācaḥ sa samudīrayanc ślāghate jñātimadhye sma tvayi pravrajite vanama ye tatrāsan samānītās te dṛṣṭvā tvām anāgasamc aśrukaṇṭhā rudantaś ca sabhāyām āsate tadāa na cainam abhyanandaṃs te rājāno brāhmaṇaiḥ sahac sarve duryodhanaṃ tatra nindanti sma sabhāsadaḥa kulīnasya ca yā nindā vadhaś cāmitrakarśanac mahāguṇo vadho rājan na tu nindā kujīvikāa tadaiva nihato rājan yadaiva nirapatrapaḥc ninditaś ca mahārāja pṛthivyāṃ sarvarājasua īṣatkāryo vadhas tasya yasya cāritram īdṛśamc praskambhanapratistabdhaś chinnamūla iva drumaḥa vadhyaḥ sarpa ivānāryaḥ sarvalokasya durmatiḥc jahy enaṃ tvam amitraghna mā rājan vicikitsithāḥa sarvathā tvatkṣamaṃ caitad rocate ca mamānaghac yat tvaṃ pitari bhīṣme ca praṇipātaṃ samācareḥa ahaṃ tu sarvalokasya gatvā chetsyāmi saṃśayamc yeṣām asti dvidhābhāvo rājan duryodhanaṃ pratia madhye rājñām ahaṃ tatra prātipauruṣikān guṇānc tava saṃkīrtayiṣyāmi ye ca tasya vyatikramāḥa bruvatas tatra me vākyaṃ dharmārthasahitaṃ hitamc niśamya pārthivāḥ sarve nānājanapadeśvarāḥa tvayi saṃpratipatsyante dharmātmā satyavāg itic tasmiṃś cādhigamiṣyanti yathā lobhād avartataa garhayiṣyāmi caivainaṃ paurajānapadeṣv apic vṛddhabālān upādāya cāturvarṇyasamāgamea śamaṃ ced yācamānas tvaṃ na dharmaṃ tatra lapsyasec kurūn vigarhayiṣyanti dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca pārthivāḥa tasmiṃl lokaparityakte kiṃ kāryam avaśiṣyatec hate duryodhane rājan yad anyat kriyatām itia yātvā cāhaṃ kurūn sarvān yuṣmadartham ahāpayanc yatiṣye praśamaṃ kartuṃ lakṣayiṣye ca ceṣṭitama kauravāṇāṃ pravṛttiṃ ca gatvā yuddhādhikārikāmc niśāmya vinivartiṣye jayāya tava bhārataa sarvathā yuddham evāham āśaṃsāmi paraiḥ sahac nimittāni hi sarvāṇi tathā prādurbhavanti mea mṛgāḥ śakuntāś ca vadanti ghoraṃhastyaśvamukhyeṣu niśāmukheṣuc ghorāṇi rūpāṇi tathaiva cāgnirvarṇān bahūn puṣyati ghorarūpāne manuṣyalokakṣapaṇo tha ghorono ced anuprāpta ihāntakaḥ syāta śastrāṇi patraṃ kavacān rathāṃś canāgān dhvajāṃś ca pratipādayitvāc yodhāś ca sarve kṛtaniśramās tebhavantu hastyaśvaratheṣu yattāḥe sāṃgrāmikaṃ te yad upārjanīyaṃsarvaṃ samagraṃ kuru tan narendraa duryodhano na hy alam adya dātuṃjīvaṃs tavaitan nṛpate kathaṃ citc yat te purastād abhavat samṛddhaṃdyūte hṛtaṃ pāṇḍavamukhya rājyam bhīmasena uvācaa yathā yathaiva śāntiḥ syāt kurūṇāṃ madhusūdanac tathā tathaiva bhāṣethā mā sma yuddhena bhīṣayeḥa amarṣī nityasaṃrabdhaḥ śreyodveṣī mahāmanāḥc nograṃ duryodhano vācyaḥ sāmnaivainaṃ samācareḥa prakṛtyā pāpasattvaś ca tulyacetāś ca dasyubhiḥc aiśvaryamadamattaś ca kṛtavairaś ca pāṇḍavaiḥa adīrghadarśī niṣṭhūrī kṣeptā krūraparākramaḥc dīrghamanyur aneyaś ca pāpātmā nikṛtipriyaḥa mriyetāpi na bhajyeta naiva jahyāt svakaṃ matamc tādṛśena śamaṃ kṛṣṇa manye paramaduṣkarama suhṛdām apy avācīnas tyaktadharmaḥ priyānṛtaḥc pratihanty eva suhṛdāṃ vācaś caiva manāṃsi caa sa manyuvaśam āpannaḥ svabhāvaṃ duṣṭam āsthitaḥc svabhāvāt pāpam anveti tṛṇais tunna ivoragaḥa duryodhano hi yat senaḥ sarvathā viditas tavac yacchīlo yatsvabhāvaś ca yadbalo yatparākramaḥa purā prasannāḥ kuravaḥ sahaputrās tathā vayamc indrajyeṣṭhā ivābhūma modamānāḥ sabāndhavāḥa duryodhanasya krodhena bhāratā madhusūdanac dhakṣyante śiśirāpāye vanānīva hutāśanaiḥa aṣṭādaśeme rājānaḥ prakhyātā madhusūdanac ye samuccicchidur jñātīn suhṛdaś ca sabāndhavāna asurāṇāṃ samṛddhānāṃ jvalatām iva tejasāc paryāyakāle dharmasya prāpte balir ajāyataa haihayānām udāvarto nīpānāṃ janamejayaḥc bahulas tālajaṅghānāṃ kṛmīṇām uddhato vasuḥa ajabinduḥ suvīrāṇāṃ surāṣṭrāṇāṃ kuśarddhikaḥc arkajaś ca balīhānāṃ cīnānāṃ dhautamūlakaḥa hayagrīvo videhānāṃ varapraś ca mahaujasāmc bāhuḥ sundaravegānāṃ dīptākṣāṇāṃ purūravāḥa sahajaś cedimatsyānāṃ pracetānāṃ bṛhadbalaḥc dhāraṇaś cendravatsānāṃ mukuṭānāṃ vigāhanaḥa śamaś ca nandivegānām ity ete kulapāṃsanāḥc yugānte kṛṣṇa saṃbhūtāḥ kuleṣu puruṣādhamāḥa apy ayaṃ naḥ kurūṇāṃ syād yugānte kālasaṃbhṛtaḥc duryodhanaḥ kulāṅgāro jaghanyaḥ pāpapūruṣaḥa tasmān mṛdu śanair enaṃ brūyā dharmārthasaṃhitamc kāmānubandhabahulaṃ nogram ugraparākramama api duryodhanaṃ kṛṣṇa sarve vayam adhaścarāḥc nīcair bhūtvānuyāsyāmo mā sma no bharatā naśana apy udāsīnavṛttiḥ syād yathā naḥ kurubhiḥ sahac vāsudeva tathā kāryaṃ na kurūn anayaḥ spṛśeta vācyaḥ pitāmaho vṛddho ye ca kṛṣṇa sabhāsadaḥc bhrātṝṇām astu saubhrātraṃ dhārtarāṣṭraḥ praśāmyatāma aham etad bravīmy evaṃ rājā caiva praśaṃsatic arjuno naiva yuddhārthī bhūyasī hi dayārjune vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa etac chrutvā mahābāhuḥ keśavaḥ prahasann ivac abhūtapūrvaṃ bhīmasya mārdavopagataṃ vacaḥa girer iva laghutvaṃ tac chītatvam iva pāvakec matvā rāmānujaḥ śauriḥ śārṅgadhanvā vṛkodarama saṃtejayaṃs tadā vāgbhir mātariśveva pāvakamc uvāca bhīmam āsīnaṃ kṛpayābhipariplutama tvam anyadā bhīmasena yuddham eva praśaṃsasic vadhābhinandinaḥ krūrān dhārtarāṣṭrān mimardiṣuḥa na ca svapiṣi jāgarṣi nyubjaḥ śeṣe paraṃtapac ghorām aśāntāṃ ruśatīṃ sadā vācaṃ prabhāṣasea niḥśvasann agnivarṇena saṃtaptaḥ svena manyunāc apraśāntamanā bhīma sadhūma iva pāvakaḥa ekānte niṣṭanañ śeṣe bhārārta iva durbalaḥc api tvāṃ ke cid unmattaṃ manyante tadvido janāḥa ārujya vṛkṣān nirmūlān gajaḥ paribhujann ivac nighnan padbhiḥ kṣitiṃ bhīma niṣṭanan paridhāvasia nāsmiñ jane bhiramase rahaḥ kṣiyasi pāṇḍavac nānyaṃ niśi divā vāpi kadā cid abhinandasia akasmāt smayamānaś ca rahasy āsse rudann ivac jānvor mūrdhānam ādhāya ciram āsse pramīlitaḥa bhrukuṭiṃ ca punaḥ kurvann oṣṭhau ca vilihann ivac abhīkṣṇaṃ dṛśyase bhīma sarvaṃ tan manyukāritama yathā purastāt savitā dṛśyate śukram uccaranc yathā ca paścān nirmukto dhruvaṃ paryeti raśmivāna tathā satyaṃ bravīmy etan nāsti tasya vyatikramaḥc hantāhaṃ gadayābhyetya duryodhanam amarṣaṇama iti sma madhye bhrātṝṇāṃ satyenālabhase gadāmc tasya te praśame buddhir dhīyate dya paraṃtapaa aho yuddhapratīpāni yuddhakāla upasthitec paśyasīvāpratīpāni kiṃ tvāṃ bhīr bhīma vindatia aho pārtha nimittāni viparītāni paśyasic svapnānte jāgarānte ca tasmāt praśamam icchasia aho nāśaṃsase kiṃ cit puṃstvaṃ klība ivātmanic kaśmalenābhipanno si tena te vikṛtaṃ manaḥa udvepate te hṛdayaṃ manas te praviṣīdatic ūrustambhagṛhīto si tasmāt praśamam icchasia anityaṃ kila martyasya cittaṃ pārtha calācalamc vātavegapracalitā aṣṭhīlā śālmaler ivaa tavaiṣā vikṛtā buddhir gavāṃ vāg iva mānuṣīc manāṃsi pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ majjayaty aplavān ivaa idaṃ me mahad āścaryaṃ parvatasyeva sarpaṇamc yadīdṛśaṃ prabhāṣethā bhīmasenāsamaṃ vacaḥa sa dṛṣṭvā svāni karmāṇi kule janma ca bhāratac uttiṣṭhasva viṣādaṃ mā kṛthā vīra sthiro bhavaa na caitad anurūpaṃ te yat te glānir ariṃdamac yad ojasā na labhate kṣatriyo na tad aśnute vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tathokto vāsudevena nityamanyur amarṣaṇaḥc sadaśvavat samādhāvad babhāṣe tadanantarama anyathā māṃ cikīrṣantam anyathā manyase cyutac praṇītabhāvam atyantaṃ yudhi satyaparākramama vettha dāśārha sattvaṃ me dīrghakālaṃ sahoṣitaḥc uta vā māṃ na jānāsi plavan hrada ivālpavaḥe tasmād apratirūpābhir vāgbhir māṃ tvaṃ samarchasia kathaṃ hi bhīmasenaṃ māṃ jānan kaś cana mādhavac brūyād apratirūpāṇi yathā māṃ vaktum arhasia tasmād idaṃ pravakṣyāmi vacanaṃ vṛṣṇinandanac ātmanaḥ pauruṣaṃ caiva balaṃ ca na samaṃ paraiḥa sarvathā nāryakarmaitat praśaṃsā svayam ātmanaḥc ativādāpaviddhas tu vakṣyāmi balam ātmanaḥa paśyeme rodasī kṛṣṇa yayor āsann imāḥ prajāḥc acale cāpy anante ca pratiṣṭhe sarvamātaraua yadīme sahasā kruddhe sameyātāṃ śile ivac aham ete nigṛhṇīyāṃ bāhubhyāṃ sacarācarea paśyaitad antaraṃ bāhvor mahāparighayor ivac ya etat prāpya mucyeta na taṃ paśyāmi pūruṣama himavāṃś ca samudraś ca vajrī ca balabhit svayamc mayābhipannaṃ trāyeran balam āsthāya na trayaḥa yudhyeyaṃ kṣatriyān sarvān pāṇḍaveṣv ātatāyinaḥc adhaḥ pādatalenaitān adhiṣṭhāsyāmi bhūtalea na hi tvaṃ nābhijānāsi mama vikramam acyutac yathā mayā vinirjitya rājāno vaśagāḥ kṛtāḥa atha cen māṃ na jānāsi sūryasyevodyataḥ prabhāmc vigāḍhe yudhi saṃbādhe vetsyase māṃ janārdanaa kiṃ mātyavākṣīḥ paruṣair vraṇaṃ sūcyā ivānaghac yathāmati bravīmy etad viddhi mām adhikaṃ tataḥa draṣṭāsi yudhi saṃbādhe pravṛtte vaiśase hanic mayā praṇunnān mātaṅgān rathinaḥ sādinas tathāa tathā narān abhikruddhaṃ nighnantaṃ kṣatriyarṣabhānc draṣṭā māṃ tvaṃ ca lokaś ca vikarṣantaṃ varān varāna na me sīdanti majjāno na mamodvepate manaḥc sarvalokād abhikruddhān na bhayaṃ vidyate mamaa kiṃ tu sauhṛdam evaitat kṛpayā madhusūdanac sarvāṃs titikṣe saṃkleśān mā sma no bharatā naśan bhagavān uvācaa bhāvaṃ jijñāsamāno haṃ praṇayād idam abruvamc na cākṣepān na pāṇḍityān na krodhān na vivakṣayāa vedāhaṃ tava māhātmyam uta te veda yad balamc uta te veda karmāṇi na tvāṃ paribhavāmy ahama yathā cātmani kalyāṇaṃ saṃbhāvayasi pāṇḍavac sahasraguṇam apy etat tvayi saṃbhāvayāmy ahama yādṛśe ca kule janma sarvarājābhipūjitec bandhubhiś ca suhṛdbhiś ca bhīma tvam asi tādṛśaḥa jijñāsanto hi dharmasya saṃdigdhasya vṛkodarac paryāyaṃ na vyavasyanti daivamānuṣayor janāḥa sa eva hetur bhūtvā hi puruṣasyārthasiddhiṣuc vināśe pi sa evāsya saṃdigdhaṃ karma pauruṣama anyathā paridṛṣṭāni kavibhir doṣadarśibhiḥc anyathā parivartante vegā iva nabhasvataḥa sumantritaṃ sunītaṃ ca nyāyataś copapāditamc kṛtaṃ mānuṣyakaṃ karma daivenāpi virudhyatea daivam apy akṛtaṃ karma pauruṣeṇa vihanyatec śītam uṣṇaṃ tathā varṣaṃ kṣutpipāse ca bhārataa yad anyad diṣṭabhāvasya puruṣasya svayaṃkṛtamc tasmād anavarodhaś ca vidyate tatra lakṣaṇama lokasya nānyato vṛttiḥ pāṇḍavānyatra karmaṇaḥb bāhuśālin mahāvīrya bhīmasena vicakṣaṇab   mātrā syād avadhāraṇec evaṃbuddhiḥ pravarteta phalaṃ syād ubhayānvayāta ya evaṃ kṛtabuddhiḥ san karmasv eva pravartatec nāsiddhau vyathate tasya na siddhau harṣam aśnutea tatreyam arthamātrā me bhīmasena vivakṣitāc naikāntasiddhir mantavyā kurubhiḥ saha saṃyugea nātipraṇītaraśmiḥ syāt tathā bhavati paryayec viṣādam arched glāniṃ vā etadarthaṃ bravīmi tea śvobhūte dhṛtarāṣṭrasya samīpaṃ prāpya pāṇḍavac yatiṣye praśamaṃ kartuṃ yuṣmadartham ahāpayana śamaṃ cet te kariṣyanti tato nantaṃ yaśo mamac bhavatāṃ ca kṛtaḥ kāmas teṣāṃ ca śreya uttamama te ced abhinivekṣyanti nābhyupaiṣyanti me vacaḥc kuravo yuddham evātra raudraṃ karma bhaviṣyatia asmin yuddhe bhīmasena tvayi bhāraḥ samāhitaḥc dhūr arjunena dhāryā syād voḍhavya itaro janaḥa ahaṃ hi yantā bībhatsor bhavitā saṃyuge satic dhanaṃjayasyaiṣa kāmo na hi yuddhaṃ na kāmayea tasmād āśaṅkamāno haṃ vṛkodara matiṃ tavac tudann aklībayā vācā tejas te samadīpayam arjuna uvācaa uktaṃ yudhiṣṭhireṇaiva yāvad vācyaṃ janārdanac tava vākyaṃ tu me śrutvā pratibhāti paraṃtapaa naiva praśamam atra tvaṃ manyase sukaraṃ prabhoc lobhād vā dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dainyād vā samupasthitāta aphalaṃ manyase cāpi puruṣasya parākramamc na cāntareṇa karmāṇi pauruṣeṇa phalodayaḥa tad idaṃ bhāṣitaṃ vākyaṃ tathā ca na tathaiva cac na caitad evaṃ draṣṭavyam asādhyam iti kiṃ canaa kiṃ caitan manyase kṛcchram asmākaṃ pāpam āditaḥc kurvanti teṣāṃ karmāṇi yeṣāṃ nāsti phalodayaḥa saṃpādyamānaṃ samyak ca syāt karma saphalaṃ prabhoc sa tathā kṛṣṇa vartasva yathā śarma bhavet paraiḥa pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca bhavān paramakaḥ suhṛtc surāṇām asurāṇāṃ ca yathā vīra prajāpatiḥa kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca pratipatsva nirāmayamc asmaddhitam anuṣṭhātuṃ na manye tava duṣkarama evaṃ cet kāryatām eti kāryaṃ tava janārdanac gamanād evam eva tvaṃ kariṣyasi na saṃśayaḥa cikīrṣitam athānyat te tasmin vīra durātmanic bhaviṣyati tathā sarvaṃ yathā tava cikīrṣitama śarma taiḥ saha vā no stu tava vā yac cikīrṣitamc vicāryamāṇo yaḥ kāmas tava kṛṣṇa sa no guruḥa na sa nārhati duṣṭātmā vadhaṃ sasutabāndhavaḥc yena dharmasute dṛṣṭvā na sā śrīr upamarṣitāa yac cāpy apaśyatopāyaṃ dharmiṣṭhaṃ madhusūdanac upāyena nṛśaṃsena hṛtā durdyūtadevināa kathaṃ hi puruṣo jātaḥ kṣatriyeṣu dhanurdharaḥc samāhūto nivarteta prāṇatyāge py upasthitea adharmeṇa jitān dṛṣṭvā vane pravrajitāṃs tathāc vadhyatāṃ mama vārṣṇeya nirgato sau suyodhanaḥa na caitad adbhutaṃ kṛṣṇa mitrārthe yac cikīrṣasic kriyā kathaṃ nu mukhyā syān mṛdunā vetareṇa vāa atha vā manyase jyāyān vadhas teṣām anantaramc tad eva kriyatām āśu na vicāryam atas tvayāa jānāsi hi yathā tena draupadī pāpabuddhināc parikliṣṭā sabhāmadhye tac ca tasyāpi marṣitama sa nāma samyag varteta pāṇḍaveṣv iti mādhavac na me saṃjāyate buddhir bījam uptam ivoṣarea tasmād yan manyase yuktaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca yad dhitamc tad āśu kuru vārṣṇeya yan naḥ kāryam anantaram bhagavān uvācaa evam etan mahābāho yathā vadasi pāṇḍavab pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca pratipatsye nirāmayamc sarvaṃ tv idaṃ samāyattaṃ bībhatso karmaṇor dvayoḥa kṣetraṃ hi rasavac chuddhaṃ karṣakeṇopapāditamc ṛte varṣaṃ na kaunteya jātu nirvartayet phalama tatra vai pauruṣaṃ brūyur āsekaṃ yatnakāritamc tatra cāpi dhruvaṃ paśyec choṣaṇaṃ daivakāritama tad idaṃ niścitaṃ buddhyā pūrvair api mahātmabhiḥc daive ca mānuṣe caiva saṃyuktaṃ lokakāraṇama ahaṃ hi tat kariṣyāmi paraṃ puruṣakārataḥc daivaṃ tu na mayā śakyaṃ karma kartuṃ kathaṃ canaa sa hi dharmaṃ ca satyaṃ ca tyaktvā carati durmatiḥc na hi saṃtapyate tena tathārūpeṇa karmaṇāa tāṃ cāpi buddhiṃ pāpiṣṭhāṃ vardhayanty asya mantriṇaḥc śakuniḥ sūtaputraś ca bhrātā duḥśāsanas tathāa sa hi tyāgena rājyasya na śamaṃ samupeṣyatic antareṇa vadhāt pārtha sānubandhaḥ suyodhanaḥa na cāpi praṇipātena tyaktum icchati dharmarāṭc yācyamānas tu rājyaṃ sa na pradāsyati durmatiḥa na tu manye sa tad vācyo yad yudhiṣṭhiraśāsanamc uktaṃ prayojanaṃ tatra dharmarājena bhārataa tathā pāpas tu tat sarvaṃ na kariṣyati kauravaḥc tasmiṃś cākriyamāṇe sau lokavadhyo bhaviṣyatia mama cāpi sa vadhyo vai jagataś cāpi bhāratac yena kaumārake yūyaṃ sarve viprakṛtās tathāa vipraluptaṃ ca vo rājyaṃ nṛśaṃsena durātmanāc na copaśāmyate pāpaḥ śriyaṃ dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhirea asakṛc cāpy ahaṃ tena tvatkṛte pārtha bheditaḥc na mayā tad gṛhītaṃ ca pāpaṃ tasya cikīrṣitama jānāsi hi mahābāho tvam apy asya paraṃ matamc priyaṃ cikīrṣamāṇaṃ ca dharmarājasya mām apia sa jānaṃs tasya cātmānaṃ mama caiva paraṃ matamc ajānann iva cākasmād arjunādyābhiśaṅkasea yac cāpi paramaṃ divyaṃ tac cāpy avagataṃ tvayāc vidhānavihitaṃ pārtha kathaṃ śarma bhavet paraiḥa yat tu vācā mayā śakyaṃ karmaṇā cāpi pāṇḍavac kariṣye tad ahaṃ pārtha na tv āśaṃse śamaṃ paraiḥa kathaṃ goharaṇe brūyād icchañ śarma tathāvidhamc yācyamāno pi bhīṣmeṇa saṃvatsaragate dhvania tadaiva te parābhūtā yadā saṃkalpitās tvayāc lavaśaḥ kṣaṇaśaś cāpi na ca tuṣṭaḥ suyodhanaḥa sarvathā tu mayā kāryaṃ dharmarājasya śāsanamc vibhāvyaṃ tasya bhūyaś ca karma pāpaṃ durātmanaḥ nakula uvācaa uktaṃ bahuvidhaṃ vākyaṃ dharmarājena mādhavac dharmajñena vadānyena dharmayuktaṃ ca tattvataḥa matam ājñāya rājñaś ca bhīmasenena mādhavac saṃśamo bāhuvīryaṃ ca khyāpitaṃ mādhavātmanaḥa tathaiva phalgunenāpi yad uktaṃ tat tvayā śrutamc ātmanaś ca mataṃ vīra kathitaṃ bhavatāsakṛta sarvam etad atikramya śrutvā paramataṃ bhavānc yat prāptakālaṃ manyethās tat kuryāḥ puruṣottamaa tasmiṃs tasmin nimitte hi mataṃ bhavati keśavac prāptakālaṃ manuṣyeṇa svayaṃ kāryam ariṃdamaa anyathā cintito hy arthaḥ punar bhavati so nyathāc anityamatayo loke narāḥ puruṣasattamaa anyathā buddhayo hy āsann asmāsu vanavāsiṣuc adṛśyeṣv anyathā kṛṣṇa dṛśyeṣu punar anyathāa asmākam api vārṣṇeya vane vicaratāṃ tadāc na tathā praṇayo rājye yathā saṃprati vartatea nivṛttavanavāsān naḥ śrutvā vīra samāgatāḥc akṣauhiṇyo hi saptemās tvatprasādāj janārdanaa imān hi puruṣavyāghrān acintyabalapauruṣānc āttaśastrān raṇe dṛṣṭvā na vyathed iha kaḥ pumāna sa bhavān kurumadhye taṃ sāntvapūrvaṃ bhayānvitamc brūyād vākyaṃ yathā mando na vyatheta suyodhanaḥa yudhiṣṭhiraṃ bhīmasenaṃ bībhatsuṃ cāparājitamc sahadevaṃ ca māṃ caiva tvāṃ ca rāmaṃ ca keśavaa sātyakiṃ ca mahāvīryaṃ virāṭaṃ ca sahātmajamc drupadaṃ ca sahāmātyaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatama kāśirājaṃ ca vikrāntaṃ dhṛṣṭaketuṃ ca cedipamc māṃsaśoṇitabhṛn martyaḥ pratiyudhyeta ko yudhia sa bhavān gamanād eva sādhayiṣyaty asaṃśayamc iṣṭam arthaṃ mahābāho dharmarājasya kevalama viduraś caiva bhīṣmaś ca droṇaś ca sahabāhlikaḥc śreyaḥ samarthā vijñātum ucyamānaṃ tvayānaghaa te cainam anuneṣyanti dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janādhipamc taṃ ca pāpasamācāraṃ sahāmātyaṃ suyodhanama śrotā cārthasya viduras tvaṃ ca vaktā janārdanac kam ivārthaṃ vivartantaṃ sthāpayetāṃ na vartmani sahadeva uvācaa yad etat kathitaṃ rājñā dharma eṣa sanātanaḥc yathā tu yuddham eva syāt tathā kāryam ariṃdamaa yadi praśamam iccheyuḥ kuravaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahac tathāpi yuddhaṃ dāśārha yojayethāḥ sahaiva taiḥa kathaṃ nu dṛṣṭvā pāñcālīṃ tathā kliṣṭāṃ sabhāgatāmc avadhena praśāmyeta mama manyuḥ suyodhanea yadi bhīmārjunau kṛṣṇa dharmarājaś ca dhārmikaḥc dharmam utsṛjya tenāhaṃ yoddhum icchāmi saṃyuged brūhi madvacanaṃ kṛṣṇa suyodhanam apaṇḍitamd kṛcchre vane vā vastavyaṃ pure vā nāgasāhvaye sātyakir uvācaa satyam āha mahābāho sahadevo mahāmatiḥc duryodhanavadhe śāntis tasya kopasya me bhaveta jānāsi hi yathā dṛṣṭvā cīrājinadharān vanec tavāpi manyur udbhūto duḥkhitān prekṣya pāṇḍavāna tasmān mādrīsutaḥ śūro yad āha puruṣarṣabhaḥc vacanaṃ sarvayodhānāṃ tan mataṃ puruṣottama vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa evaṃ vadati vākyaṃ tu yuyudhāne mahāmatauc subhīmaḥ siṃhanādo bhūd yodhānāṃ tatra sarvaśaḥa sarve hi sarvato vīrās tad vacaḥ pratyapūjayanc sādhu sādhv iti śaineyaṃ harṣayanto yuyutsavaḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa rājñas tu vacanaṃ śrutvā dharmārthasahitaṃ hitamc kṛṣṇā dāśārham āsīnam abravīc chokakarṣitāa sutā drupadarājasya svasitāyatamūrdhajāc saṃpūjya sahadevaṃ ca sātyakiṃ ca mahārathama bhīmasenaṃ ca saṃśāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā paramadurmanāḥc aśrupūrṇekṣaṇā vākyam uvācedaṃ manasvinīa viditaṃ te mahābāho dharmajña madhusūdanac yathā nikṛtim āsthāya bhraṃśitāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ sukhāta dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putreṇa sāmātyena janārdanac yathā ca saṃjayo rājñā mantraṃ rahasi śrāvitaḥa yudhiṣṭhireṇa dāśārha tac cāpi viditaṃ tavac yathoktaḥ saṃjayaś caiva tac ca sarvaṃ śrutaṃ tvayāa pañca nas tāta dīyantāṃ grāmā iti mahādyutec kuśasthalaṃ vṛkasthalam āsandī vāraṇāvatama avasānaṃ mahābāho kiṃ cid eva tu pañcamamc iti duryodhano vācyaḥ suhṛdaś cāsya keśavaa tac cāpi nākarod vākyaṃ śrutvā kṛṣṇa suyodhanaḥc yudhiṣṭhirasya dāśārha hrīmataḥ saṃdhim icchataḥa apradānena rājyasya yadi kṛṣṇa suyodhanaḥc saṃdhim icchen na kartavyas tatra gatvā kathaṃ canaa śakṣyanti hi mahābāho pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ sahac dhārtarāṣṭrabalaṃ ghoraṃ kruddhaṃ pratisamāsituma na hi sāmnā na dānena śakyo rthas teṣu kaś canac tasmāt teṣu na kartavyā kṛpā te madhusūdanaa sāmnā dānena vā kṛṣṇa ye na śāmyanti śatravaḥc moktavyas teṣu daṇḍaḥ syāj jīvitaṃ parirakṣatāa tasmāt teṣu mahādaṇḍaḥ kṣeptavyaḥ kṣipram acyutac tvayā caiva mahābāho pāṇḍavaiḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥa etat samarthaṃ pārthānāṃ tava caiva yaśaskaramc kriyamāṇaṃ bhavet kṛṣṇa kṣatrasya ca sukhāvahama kṣatriyeṇa hi hantavyaḥ kṣatriyo lobham āsthitaḥc akṣatriyo vā dāśārha svadharmam anutiṣṭhatāa anyatra brāhmaṇāt tāta sarvapāpeṣv avasthitātc gurur hi sarvavarṇānāṃ brāhmaṇaḥ prasṛtāgrabhuka yathāvadhye bhaved doṣo vadhyamāne janārdanac sa vadhyasyāvadhe dṛṣṭa iti dharmavido viduḥa yathā tvāṃ na spṛśed eṣa doṣaḥ kṛṣṇa tathā kuruc pāṇḍavaiḥ saha dāśārha sṛñjayaiś ca sasainikaiḥa punar uktaṃ ca vakṣyāmi viśrambheṇa janārdanac kā nu sīmantinī mādṛk pṛthivyām asti keśavaa sutā drupadarājasya vedimadhyāt samutthitāc dhṛṣṭadyumnasya bhaginī tava kṛṣṇa priyā sakhīa ājamīḍhakulaṃ prāptā snuṣā pāṇḍor mahātmanaḥc mahiṣī pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ pañcendrasamavarcasāma sutā me pañcabhir vīraiḥ pañca jātā mahārathāḥc abhimanyur yathā kṛṣṇa tathā te tava dharmataḥa sāhaṃ keśagrahaṃ prāptā parikliṣṭā sabhāṃ gatāc paśyatāṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ tvayi jīvati keśavaa jīvatsu kauraveyeṣu pāñcāleṣv atha vṛṣṇiṣuc dāsībhūtāsmi pāpānāṃ sabhāmadhye vyavasthitāa nirāmarṣeṣv aceṣṭeṣu prekṣamāṇeṣu pāṇḍuṣuc trāhi mām iti govinda manasā kāṅkṣito si mea yatra māṃ bhagavān rājā śvaśuro vākyam abravītc varaṃ vṛṇīṣva pāñcāli varārhāsi matāsi mea adāsāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ santu sarathāḥ sāyudhā itic mayokte yatra nirmuktā vanavāsāya keśavaa evaṃvidhānāṃ duḥkhānām abhijño si janārdanac trāhi māṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa sabhartṛjñātibāndhavāma nanv ahaṃ kṛṣṇa bhīṣmasya dhṛtarāṣṭrasya cobhayoḥc snuṣā bhavāmi dharmeṇa sāhaṃ dāsīkṛtābhavama dhig balaṃ bhīmasenasya dhik pārthasya dhanuṣmatāmc yatra duryodhanaḥ kṛṣṇa muhūrtam api jīvatia yadi te ham anugrāhyā yadi te sti kṛpā mayic dhārtarāṣṭreṣu vai kopaḥ sarvaḥ kṛṣṇa vidhīyatāma ity uktvā mṛdusaṃhāraṃ vṛjināgraṃ sudarśanamc sunīlam asitāpāṅgī puṇyagandhādhivāsitama sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ mahābhujagavarcasamc keśapakṣaṃ varārohā gṛhya savyena pāṇināa padmākṣī puṇḍarīkākṣam upetya gajagāminīc aśrupūrṇekṣaṇā kṛṣṇā kṛṣṇaṃ vacanam abravīta ayaṃ te puṇḍarīkākṣa duḥśāsanakaroddhṛtaḥc smartavyaḥ sarvakāleṣu pareṣāṃ saṃdhim icchatāa yadi bhīmārjunau kṛṣṇa kṛpaṇau saṃdhikāmukauc pitā me yotsyate vṛddhaḥ saha putrair mahārathaiḥa pañca caiva mahāvīryāḥ putrā me madhusūdanac abhimanyuṃ puraskṛtya yotsyanti kurubhiḥ sahaa duḥśāsanabhujaṃ śyāmaṃ saṃchinnaṃ pāṃsuguṇṭhitamc yady ahaṃ taṃ na paśyāmi kā śāntir hṛdayasya mea trayodaśa hi varṣāṇi pratīkṣantyā gatāni mec nidhāya hṛdaye manyuṃ pradīptam iva pāvakama vidīryate me hṛdayaṃ bhīmavākśalyapīḍitamc yo yam adya mahābāhur dharmaṃ samanupaśyatia ity uktvā bāṣpasannena kaṇṭhenāyatalocanāc ruroda kṛṣṇā sotkampaṃ sasvaraṃ bāṣpagadgadama stanau pīnāyataśroṇī sahitāv abhivarṣatīc dravībhūtam ivātyuṣṇam utsṛjad vāri netrajama tām uvāca mahābāhuḥ keśavaḥ parisāntvayanc acirād drakṣyase kṛṣṇe rudatīr bharatastriyaḥa evaṃ tā bhīru rotsyanti nihatajñātibāndhavāḥc hatamitrā hatabalā yeṣāṃ kruddhāsi bhāminia ahaṃ ca tat kariṣyāmi bhīmārjunayamaiḥ sahac yudhiṣṭhiraniyogena daivāc ca vidhinirmitāta dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ kālapakvā na cec chṛṇvanti me vacaḥc śeṣyante nihatā bhūmau śvaśṛgālādanīkṛtāḥa caled dhi himavāñ śailo medinī śatadhā bhavetc dyauḥ patec ca sanakṣatrā na me moghaṃ vaco bhavetd dyauḥ patet pṛthivī śīryed dhimavāñ chithilībhavetd śuṣyet toyanidhiḥ kṛṣṇe na me moghaṃ vaco bhaveta satyaṃ te pratijānāmi kṛṣṇe bāṣpo nigṛhyatāmc hatāmitrāñ śriyā yuktān acirād drakṣyase patīn arjuna uvācaa kurūṇām adya sarveṣāṃ bhavān suhṛd anuttamaḥc saṃbandhī dayito nityam ubhayoḥ pakṣayor apia pāṇḍavair dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ pratipādyam anāmayamc samarthaḥ praśamaṃ caiṣāṃ kartuṃ tvam asi keśavaa tvam itaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣa suyodhanam amarṣaṇamc śāntyarthaṃ bhārataṃ brūyā yat tad vācyam amitrahana tvayā dharmārthayuktaṃ ced uktaṃ śivam anāmayamc hitaṃ nādāsyate bālo diṣṭasya vaśam eṣyati bhagavān uvācaa dharmyam asmaddhitaṃ caiva kurūṇāṃ yad anāmayamc eṣa yāsyāmi rājānaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭram abhīpsayā vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tato vyapete tamasi sūrye vimala udgatec maitre muhūrte saṃprāpte mṛdvarciṣi divākarea kaumude māsi revatyāṃ śaradante himāgamec sphītasasyasukhe kāle kalyaḥ sattvavatāṃ varaḥa maṅgalyāḥ puṇyanirghoṣā vācaḥ śṛṇvaṃś ca sūnṛtāḥc brāhmaṇānāṃ pratītānām ṛṣīṇām iva vāsavaḥa kṛtvā paurvāhṇikaṃ kṛtyaṃ snātaḥ śucir alaṃkṛtaḥc upatasthe vivasvantaṃ pāvakaṃ ca janārdanaḥa ṛṣabhaṃ pṛṣṭha ālabhya brāhmaṇān abhivādya cac agniṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā paśyan kalyāṇam agrataḥa tat pratijñāya vacanaṃ pāṇḍavasya janārdanaḥc śiner naptāram āsīnam abhyabhāṣata sātyakima ratha āropyatāṃ śaṅkhaś cakraṃ ca gadayā sahac upāsaṅgāś ca govindaṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥc rājñāṃ sakāśe dyutimān uvācedaṃ vacas tadāa yo naiva kāmān na bhayān na lobhān nārthakāraṇātc anyāyam anuvarteta sthirabuddhir alolupaḥa dharmajño dhṛtimān prājñaḥ bhīṣmādayaḥ sarve dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janādhipamc ūcuḥ paramam ity evaṃ pūjayanto sya tad vacaḥa teṣām anumataṃ jñātvā rājā duryodhanas tadāc sabhāvāstūni ramyāṇi pradeṣṭum upacakramea tato deśeṣu deśeṣu ramaṇīyeṣu bhāgaśaḥc sarvaratnasamākīrṇāḥ sabhāś cakrur anekaśaḥa āsanāni vicitrāṇi yuktāni vividhair guṇaiḥc striyo gandhān alaṃkārān sūkṣmāṇi vasanāni caa guṇavanty annapānāni bhojyāni vividhāni cac mālyāni ca sugandhīni tāni rājā dadau tataḥa viśeṣataś ca vāsārthaṃ sabhāṃ grāme vṛkasthalec vidadhe kauravo rājā bahuratnāṃ manoramāma etad vidhāya vai sarvaṃ devārham atimānuṣamc ācakhyau dhṛtarāṣṭrāya rājā duryodhanas tadāa tāḥ sabhāḥ keśavaḥ sarvā ratnāni vividhāni cac asamīkṣyaiva dāśārha upāyāt kurusadma tat dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa upaplavyād iha kṣattar upayāto janārdanaḥc vṛkasthale nivasati sa ca prātar iheṣyatia āhukānām adhipatiḥ purogaḥ sarvasātvatāmc mahāmanā mahāvīryo mahāmātro janārdanaḥa sphītasya vṛṣṇivaṃśasya bhartā goptā ca mādhavaḥc trayāṇām api lokānāṃ bhagavān prapitāmahaḥa vṛṣṇyandhakāḥ sumanaso yasya prajñām upāsatec ādityā vasavo rudrā yathā buddhiṃ bṛhaspateḥa tasmai pūjāṃ prayokṣyāmi dāśārhāya mahātmanec pratyakṣaṃ tava dharmajña tan me kathayataḥ śṛṇua ekavarṇaiḥ sukṛṣṇāṅgair bāhlijātair hayottamaiḥc caturyuktān rathāṃs tasmai raukmān dāsyāmi ṣoḍaśaa nityaprabhinnān mātaṅgān īṣādantān prahāriṇaḥc aṣṭānucaram ekaikam aṣṭau dāsyāmi keśavea dāsīnām aprajātānāṃ śubhānāṃ rukmavarcasāmc śatam asmai pradāsyāmi dāsānām api tāvataḥa āvikaṃ bahu susparśaṃ pārvatīyair upāhṛtamc tad apy asmai pradāsyāmi sahasrāṇi daśāṣṭa caa ajinānāṃ sahasrāṇi cīnadeśodbhavāni cac tāny apy asmai pradāsyāmi yāvad arhati keśavaḥa divā rātrau ca bhāty eṣa sutejā vimalo maṇiḥc tam apy asmai pradāsyāmi tam apy arhati keśavaḥa ekenāpi pataty ahnā yojanāni caturdaśac yānam aśvatarīyuktaṃ dāsye tasmai tad apy ahama yāvanti vāhanāny asya yāvantaḥ puruṣāś ca tec tato ṣṭaguṇam apy asmai bhojyaṃ dāsyāmy ahaṃ sadāa mama putrāś ca pautrāś ca sarve duryodhanād ṛtec pratyudyāsyanti dāśārhaṃ rathair mṛṣṭair alaṃkṛtāḥa svalaṃkṛtāś ca kalyāṇyaḥ pādair eva sahasraśaḥc vāramukhyā mahābhāgaṃ pratyudyāsyanti keśavama nagarād api yāḥ kāś cid gamiṣyanti janārdanamc draṣṭuṃ kanyāś ca kalyāṇyas tāś ca yāsyanty anāvṛtāḥa sastrīpuruṣabālaṃ hi nagaraṃ madhusūdanamc udīkṣate mahātmānaṃ bhānumantam iva prajāḥa mahādhvajapatākāś ca kriyantāṃ sarvatodiśamc jalāvasikto virajāḥ panthās tasyeti cānvaśāta duḥśāsanasya ca gṛhaṃ duryodhanagṛhād varamc tad asya kriyatāṃ kṣipraṃ susaṃmṛṣṭam alaṃkṛtama etad dhi rucirākāraiḥ prāsādair upaśobhitamc śivaṃ ca ramaṇīyaṃ ca sarvartu sumahādhanama sarvam asmin gṛhe ratnaṃ mama duryodhanasya cac yad yad arhet sa vārṣṇeyas tat tad deyam asaṃśayam vidura uvācaa rājan bahumataś cāsi trailokyasyāpi sattamaḥc saṃbhāvitaś ca lokasya saṃmataś cāsi bhārataa yat tvam evaṃgate brūyāḥ paścime vayasi sthitaḥc śāstrād vā supratarkād vā susthiraḥ sthaviro hy asia lekhāśmanīva bhāḥ sūrye mahormir iva sāgarec dharmas tvayi mahān rājann iti vyavasitāḥ prajāḥa sadaiva bhāvito loko guṇaughais tava pārthivac guṇānāṃ rakṣaṇe nityaṃ prayatasva sabāndhavaḥa ārjavaṃ pratipadyasva mā bālyād bahudhā naśīḥc rājyaṃ putrāṃś ca pautrāṃś ca suhṛdaś cāpi supriyāna yat tvaṃ ditsasi kṛṣṇāya rājann atithaye bahuc etad anyac ca dāśārhaḥ pṛthivīm api cārhatia na tu tvaṃ dharmam uddiśya tasya vā priyakāraṇātc etad icchasi kṛṣṇāya satyenātmānam ālabhea māyaiṣātattvam evaitac chadmaitad bhūridakṣiṇac jānāmi te mataṃ rājan gūḍhaṃ bāhyena karmaṇāa pañca pañcaiva lipsanti grāmakān pāṇḍavā nṛpac na ca ditsasi tebhyas tāṃs tac chamaṃ kaḥ kariṣyatia arthena tu mahābāhuṃ vārṣṇeyaṃ tvaṃ jihīrṣasic anenaivābhyupāyena pāṇḍavebhyo bibhitsasia na ca vittena śakyo sau nodyamena na garhayāc anyo dhanaṃjayāt kartum etat tattvaṃ bravīmi tea veda kṛṣṇasya māhātmyaṃ vedāsya dṛḍhabhaktitāmc atyājyam asya jānāmi prāṇais tulyaṃ dhanaṃjayama anyat kumbhād apāṃ pūrṇād anyat pādāvasecanātc anyat kuśalasaṃpraśnān naiṣiṣyati janārdanaḥa yat tv asya priyam ātithyaṃ mānārhasya mahātmanaḥc tad asmai kriyatāṃ rājan mānārho hi janārdanaḥa āśaṃsamānaḥ kalyāṇaṃ kurūn abhyeti keśavaḥc yenaiva rājann arthena tad evāsmā upākurua śamam icchati dāśārhas tava duryodhanasya cac pāṇḍavānāṃ ca rājendra tad asya vacanaṃ kurua pitāsi rājan putrās te vṛddhas tvaṃ śiśavaḥ parec vartasva pitṛvat teṣu vartante te hi putravatd nirvairān matsyapāñcālān pāṇḍavān kurubhiḥ sahad kṛtvā sukhaṃ yathādharmaṃ kīrtiṃ ca samavāpnuhi duryodhana uvācaa yad āha viduraḥ kṛṣṇe sarvaṃ tat satyam ucyatec anurakto hy asaṃhāryaḥ pārthān prati janārdanaḥa yat tu satkārasaṃyuktaṃ deyaṃ vasu janārdanec anekarūpaṃ rājendra na tad deyaṃ kadā canaa deśaḥ kālas tathāyukto na hi nārhati keśavaḥc maṃsyaty adhokṣajo rājan bhayād arcati mām itia avamānaś ca yatra syāt kṣatriyasya viśāṃ patec na tat kuryād budhaḥ kāryam iti me niścitā matiḥa sa hi pūjyatamo devaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ kamalalocanaḥc trayāṇām api lokānāṃ viditaṃ mama sarvathāa na tu tasmin pradeyaṃ syāt tathā kāryagatiḥ prabhoc vigrahaḥ samupārabdho na hi śāmyaty avigrahāt vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā bhīṣmaḥ kurupitāmahaḥc vaicitravīryaṃ rājānam idaṃ vacanam abravīta satkṛto satkṛto vāpi na krudhyeta janārdanaḥc nālam anyam avajñātum avajñāto pi keśavaḥa yat tu kāryaṃ mahābāho manasā kāryatāṃ gatamc sarvopāyair na tac chakyaṃ kena cit kartum anyathāa sa yad brūyān mahābāhus tat kāryam aviśaṅkayāc vāsudevena tīrthena kṣipraṃ saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥa dharmyam arthyaṃ sa dharmātmā dhruvaṃ vaktā janārdanaḥc tasmin vācyāḥ priyā vāco bhavatā bāndhavaiḥ saha duryodhana uvācaa na paryāyo sti yad rājañ śriyaṃ niṣkevalām ahamc taiḥ sahemām upāśnīyāṃ jīvañ jīvaiḥ pitāmahaa idaṃ tu sumahat kāryaṃ śṛṇu me yat samarthitamb na bhedasyāntaraṃ dātuṃ prayāṇāyāsya vā punaḥc parāyaṇaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ niyaṃsyāmi janārdanama tasmin baddhe bhaviṣyanti vṛṣṇayaḥ pṛthivī tathāc pāṇḍavāś ca vidheyā me sa ca prātar iheṣyatia atropāyaṃ yathā samyaṅ na budhyeta janārdanaḥc na cāpāyo bhavet kaś cit tad bhavān prabravītu me vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā ghoraṃ kṛṣṇābhisaṃhitamc dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ sahāmātyo vyathito vimanābhavata tato duryodhanam idaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro bravīd vacaḥc maivaṃ vocaḥ prajāpāla naiṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥa dūtaś ca hi hṛṣīkeśaḥ saṃbandhī ca priyaś ca naḥc apāpaḥ kauraveyeṣu kathaṃ bandhanam arhati bhīṣma uvācaa parīto dhṛtarāṣṭrāyaṃ tava putraḥ sumandadhīḥc vṛṇoty anarthaṃ na tv arthaṃ yācyamānaḥ suhṛdgaṇaiḥa imam utpathi vartantaṃ pāpaṃ pāpānubandhinamc vākyāni suhṛdāṃ hitvā tvam apy asyānuvartasea kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakarmāṇam āsādyāyaṃ sudurmatiḥc tava putraḥ sahāmātyaḥ kṣaṇena na bhaviṣyatia pāpasyāsya nṛśaṃsasya tyaktadharmasya durmateḥc notsahe narthasaṃyuktāṃ vācaṃ śrotuṃ kathaṃ cana vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa ity uktvā bharataśreṣṭho vṛddhaḥ paramamanyumānc utthāya tasmāt prātiṣṭhad bhīṣmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa prātar utthāya kṛṣṇas tu kṛtavān sarvam āhnikamc brāhmaṇair abhyanujñātaḥ prayayau nagaraṃ pratia taṃ prayāntaṃ mahābāhum anujñāpya tato nṛpac paryavartanta te sarve vṛkasthalanivāsinaḥd prayayau puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ kurūṇāṃ sadanaṃ pratid ācakramuś ca panthānaṃ grasamānā ivāmbaramd dārukeṇa pracoditā hayās tasya mahātmanaḥd annāni śayyā vāsāṃsi tathā ratnāni sarvaśaḥd duryodhanena kṛṣṇārthaṃ pathi saṃvihitaṃ bahud tāḥ sabhāḥ puṇḍarīkākṣo ratnāni ca mahāyaśāḥd nābhyanandan mahābāhur upāyāt kurusaṃsadama dhārtarāṣṭrās tam āyāntaṃ pratyujjagmuḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥc duryodhanam ṛte sarve bhīṣmadroṇakṛpādayaḥa paurāś ca bahulā rājan hṛṣīkeśaṃ didṛkṣavaḥc yānair bahuvidhair anye padbhir eva tathāparea sa vai pathi samāgamya bhīṣmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇāc droṇena dhārtarāṣṭraiś ca tair vṛto nagaraṃ yayaua kṛṣṇasaṃmānanārthaṃ ca nagaraṃ samalaṃkṛtamc babhūvū rājamārgāś ca bahuratnasamācitāḥa na sma kaś cid gṛhe rājaṃs tad āsīd bharatarṣabhac na strī na vṛddho na śiśur vāsudevadidṛkṣayāa rājamārge narā na sma saṃbhavanty avaniṃ gatāḥc tathā hi sumahad rājan hṛṣīkeśapraveśanea āvṛtāni varastrībhir gṛhāṇi sumahānty apic pracalantīva bhāreṇa dṛśyante sma mahītalea tathā ca gatimantas te vāsudevasya vājinaḥc pranaṣṭagatayo bhūvan rājamārge narair vṛtea sa gṛhaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya prāviśac chatrukarśanaḥc pāṇḍuraṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ prāsādair upaśobhitama tisraḥ kakṣyā vyatikramya keśavo rājaveśmanaḥc vaicitravīryaṃ rājānam abhyagacchad ariṃdamaḥa abhyāgacchati dāśārhe prajñācakṣur nareśvaraḥc sahaiva droṇabhīṣmābhyām udatiṣṭhan mahāyaśāḥa kṛpaś ca somadattaś ca mahārājaś ca bāhlikaḥc āsanebhyo calan sarve pūjayanto janārdanama tato rājānam āsādya dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ yaśasvinamc sa bhīṣmaṃ pūjayām āsa vārṣṇeyo vāgbhir añjasād te svadharmān akurvanta saṃpūjya madhusūdanama teṣu dharmānupūrvīṃ tāṃ prayujya madhusūdanaḥc yathāvayaḥ samīyāya rājabhis tatra mādhavaḥa atha droṇaṃ saputraṃ sa bāhlīkaṃ ca yaśasvinamc kṛpaṃ ca somadattaṃ ca samīyāya janārdanaḥa tatrāsīd ūrjitaṃ mṛṣṭaṃ kāñcanaṃ mahad āsanamc śāsanād dhṛtarāṣṭrasya tatropāviśad acyutaḥa atha gāṃ madhuparkaṃ cāpy udakaṃ ca janārdanec upajahrur yathānyāyaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrapurohitāḥa kṛtātithyas tu govindaḥ sarvān parihasan kurūnc āste saṃbandhakaṃ kurvan kurubhiḥ parivāritaḥa so rcito dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa pūjitaś ca mahāyaśāḥc rājānaṃ samanujñāpya nirākrāmad ariṃdamaḥa taiḥ sametya yathānyāyaṃ kurubhiḥ kurusaṃsadic vidurāvasathaṃ ramyam upātiṣṭhata mādhavaḥa viduraḥ sarvakalyāṇair abhigamya janārdanamc arcayām āsa dāśārhaṃ sarvakāmair upasthitamd yā prītiḥ puṇḍarīkākṣa tavāgamanakāraṇāta kṛtātithyaṃ tu govindaṃ viduraḥ sarvadharmavitc kuśalaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇām apṛcchan madhusūdanama prīyamāṇasya suhṛdo viduṣo buddhisattamaḥc dharmanityasya ca tadā gatadoṣasya dhīmataḥa tasya sarvaṃ savistāraṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ viceṣṭitamc kṣattur ācaṣṭa dāśārhaḥ sarvapratyakṣadarśivān vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa athopagamya viduram aparāhṇe janārdanaḥc pitṛṣvasāraṃ govindaḥ so bhyagacchad ariṃdamaḥa sā dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam āyāntaṃ prasannādityavarcasamc kaṇṭhe gṛhītvā prākrośat pṛthā pārthān anusmarana teṣāṃ sattvavatāṃ madhye govindaṃ sahacāriṇamc cirasya dṛṣṭvā vārṣṇeyaṃ bāṣpam āhārayat pṛthāa sābravīt kṛṣṇam āsīnaṃ kṛtātithyaṃ yudhāṃ patimc bāṣpagadgadapūrṇena mukhena pariśuṣyatāa ye te bālyāt prabhṛtyeva guruśuśrūṣaṇe ratāḥc parasparasya suhṛdaḥ saṃmatāḥ samacetasaḥa nikṛtyā bhraṃśitā rājyāj janārhā nirjanaṃ gatāḥc vinītakrodhaharṣāś ca brahmaṇyāḥ satyavādinaḥa tyaktvā priyasukhe pārthā rudantīm apahāya māmc ahārṣuś ca vanaṃ yāntaḥ samūlaṃ hṛdayaṃ mamaa atadarhā mahātmānaḥ kathaṃ keśava pāṇḍavāḥc ūṣur mahāvane tāta siṃhavyāghragajākulea bālā vihīnāḥ pitrā te mayā satatalālitāḥc apaśyantaḥ svapitarau katham ūṣur mahāvanea śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣair mṛdaṅgair vaiṇavair apic pāṇḍavāḥ samabodhyanta bālyāt prabhṛti keśavaa ye sma vāraṇaśabdena hayānāṃ heṣitena cac rathanemininādaiś ca vyabodhyanta sadā gṛhea śaṅkhabherīninādena veṇuvīṇānunādināc puṇyāhaghoṣamiśreṇa pūjyamānā dvijātibhiḥa vastrai ratnair alaṃkāraiḥ pūjayanto dvijanmanaḥc gīrbhir maṅgalayuktābhir brāhmaṇānāṃ mahātmanāma arcitair arcanārhaiś ca stuvadbhir abhinanditāḥc prāsādāgreṣv abodhyanta rāṅkavājinaśāyinaḥa te nūnaṃ ninadaṃ śrutvā śvāpadānāṃ mahāvanec na smopayānti nidrāṃ vai atadarhā janārdanaa bherīmṛdaṅganinadaiḥ śaṅkhavaiṇavanisvanaiḥc strīṇāṃ gītaninādaiś ca madhurair madhusūdanaa bandimāgadhasūtaiś ca stuvadbhir bodhitāḥ kathamc mahāvane vyabodhyanta śvāpadānāṃ rutena tea hrīmān satyadhṛtir dānto bhūtānām anukampitāc kāmadveṣau vaśe kṛtvā satāṃ vartmānuvartatea ambarīṣasya māndhātur yayāter nahuṣasya cac bharatasya dilīpasya śiber auśīnarasya caa rājarṣīṇāṃ purāṇānāṃ dhuraṃ dhatte durudvahāmc śīlavṛttopasaṃpanno dharmajñaḥ satyasaṃgaraḥa rājā sarvaguṇopetas trailokyasyāpi yo bhavetc ajātaśatrur dharmātmā śuddhajāmbūnadaprabhaḥa śreṣṭhaḥ kuruṣu sarveṣu dharmataḥ śrutavṛttataḥc priyadarśano dīrghabhujaḥ kathaṃ kṛṣṇa yudhiṣṭhiraḥa yaḥ sa nāgāyutaprāṇo vātaraṃhā vṛkodaraḥc amarṣī pāṇḍavo nityaṃ priyo bhrātuḥ priyaṃkaraḥa kīcakasya ca sajñāter yo hantā madhusūdanac śūraḥ krodhavaśānāṃ ca hiḍimbasya bakasya caa parākrame śakrasamo vāyuvegasamo javec maheśvarasamaḥ krodhe bhīmaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥa krodhaṃ balam amarṣaṃ ca yo nidhāya paraṃtapaḥc jitātmā pāṇḍavo marṣī bhrātus tiṣṭhati śāsanea tejorāśiṃ mahātmānaṃ balaugham amitaujasamc bhīmaṃ pradarśanenāpi bhīmasenaṃ janārdanae taṃ mamācakṣva vārṣṇeya katham adya vṛkodaraḥa āste parighabāhuḥ sa madhyamaḥ pāṇḍavo cyutac arjunenārjuno yaḥ sa kṛṣṇa bāhusahasriṇāe dvibāhuḥ spardhate nityam atītenāpi keśavaa kṣipaty ekena vegena pañca bāṇaśatāni yaḥc iṣvastre sadṛśo rājñaḥ kārtavīryasya pāṇḍavaḥa tejasādityasadṛśo maharṣipratimo damec kṣamayā pṛthivītulyo mahendrasamavikramaḥa ādhirājyaṃ mahad dīptaṃ prathitaṃ madhusūdanac āhṛtaṃ yena vīryeṇa kurūṇāṃ sarvarājasua yasya bāhubalaṃ ghoraṃ kauravāḥ paryupāsatec sa sarvarathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ satyavikramaḥd yaṃ gatvābhimukhaḥ saṃkhye na jīvan kaś cid āvrajetd yo jetā sarvabhūtānām ajeyo jiṣṇur acyutaa yo pāśrayaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ devānām iva vāsavaḥc sa te bhrātā sakhā caiva katham adya dhanaṃjayaḥa dayāvān sarvabhūteṣu hrīniṣedho mahāstravitc mṛduś ca sukumāraś ca dhārmikaś ca priyaś ca mea sahadevo maheṣvāsaḥ śūraḥ samitiśobhanaḥc bhrātṝṇāṃ kṛṣṇa śuśrūṣur dharmārthakuśalo yuvāa sadaiva sahadevasya bhrātaro madhusūdanac vṛttaṃ kalyāṇavṛttasya pūjayanti mahātmanaḥa jyeṣṭhāpacāyinaṃ vīraṃ sahadevaṃ yudhāṃ patimc śuśrūṣuṃ mama vārṣṇeya mādrīputraṃ pracakṣva mea sukumāro yuvā śūro darśanīyaś ca pāṇḍavaḥc bhrātṝṇāṃ kṛṣṇa sarveṣāṃ priyaḥ prāṇo bahiścaraḥa citrayodhī ca nakulo maheṣvāso mahābalaḥc kaccit sa kuśalī kṛṣṇa vatso mama sukhaidhitaḥa sukhocitam aduḥkhārhaṃ sukumāraṃ mahārathamc api jātu mahābāho paśyeyaṃ nakulaṃ punaḥa pakṣmasaṃpātaje kāle nakulena vinākṛtāc na labhāmi sukhaṃ vīra sādya jīvāmi paśya māma sarvaiḥ putraiḥ priyatamā draupadī me janārdanac kulīnā śīlasaṃpannā sarvaiḥ samuditā guṇaiḥd putrī drupadarājasya vikhyātā satyavādinīa putralokāt patilokān vṛṇvānā satyavādinīc priyān putrān parityajya pāṇḍavān anvapadyataa mahābhijanasaṃpannā sarvakāmaiḥ supūjitāc īśvarī sarvakalyāṇī draupadī katham acyutaa patibhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śūrair agnikalpaiḥ prahāribhiḥc upapannā maheṣvāsair draupadī duḥkhabhāginīa caturdaśam imaṃ varṣaṃ yan nāpaśyam ariṃdamac putrādhibhiḥ paridyūnāṃ draupadīṃ satyavādinīma na nūnaṃ karmabhiḥ puṇyair aśnute puruṣaḥ sukhamc draupadī cet tathāvṛttā nāśnute sukham avyayama na priyo mama kṛṣṇāya bībhatsur na yudhiṣṭhiraḥc bhīmaseno yamau vāpi yad apaśyaṃ sabhāgatāma na me duḥkhataraṃ kiṃ cid bhūtapūrvaṃ tato dhikamc yad draupadīṃ nivātasthāṃ śvaśurāṇāṃ samīpagāma ānāyitām anāryeṇa krodhalobhānuvartināc sarve praikṣanta kurava ekavastrāṃ sabhāgatāma tatraiva dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca mahārājaś ca bāhlikaḥc kṛpaś ca somadattaś ca nirviṇṇāḥ kuravas tathāa tasyāṃ saṃsadi sarvasyāṃ kṣattāraṃ pūjayāmy ahamc vṛttena hi bhavaty āryo na dhanena na vidyayāa tasya kṛṣṇa mahābuddher gambhīrasya mahātmanaḥc kṣattuḥ śīlam alaṃkāro lokān viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhatia sā śokārtā ca hṛṣṭā ca dṛṣṭvā govindam āgatamc nānāvidhāni duḥkhāni sarvāṇy evānvakīrtayatd janmaprabhṛti saṃprāptaṃ duḥkhaṃ nānāvidhaṃ bahud aśrupūrṇamukhī khinnā sarvaṃ caivānvacintayata pūrvair ācaritaṃ yat tat kurājabhir ariṃdamac akṣadyūtaṃ mṛgavadhaḥ kaccid eṣāṃ sukhāvahamd tan naḥ kleśatamaṃ me syāt putraiḥ saha paraṃtapaa tan māṃ dahati yat kṛṣṇā sabhāyāṃ kurusaṃnidhauc dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ parikliṣṭā yathā nakuśalaṃ tathāa nirvāsanaṃ ca nagarāt pravrajyā ca paraṃtapac nānāvidhānāṃ duḥkhānām āvāso smi janārdanae ajñātacaryā bālānām avarodhaś ca keśavaa na sma kleśatamaṃ me syāt putraiḥ saha paraṃtapac duryodhanena nikṛtā varṣam adya caturdaśama duḥkhād api sukhaṃ na syād yadi puṇyaphalakṣayaḥc na me viśeṣo jātv āsīd dhārtarāṣṭreṣu pāṇḍavaiḥa tena satyena kṛṣṇa tvāṃ hatāmitraṃ śriyā vṛtamc asmād vimuktaṃ saṃgrāmāt paśyeyaṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahae naiva śakyāḥ parājetuṃ sattvaṃ hy eṣāṃ tathāgatama pitaraṃ tv eva garheyaṃ nātmānaṃ na suyodhanamc yenāhaṃ kuntibhojāya dhanaṃ dhūrtair ivārpitāa bālāṃ mām āryakas tubhyaṃ krīḍantīṃ kanduhastakāmc adadāt kuntibhojāya sakhā sakhye mahātmanea sāhaṃ pitrā ca nikṛtā śvaśuraiś ca paraṃtapac atyantaduḥkhitā kṛṣṇa kiṃ jīvitaphalaṃ mamaa yan mā vāg abravīn naktaṃ sūtake savyasācinaḥc putras te pṛthivīṃ jetā yaśaś cāsya divaṃ spṛśeta hatvā kurūn grāmajanye rājyaṃ prāpya dhanaṃjayaḥc bhrātṛbhiḥ saha kaunteyas trīn medhān āhariṣyatia nāhaṃ tām abhyasūyāmi namo dharmāya vedhasec kṛṣṇāya mahate nityaṃ dharmo dhārayati prajāḥa dharmaś ced asti vārṣṇeya tathā satyaṃ bhaviṣyatic tvaṃ cāpi tat tathā kṛṣṇa sarvaṃ saṃpādayiṣyasia na māṃ mādhava vaidhavyaṃ nārthanāśo na vairitāc tathā śokāya bhavati yathā putrair vinābhavaḥa yāhaṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varamc dhanaṃjayaṃ na paśyāmi kā śāntir hṛdayasya mea idaṃ caturdaśaṃ varṣaṃ yan nāpaśyaṃ yudhiṣṭhiramc dhanaṃjayaṃ ca govinda yamau taṃ ca vṛkodarama jīvanāśaṃ pranaṣṭānāṃ śrāddhaṃ kurvanti mānavāḥc arthatas te mama mṛtās teṣāṃ cāhaṃ janārdanaa brūyā mādhava rājānaṃ dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiramc bhūyāṃs te hīyate dharmo mā putraka vṛthā kṛthāḥa parāśrayā vāsudeva yā jīvāmi dhig astu māmc vṛtteḥ kṛpaṇalabdhāyā apratiṣṭhaiva jyāyasīa atho dhanaṃjayaṃ brūyā nityodyuktaṃ vṛkodaramc yadarthaṃ kṣatriyā sūte tasya kālo yam āgataḥa asmiṃś ced āgate kāle kālo vo tikramiṣyatic lokasaṃbhāvitāḥ santaḥ sunṛśaṃsaṃ kariṣyathaa nṛśaṃsena ca vo yuktāṃs tyajeyaṃ śāśvatīḥ samāḥc kāle hi samanuprāpte tyaktavyam api jīvitama mādrīputrau ca vaktavyau kṣatradharmaratau sadāc vikrameṇārjitān bhogān vṛṇītaṃ jīvitād apia vikramādhigatā hy arthāḥ kṣatradharmeṇa jīvataḥc mano manuṣyasya sadā prīṇanti puruṣottamaa gatvā brūhi mahābāho sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varamc arjunaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ vīraṃ draupadyāḥ padavīṃ caraa viditau hi tavātyantaṃ kruddhāv iva yathāntakauc bhīmārjunau nayetāṃ hi devān api parāṃ gatima tayoś caitad avajñānaṃ yat sā kṛṣṇā sabhāṃ gatāc duḥśāsanaś ca karṇaś ca paruṣāṇy abhyabhāṣatāma duryodhano bhīmasenam abhyagacchan manasvinamc paśyatāṃ kurumukhyānāṃ tasya drakṣyati yat phalama na hi vairaṃ samāsādya praśāmyati vṛkodaraḥc sucirād api bhīmasya na hi vairaṃ praśāmyatie yāvadantaṃ na nayati śātravāñ śatrukarśanaḥf tāvad eva mahābāhur niśāsu na sukhaṃ labheta na duḥkhaṃ rājyaharaṇaṃ na ca dyūte parājayaḥc pravrājanaṃ ca putrāṇāṃ na me tad duḥkhakāraṇamd paśyatāṃ kuruputrāṇāṃ na me tad duḥkhakāraṇama yat tu sā bṛhatī śyāmā ekavastrā sabhāṃ gatāc aśṛṇot paruṣā vācas tato duḥkhataraṃ nu kima strīdharmiṇī varārohā kṣatradharmaratā sadāc nādhyagacchat tathā nāthaṃ kṛṣṇā nāthavatī satīd sa tv asyā devaputrāyās tvaṃ nātho madhusūdanaa yasyā mama saputrāyās tvaṃ nātho madhusūdanac rāmaś ca balināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pradyumnaś ca mahārathaḥa sāham evaṃvidhaṃ duḥkhaṃ sahe dya puruṣottamac bhīme jīvati durdharṣe vijaye cāpalāyinia tata āśvāsayām āsa putrādhibhir abhiplutāmc pitṛṣvasāraṃ śocantīṃ śauriḥ pārthasakhaḥ pṛthāma kā nu sīmantinī tvādṛg lokeṣv asti pitṛṣvasaḥc śūrasya rājño duhitā ājamīḍhakulaṃ gatāa mahākulīnā bhavatī hradād dhradam ivāgatāc īśvarī sarvakalyāṇī bhartrā paramapūjitāa vīrasūr vīrapatnī ca sarvaiḥ samuditā guṇaiḥc sukhaduḥkhe mahāprājñe tvādṛśī soḍhum arhatia nidrātandrī krodhaharṣau kṣutpipāse himātapauc etāni pārthā nirjitya nityaṃ vīrāḥ sukhe ratāḥa tyaktagrāmyasukhāḥ pārthā nityaṃ vīrasukhapriyāḥc na te svalpena tuṣyeyur mahotsāhā mahābalāḥa antaṃ dhīrā niṣevante madhyaṃ grāmyasukhapriyāḥc uttamāṃś ca parikleśān bhogāṃś cātīva mānuṣāna anteṣu remire dhīrā na te madhyeṣu remirec antaprāptiṃ sukhām āhur duḥkham antaram antayoḥa abhivādayanti bhavatīṃ pāṇḍavāḥ saha kṛṣṇayāc ātmānaṃ ca kuśalinaṃ nivedyāhur anāmayama arogān sarvasiddhārthān kṣipraṃ drakṣyasi pāṇḍavānc īśvarān sarvalokasya hatāmitrāñ śriyā vṛtāna evam āśvāsitā kuntī pratyuvāca janārdanamc putrādhibhir abhidhvastā nigṛhyābuddhijaṃ tamaḥa yad yat teṣāṃ mahābāho pathyaṃ syān madhusūdanac yathā yathā tvaṃ manyethāḥ kuryāḥ kṛṣṇa tathā tathāa avilopena dharmasya anikṛtyā paraṃtapac prabhāvajñāsmi te kṛṣṇa satyasyābhijanasya caa vyavasthāyāṃ ca mitreṣu buddhivikramayos tathāc tvam eva naḥ kule dharmas tvaṃ satyaṃ tvaṃ tapo mahata tvaṃ trātā tvaṃ mahad brahma tvayi sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitamc yathaivāttha tathaivaitat tvayi satyaṃ bhaviṣyatid kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca lokānāṃ cāparājitad sarvasyaitasya vārṣṇeya gatis tvam asi mādhavad prabhāvaṃ buddhivīryaṃ ca tādṛśaṃ tava keśavaa tām āmantrya ca govindaḥ kṛtvā cābhipradakṣiṇamc prātiṣṭhata mahābāhur duryodhanagṛhān prati vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa pṛthām āmantrya govindaḥ kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇamc duryodhanagṛhaṃ śaurir abhyagacchad ariṃdamaḥa lakṣmyā paramayā yuktaṃ puraṃdaragṛhopamamb vicitrair āsanair yuktaṃ praviveśa janārdanaḥc tasya kakṣyā vyatikramya tisro dvāḥsthair avāritaḥa tato bhraghanasaṃkāśaṃ girikūṭam ivocchritamc śriyā jvalantaṃ prāsādam āruroha mahāyaśāḥa tatra rājasahasraiś ca kurubhiś cābhisaṃvṛtamc dhārtarāṣṭraṃ mahābāhuṃ dadarśāsīnam āsanea duḥśāsanaṃ ca karṇaṃ ca śakuniṃ cāpi saubalamc duryodhanasamīpe tān āsanasthān dadarśa saḥa abhyāgacchati dāśārhe dhārtarāṣṭro mahāyaśāḥc udatiṣṭhat sahāmātyaḥ pūjayan madhusūdanama sametya dhārtarāṣṭreṇa sahāmātyena keśavaḥc rājabhis tatra vārṣṇeyaḥ samāgacchad yathāvayaḥa tatra jāmbūnadamayaṃ paryaṅkaṃ supariṣkṛtamc vividhāstaraṇāstīrṇam abhyupāviśad acyutaḥa tasmin gāṃ madhuparkaṃ ca upahṛtya janārdanec nivedayām āsa tadā gṛhān rājyaṃ ca kauravaḥd āsanaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ sarvaratnavibhūṣitamd kṛṣṇārtham eva saṃsiddhaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāta tatra govindam āsīnaṃ prasannādityavarcasamc upāsāṃ cakrire sarve kuravo rājabhiḥ sahaa tato duryodhano rājā vārṣṇeyaṃ jayatāṃ varamc nyamantrayad bhojanena nābhyanandac ca keśavaḥc   nābhyanandaj janārdanaḥc punaḥ punaḥ kauraveyo bhojanena nyamantrayatc asakṛt prārthyamāno pia tato duryodhanaḥ kṛṣṇam abravīd rājasaṃsadic mṛdupūrvaṃ śaṭhodarkaṃ karṇam ābhāṣya kauravaḥa kasmād annāni pānāni vāsāṃsi śayanāni cac tvadartham upanītāni nāgrahīs tvaṃ janārdanaa ubhayoś cādadaḥ sāhyam ubhayoś ca hite rataḥc saṃbandhī dayitaś cāsi dhṛtarāṣṭrasya mādhavaa tvaṃ hi govinda dharmārthau vettha tattvena sarvaśaḥc tatra kāraṇam icchāmi śrotuṃ cakragadādharaa sa evam ukto govindaḥ pratyuvāca mahāmanāḥc oghameghasvanaḥ kāle pragṛhya vipulaṃ bhujama anambūkṛtam agrastam anirastam asaṃkulamc rājīvanetro rājānaṃ hetumadvākyam uttamama kṛtārthā bhuñjate dūtāḥ pūjāṃ gṛhṇanti caiva hic kṛtārthaṃ māṃ sahāmātyas tvam arciṣyasi bhārataa evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca dhārtarāṣṭro janārdanamc na yuktaṃ bhavatāsmāsu pratipattum asāṃpratama kṛtārthaṃ cākṛtārthaṃ ca tvāṃ vayaṃ madhusūdanac yatāmahe pūjayituṃ govinda na ca śaknumaḥa na ca tat kāraṇaṃ vidmo yasmin no madhusūdanac pūjāṃ kṛtāṃ prīyamāṇair nāmaṃsthāḥ puruṣottamaa vairaṃ no nāsti bhavatā govinda na ca vigrahaḥc sa bhavān prasamīkṣyaitan nedṛśaṃ vaktum arhatia evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca dhārtarāṣṭraṃ janārdanaḥc abhivīkṣya sahāmātyaṃ dāśārhaḥ prahasann ivaa nāhaṃ kāmān na saṃrambhān na dveṣān nārthakāraṇātc na hetuvādāl lobhād vā dharmaṃ jahyāṃ kathaṃ canad pūjāṃ kṛtāṃ prīyamāṇo ko vidvāṃs tyaktum arhatia saṃprītibhojyāny annāni āpadbhojyāni vā punaḥc na ca saṃprīyase rājan na cāpy āpadgatā vayama akasmād dviṣase rājañ janmaprabhṛti pāṇḍavānc priyānuvartino bhrātṝn sarvaiḥ samuditān guṇaiḥa akasmāc caiva pārthānāṃ dveṣaṇaṃ nopapadyatec dharme sthitāḥ pāṇḍaveyāḥ kas tān kiṃ vaktum arhatia yas tān dveṣṭi sa māṃ dveṣṭi yas tān anu sa mām anuc aikātmyaṃ māṃ gataṃ viddhi pāṇḍavair dharmacāribhiḥa kāmakrodhānuvartī hi yo mohād virurutsatec guṇavantaṃ ca yo dveṣṭi tam āhuḥ puruṣādhamama yaḥ kalyāṇaguṇāñ jñātīn mohāl lobhād didṛkṣatec so jitātmājitakrodho na ciraṃ tiṣṭhati śriyama atha yo guṇasaṃpannān hṛdayasyāpriyān apic priyeṇa kurute vaśyāṃś ciraṃ yaśasi tiṣṭhatid dviṣadannaṃ na bhoktavyaṃ dviṣantaṃ naiva bhojayetd pāṇḍavān dviṣase rājan mama prāṇā hi pāṇḍavāḥa sarvam etad abhoktavyam annaṃ duṣṭābhisaṃhitamc kṣattur ekasya bhoktavyam iti me dhīyate matiḥa evam uktvā mahābāhur duryodhanam amarṣaṇamc niścakrāma tataḥ śubhrād dhārtarāṣṭraniveśanāta niryāya ca mahābāhur vāsudevo mahāmanāḥc niveśāya yayau veśma vidurasya mahātmanaḥa tam abhyagacchad droṇaś ca kṛpo bhīṣmo tha bāhlikaḥc kuravaś ca mahābāhuṃ vidurasya gṛhe sthitama te bhigamyābruvaṃs tatra kuravo madhusūdanamc nivedayāmo vārṣṇeya saratnāṃs te gṛhānvayama tān uvāca mahātejāḥ kauravān madhusūdanaḥc sarve bhavanto gacchantu sarvā me pacitiḥ kṛtād na nītir asmat pūjā vo bhavatāṃ kurusattamāḥd duryodhanaś ca yuṣmāsu na ca prītiṃ kariṣyatid ta evam uktāḥ kṛṣṇena evam astv iti niryayuḥa yāteṣu kuruṣu kṣattā dāśārham aparājitamc abhyarcayām āsa tadā sarvakāmaiḥ prayatnavāna tataḥ kṣattānnapānāni śucīni guṇavanti cac upāharad anekāni keśavāya mahātmanea tair tarpayitvā prathamaṃ brāhmaṇān madhusūdanaḥc vedavidbhyo dadau kṛṣṇaḥ paramadraviṇāny apid bhuktavatsu dvijendreṣu niṣaṇṇasya varāsaned śuciḥ suprayato bhūtvā viduro nnam upāharatd śraddhayā parayā yukta idaṃ vacanam abravītd saṃbhramais tuṣya govinda etan naḥ paramaṃ dhanamd anyathā vā viśeṣeṇa kas tvām arcitum arhatid udārasya tṛṇaṃ vittaṃ śūrasya maraṇaṃ tṛṇamd viraktasya tṛṇaṃ nārī niḥspṛhasya tṛṇaṃ jagatd taṃ bhuktavantaṃ vividhāḥ suśabdāḥ sūtamāgadhāḥd abhituṣṭuvur āsīnaṃ dāśārham aparājitama tato nuyāyibhiḥ sārdhaṃ marudbhir iva vāsavaḥc vidurānnāni bubhuje śucīni guṇavanti ca vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa taṃ bhuktavantam āśvastaṃ niśāyāṃ viduro bravītb mahātmāno yam icchanti tapaḥ kṛtvā tv anekadhāb sa devo sya samāyāto mama locanagocareb tavātithyaṃ jagannātha kiṃ karomy adya keśavab kṛṣṇa uvācab aham asmi mahīpīṭhe nirdhanānāṃ śiromaṇiḥb sādhu sādhu mahāprājña sarvaśāstraviśāradab yas tvaṃ vinayasaṃpanno vayas tvayy eva dṛśyateb tavādya vacasā tuṣye dadāmi kurunandanab vidura uvācab varaṃ vṛṇīṣva dāsye haṃ yat te manasi rocateb acalā keśave bhaktir mānasaṃ tvadgataṃ sadāb dharme cintā kule janma dehi me madhusūdanab mā matiḥ paradravyeṣu paradāreṣu mā matiḥb parāpavādinī jihvā mā bhūd deva kadā canab āsanaṃ sutasaṃkīrṇaṃ viprasaṃkīrṇamandiramb hṛdayaṃ śāstrasaṃkīrṇaṃ dehi me madhusūdanab durbhikṣe cānnadātāhaṃ subhikṣe ca hiraṇyadaḥb āture haṃ bhayatrātā trīṇi kṛṣṇa bhavantu meb satyaṃ śaucaṃ dayā dānaṃ bhaktiś caiva janārdaneb etān varān ahaṃ yāce yadi tuṣṭo si mādhavac nedaṃ samyag vyavasitaṃ keśavāgamanaṃ tavaa arthadharmātigo mūḍhaḥ saṃrambhī ca janārdanac mānaghno mānakāmaś ca vṛddhānāṃ śāsanātigaḥa dharmaśāstrātigo mando durātmā pragrahaṃ gataḥc aneyaḥ śreyasāṃ pāpo dhārtarāṣṭro janārdanaa kāmātmā prājñamānī ca mitradhruk sarvaśaṅkitaḥc akartā cākṛtajñaś ca tyaktadharmaḥ priyānṛtaḥd mūḍhaś cākṛtabuddhiś ca indriyāṇām anīśvaraḥd kāmānusārī kṛtyeṣu sarveṣv akṛtaniścayaḥa etaiś cānyaiś ca bahubhir doṣair eṣa samanvitaḥc tvayocyamānaḥ śreyo pi saṃrambhān na grahīṣyatia senāsamudayaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthivaṃ madhusūdanac kṛtārthaṃ manyate bāla ātmānam avicakṣaṇaḥa ekaḥ karṇaḥ parāñ jetuṃ samartha iti niścitamc dhārtarāṣṭrasya durbuddheḥ sa śamaṃ nopayāsyatia bhīṣme droṇe kṛpe karṇe droṇaputre jayadrathec bhūyasīṃ vartate vṛttiṃ na śame kurute manaḥa niścitaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ sakarṇānāṃ janārdanac bhīṣmadroṇakṛpān pārthā na śaktāḥ prativīkṣituma saṃvic ca dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ sarveṣām eva keśavac śame prayatamānasya tava saubhrātrakāṅkṣiṇaḥa na pāṇḍavānām asmābhiḥ pratideyaṃ yathocitamc iti vyavasitās teṣu vacanaṃ syān nirarthakama yatra sūktaṃ duruktaṃ ca samaṃ syān madhusūdanac na tatra pralapet prājño badhireṣv iva gāyanaḥa avijānatsu mūḍheṣu nirmaryādeṣu mādhavac na tvaṃ vākyaṃ bruvan yuktaś cāṇḍāleṣu dvijo yathāa so yaṃ balastho mūḍhaś ca na kariṣyati te vacaḥc tasmin nirarthakaṃ vākyam uktaṃ saṃpatsyate tavaa teṣāṃ samupaviṣṭānāṃ sarveṣāṃ pāpacetasāmc tava madhyāvataraṇaṃ mama kṛṣṇa na rocatea durbuddhīnām aśiṣṭānāṃ bahūnāṃ pāpacetasāmc pratīpaṃ vacanaṃ madhye tava kṛṣṇa na rocatea anupāsitavṛddhatvāc chriyā mohāc ca darpitaḥc vayodarpād amarṣāc ca na te śreyo grahīṣyatia balaṃ balavad apy asya yadi vakṣyasi mādhavac tvayy asya mahatī śaṅkā na kariṣyati te vacaḥd mānī maurkhyeṇa pārthānāṃ na paśyaty adhikaṃ balama nedam adya yudhā śakyam indreṇāpi sahāmaraiḥc iti vyavasitāḥ sarve dhārtarāṣṭrā janārdanaa teṣv evam upapanneṣu kāmakrodhānuvartiṣuc samartham api te vākyam asamarthaṃ bhaviṣyatia madhye tiṣṭhan hastyanīkasya mandorathāśvayuktasya balasya mūḍhaḥc duryodhano manyate vītamanyuḥkṛtsnā mayeyaṃ pṛthivī jitetia āśaṃsate dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putromahārājyam asapatnaṃ pṛthivyāmc tasmiñ śamaḥ kevalo nopalabhyobaddhaṃ santam āgataṃ manyate rthama paryasteyaṃ pṛthivī kālapakvāduryodhanārthe pāṇḍavān yoddhukāmāḥc samāgatāḥ sarvayodhāḥ pṛthivyāṃrājānaś ca kṣitipālaiḥ sametāḥa sarve caite kṛtavairāḥ purastāttvayā rājāno hṛtasārāś ca kṛṣṇac tavodvegāt saṃśritā dhārtarāṣṭrānsusaṃhatāḥ saha karṇena vīrāḥa tyaktātmānaḥ saha duryodhanenasṛṣṭā yoddhuṃ pāṇḍavān sarvayodhāḥb mṛtyur jayo veti kṛtaikabhāvāḥb kāmātmāno manyuvaśāvinītāḥc teṣāṃ madhye praviśethā yadi tvaṃna tan mataṃ mama dāśārha vīraa teṣāṃ samupaviṣṭānāṃ bahūnāṃ duṣṭacetasāmc kathaṃ madhyaṃ prapadyethāḥ śatrūṇāṃ śatrukarśanaa sarvathā tvaṃ mahābāho devair api durutsahaḥc prabhāvaṃ pauruṣaṃ buddhiṃ jānāmi tava śatruhana yā me prītiḥ pāṇḍaveṣu bhūyaḥ sā tvayi mādhavac premṇā ca bahumānāc ca sauhṛdāc ca bravīmy ahamd yā me prītiḥ puṣkarākṣa tvaddarśanasamudbhavād sā kim ākhyāyate tubhyam antarātmāsi dehinām vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ vidurasya vacaḥ śrutvā praśritaṃ puruṣottamaḥ idaṃ hovāca vacanaṃ bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ bhagavān uvācaa yathā brūyān mahāprājño yathā brūyād vicakṣaṇaḥc yathā vācyas tvadvidhena suhṛdā madvidhaḥ suhṛta dharmārthayuktaṃ tathyaṃ ca yathā tvayy upapadyatec tathā vacanam ukto smi tvayaitat pitṛmātṛvata satyaṃ prāptaṃ ca yuktaṃ cāpy evam eva yathāttha māmc śṛṇuṣvāgamane hetuṃ vidurāvahito bhavaa daurātmyaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya kṣatriyāṇāṃ ca vairitāmc sarvam etad ahaṃ jānan kṣattaḥ prāpto dya kauravāna paryastāṃ pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ sāśvāṃ sarathakuñjarāmc yo mocayen mṛtyupāśāt prāpnuyād dharmam uttamama dharmakāryaṃ yatañ śaktyā na cec chaknoti mānavaḥc prāpto bhavati tat puṇyam atra me nāsti saṃśayaḥa manasā cintayan pāpaṃ karmaṇā nābhirocayanc na prāpnoti phalaṃ tasya evaṃ dharmavido viduḥa so haṃ yatiṣye praśamaṃ kṣattaḥ kartum amāyayāc kurūṇāṃ sṛñjayānāṃ ca saṃgrāme vinaśiṣyatāma seyam āpan mahāghorā kuruṣv eva samutthitāc karṇaduryodhanakṛtā sarve hy ete tadanvayāḥa vyasanaiḥ kliśyamānaṃ hi yo mitraṃ nābhipadyatec anunīya yathāśakti taṃ nṛśaṃsaṃ vidur budhāḥa ā keśagrahaṇān mitram akāryāt saṃnivartayanc avācyaḥ kasya cid bhavati kṛtayatno yathābalama tat samarthaṃ śubhaṃ vākyaṃ dharmārthasahitaṃ hitamc dhārtarāṣṭraḥ sahāmātyo grahītuṃ vidurārhatia hitaṃ hi dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ tathaiva cac pṛthivyāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ ca yatiṣye ham amāyayāa hite prayatamānaṃ māṃ śaṅked duryodhano yadic hṛdayasya ca me prītir ānṛṇyaṃ ca bhaviṣyatia jñātīnāṃ hi mitho bhede yan mitraṃ nābhipadyatec sarvayatnena madhyasthaṃ na tan mitraṃ vidur budhāḥa na māṃ brūyur adharmajñā mūḍhā asuhṛdas tathāc śakto nāvārayat kṛṣṇaḥ saṃrabdhān kurupāṇḍavāna ubhayoḥ sādhayann artham aham āgata ity utac tatra yatnam ahaṃ kṛtvā gaccheyaṃ nṛṣv avācyatāma mama dharmārthayuktaṃ hi śrutvā vākyam anāmayamc na ced ādāsyate bālo diṣṭasya vaśam eṣyatia ahāpayan pāṇḍavārthaṃ yathāvacchamaṃ kurūṇāṃ yadi cācareyamc puṇyaṃ ca me syāc caritaṃ mahārthaṃmucyeraṃś ca kuravo mṛtyupāśāta api vācaṃ bhāṣamāṇasya kāvyāṃdharmārāmām arthavatīm ahiṃsrāmc avekṣeran dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ samarthāṃmāṃ ca prāptaṃ kuravaḥ pūjayeyuḥa na cāpi mama paryāptāḥ sahitāḥ sarvapārthivāḥc kruddhasya pramukhe sthātuṃ siṃhasyevetare mṛgāḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa ity evam uktvā vacanaṃ vṛṣṇīnām ṛṣabhas tadāc śayane sukhasaṃsparśe śiśye yadusukhāvahaḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tathā kathayator eva tayor buddhimatos tadāc śivā nakṣatrasaṃpannā sā vyatīyāya śarvarīa dharmārthakāmayuktāś ca vicitrārthapadākṣarāḥc śṛṇvato vividhā vāco vidurasya mahātmanaḥa kathābhir anurūpābhiḥ kṛṣṇasyāmitatejasaḥc akāmasyeva kṛṣṇasya sā vyatīyāya śarvarīa tatas tu svarasaṃpannā bahavaḥ sūtamāgadhāḥc śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣaiḥ keśavaṃ pratyabodhayand brahmādivasudevāntaṃ vaṃśaṃ samanukīrtayand tuṣṭuvuḥ keśavaṃ tatra bahavaḥ sūtamāgadhāḥa tata utthāya dāśārha ṛṣabhaḥ sarvasātvatāmc sarvam āvaśyakaṃ cakre prātaḥkāryaṃ janārdanaḥa kṛtodakāryajapyaḥ sa hutāgniḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥc tata ādityam udyantam upātiṣṭhata mādhavaḥa atha duryodhanaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥc saṃdhyāṃ tiṣṭhantam abhyetya dāśārham aparājitama ācakṣetāṃ tu kṛṣṇasya dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ sabhāgatamc kurūṃś ca bhīṣmapramukhān rājñaḥ sarvāṃś ca pārthivāna tvām arthayante govinda divi śakram ivāmarāḥc tāv abhyanandad govindaḥ sāmnā paramavalgunād tān abhyanandad govindaḥ sāmnā paramavalgunād te bhyarcya devakīputraṃ divi śakram ivāmarāḥa tato vimala āditye brāhmaṇebhyo janārdanaḥc dadau hiraṇyaṃ vāsāṃsi gāś cāśvāṃś ca paraṃtapaḥa visṛṣṭavantaṃ ratnāni dāśārham aparājitamc tiṣṭhantam upasaṃgamya vavande sārathis tadād tato rathena śubhreṇa mahatā kiṅkiṇīkinād hayottamayujā śīghram upātiṣṭhata dārukaḥd tasmai rathavaro yuktaḥ śuśubhe lokaviśrutaḥd vājibhiḥ sainyasugrīvameghapuṣpabalāhakaiḥd sainyas tu śukapatrābhaḥ sugrīvaḥ kiṃśukaprabhaḥd meghapuṣpo meghavarṇaḥ pāṇḍaras tu balāhakaḥd dakṣiṇaṃ cāvahat sainyaḥ sugrīvaḥ savyato vahatd pṛṣṭhavāhau tayor āstāṃ meghapuṣpabalāhakaud viśvakarmakṛtāpīḍā ratnajālavibhūṣitād āśritā vai rathe tasmin dhvajayaṣṭir aśobhatad vainateyaḥ sthitas tasyāṃ prabhākaram iva spṛśand tasya sattvavataḥ ketau bhujagārir aśobhatad tasya kīrtimatas tena bhāsvareṇa virājatād śuśubhe syandanaśreṣṭhaḥ patagendreṇa ketunād rukmajālaiḥ patākābhiḥ sauvarṇena ca ketunād babhūva sa rathaśreṣṭhaḥ kālasūrya ivoditaḥd pakṣidhvajavitānaiś ca rukmajālakṛtāntaraiḥd daṇḍamārgavibhāgaiś ca sukṛtair viśvakarmaṇād pravālamaṇihemaiś ca muktāvaiḍūryabhūṣaṇaiḥd kiṅkiṇīśatasaṃghaiś ca vālajālakṛtāntaraiḥd kārtasvaramayībhiś ca padminībhir alaṃkṛtaḥd śuśubhe syandanaśreṣṭhas tāpanīyaiś ca pādapaiḥd vyāghrasiṃhavarāhaiś ca govṛṣair mṛgapakṣibhiḥd tārābhir bhāskaraiś cāpi vāraṇaiś ca hiraṇmayaiḥd vajrāṅkuśavimānaiś ca kūbarāvartasaṃdhiṣud samucchritamahānābhiḥ stanayitnumahāsvanaḥa tam upasthitam ājñāya rathaṃ divyaṃ mahāmanāḥc mahābhraghananirghoṣaṃ sarvaratnavibhūṣitama agniṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇāṃś ca janārdanaḥc kaustubhaṃ maṇim āmucya śriyā paramayā jvalana kurubhiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ kṛṣṇo vṛṣṇibhiś cābhirakṣitaḥc ātiṣṭhata rathaṃ śauriḥ sarvayādavanandanaḥa anvāruroha dāśārhaṃ viduraḥ sarvadharmavitc sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ varama tato duryodhanaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥc dvitīyena rathenainam anvayātāṃ paraṃtapama sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmā ca vṛṣṇīnāṃ ca mahārathāḥc pṛṣṭhato nuyayuḥ kṛṣṇaṃ rathair aśvair gajair apia teṣāṃ hemapariṣkārā yuktāḥ paramavājibhiḥc gacchatāṃ ghoṣiṇaś citrāś cāru babhrājire rathāḥa saṃmṛṣṭasaṃsiktarajaḥ pratipede mahāpathamc rājarṣicaritaṃ kāle kṛṣṇo dhīmāñ śriyā jvalana tataḥ prayāte dāśārhe prāvādyantaikapuṣkarāḥc śaṅkhāś ca dadhmire tatra vādyāny anyāni yāni caa pravīrāḥ sarvalokasya yuvānaḥ siṃhavikramāḥc parivārya rathaṃ śaurer agacchanta paraṃtapāḥa tato nye bahusāhasrā vicitrādbhutavāsasaḥc asiprāsāyudhadharāḥ kṛṣṇasyāsan puraḥsarāḥd yodhāḥ paraśuhastāś ca śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa gajāḥ paraḥśatās tatra varāś cāśvāḥ sahasraśaḥc prayāntam anvayur vīraṃ dāśārham aparājitama puraṃ kurūṇāṃ saṃvṛttaṃ draṣṭukāmaṃ janārdanamc savṛddhabālaṃ sastrīkaṃ rathyāgatam ariṃdamama vedikāpāśritābhiś ca samākrāntāny anekaśaḥc pracalantīva bhāreṇa yoṣidbhir bhavanāny utaa saṃpūjyamānaḥ kurubhiḥ saṃśṛṇvan vividhāḥ kathāḥc yathārhaṃ pratisatkurvan prekṣamāṇaḥ śanair yayaua tataḥ sabhāṃ samāsādya keśavasyānuyāyinaḥc saśaṅkhair veṇunirghoṣair diśaḥ sarvā vyanādayana tataḥ sā samitiḥ sarvā rājñām amitatejasāmc saṃprākampata harṣeṇa kṛṣṇāgamanakāṅkṣayāa tato bhyāśagate kṛṣṇe samahṛṣyan narādhipāḥc śrutvā taṃ rathanirghoṣaṃ parjanyaninadopamama āsādya tu sabhādvāram ṛṣabhaḥ sarvasātvatāmc avatīrya rathāc chauriḥ kailāsaśikharopamāta nagameghapratīkāśāṃ jvalantīm iva tejasāc mahendrasadanaprakhyāṃ praviveśa sabhāṃ tataḥa pāṇau gṛhītvā viduraṃ sātyakiṃ ca mahāyaśāḥc jyotīṃṣy ādityavad rājan kurūn pracchādayañ śriyāa agrato vāsudevasya karṇaduryodhanāv ubhauc vṛṣṇayaḥ kṛtavarmā ca āsan kṛṣṇasya pṛṣṭhataḥa dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ puraskṛtya bhīṣmadroṇādayas tataḥc āsanebhyo calan sarve pūjayanto janārdanama abhyāgacchati dāśārhe prajñācakṣur mahāmanāḥc sahaiva bhīṣmadroṇābhyām udatiṣṭhan mahāyaśāḥa uttiṣṭhati mahārāje dhṛtarāṣṭre janeśvarec tāni rājasahasrāṇi samuttasthuḥ samantataḥa āsanaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtamc kṛṣṇārthe kalpitaṃ tatra dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śāsanātd duryodhana uvācad bhīṣmadroṇau parityajya tvayā māṃ madhusūdanad bhagavān uvācad kimarthaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa kṛtaṃ vṛṣalabhojanamd bhaktaṃ pṛcchasi rājendra ādaraṃ kiṃ na pṛcchasid bhojanaṃ gatajīrṇaṃ tu ādaram ajarāmaramd ādareṇopanītāni śākāny api phalāni cad prīṇanti mama gātrāṇi nāmṛtaṃ mānavarjitamd varaṃ hālāhalaṃ prītaṃ sadyaḥ prāṇaharaṃ ca yatd na tu bhuktaṃ dhanāḍhyasya bhruvā kuṭiliteyuṣe sicd na jātiḥ kāraṇaṃ tāta guṇāḥ kalyāṇakāraṇamd cāṇḍālam api sadvṛttaṃ taṃ devā brāhmaṇaṃ viduḥd kaivartīgarbhasaṃbhūto vyāso nāma mahāmuniḥd tapasā brāhmaṇo jātas tasmāj jātir na kāraṇama smayamānas tu rājānaṃ bhīṣmadroṇau ca mādhavaḥc abhyabhāṣata dharmātmā rājñaś cānyān yathāvayaḥa tatra keśavam ānarcuḥ samyag abhyāgataṃ sabhāmc rājānaḥ pārthivāḥ sarve kuravaś ca janārdanama tatra tiṣṭhan sa dāśārho rājamadhye paraṃtapaḥc apaśyad antarikṣasthān ṛṣīn parapuraṃjayaḥa tatas tān abhisaṃprekṣya nāradapramukhān ṛṣīnc abhyabhāṣata dāśārho bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ śanaiḥa pārthivīṃ samitiṃ draṣṭum ṛṣayo bhyāgatā nṛpac nimantryantām āsanaiś ca satkāreṇa ca bhūyasāa naiteṣv anupaviṣṭeṣu śakyaṃ kena cid āsitumc pūjā prayujyatām āśu munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanāma ṛṣīñ śāṃtanavo dṛṣṭvā sabhādvāram upasthitānc tvaramāṇas tato bhṛtyān āsanānīty acodayata āsanāny atha mṛṣṭāni mahānti vipulāni cac maṇikāñcanacitrāṇi samājahrus tatas tataḥa teṣu tatropaviṣṭeṣu gṛhītārgheṣu bhāratac niṣasādāsane kṛṣṇo rājānaś ca yathāsanama duḥśāsanaḥ sātyakaye dadāv āsanam uttamamc viviṃśatir dadau pīṭhaṃ kāñcanaṃ kṛtavarmaṇea avidūre tha kṛṣṇasya karṇaduryodhanāv ubhauc ekāsane mahātmānau niṣīdatur amarṣaṇaua gāndhārarājaḥ śakunir gāndhārair abhirakṣitaḥc niṣasādāsane rājā sahaputro viśāṃ patea viduro maṇipīṭhe tu śuklaspardhyājinottarec saṃspṛśann āsanaṃ śaurer mahāmatir upāviśata cirasya dṛṣṭvā dāśārhaṃ rājānaḥ sarvapārthivāḥc amṛtasyeva nātṛpyan prekṣamāṇā janārdanama atasīpuṣpasaṃkāśaḥ pītavāsā janārdanaḥc vyabhrājata sabhāmadhye hemnīvopahito maṇiḥa tatas tūṣṇīṃ sarvam āsīd govindagatamānasamc na tatra kaś cit kiṃ cid dhi vyājahāra pumān kva cit vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa teṣv āsīneṣu sarveṣu tūṣṇīṃbhūteṣu rājasuc vākyam abhyādade kṛṣṇaḥ sudaṃṣṭro dundubhisvanaḥa jīmūta iva gharmānte sarvāṃ saṃśrāvayan sabhāmc dhṛtarāṣṭram abhiprekṣya samabhāṣata mādhavaḥa kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca śamaḥ syād iti bhāratac aprayatnena vīrāṇām etad yatitum āgataḥa rājan nānyat pravaktavyaṃ tava niḥśreyasaṃ vacaḥc viditaṃ hy eva te sarvaṃ veditavyam ariṃdamaa idam adya kulaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sarvarājasu pārthivab tvan nimittaṃ viśeṣeṇa neha yuktaṃ viśiṣyatec śrutavṛttopasaṃpannaṃ sarvaiḥ samuditaṃ guṇaiḥa kṛpānukampā kāruṇyam ānṛśaṃsyaṃ ca bhāratac tathārjavaṃ kṣamā satyaṃ kuruṣv etad viśiṣyatea tasminn evaṃvidhe rājan kule mahati tiṣṭhatic tvannimittaṃ viśeṣeṇa neha yuktam asāṃpratama tvaṃ hi vārayitā śreṣṭhaḥ kurūṇāṃ kurusattamac mithyā pracaratāṃ tāta bāhyeṣv ābhyantareṣu caa te putrās tava kauravya duryodhanapurogamāḥc dharmārthau pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā pracaranti nṛśaṃsavata aśiṣṭā gatamaryādā lobhena hṛtacetasaḥc bhūmiṃ bhokṣyase ca paraṃtapac yadi saṃpatsyase putraiḥ sahāmātyair narādhipaa saṃyuge vai mahārāja dṛśyate sumahān kṣayaḥc kṣaye cobhayato rājan kaṃ dharmam anupaśyasia pāṇḍavair nihataiḥ saṃkhye
